# 'dir ni 'du byed kyi phung por bsdus pa nyid 'du byed rnams su 'dod de /
rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṅgṛhītānām uktatvādvijñānaskandhasaṅgṛhītānāṃ ca vakṣyamāṇatvāt / ata evavedanāsañjñayoḥ sparśamanaskārādibhiś caitasikatvāviśeṣe 'pyāha vedanāsañjñābhyām anye caitasikā iti
# gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes kyi phung por bsdus pa rnams ni bshad zin la / / rnam par shes pa'i phung por bsdus pa rnams ni 'og nas 'byung ba de'i tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis reg pa dang yid la byed pa la sogs pa rnams dang sems las byung ba nyid du bye brag med kyang / / tshor ba dang 'du shes pa las gzhan pa'i sems las byung ba rnams zhes smos pa ni /
vedanāsañjñayoścaitasikatve saty api vedanāsañjñāskandhasaṅgṛhītatvān nasaṃskāraskandhe 'sti saṅgraha iti pradarśanārtham
# tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis sems las byung ba nyid yin du zin kyang tshor ba dang 'du shes gnyis phung por bsdus pas 'du byed kyi phung por ma bsdus par bstan pa'i phyir ro /
vedanā hyupabhogavastu
# tshor ba ni nye bar spyod pa'i dngos po ste /
tathā hi vedanayā śubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃphalavipākam anubhavati / sañjñā vyavahāravastu
# 'di ltar tshor bas ni las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa myong bar byed / / 'du shes ni tha snyad 'dogs pa'i gzhi ste /
sañjñayāhidṛṣṭaśrutamatavijñāteṣv artheṣu nimittam udgṛhya dṛṣṭādiṣudṛṣṭaśrutamatavijñātā iti lokaḥ saṃvyavahāre pravartata ity atovedanāsañjñe pṛthakskandhīkṛte nānye caitasikā iti
# 'du shes kyis mthong ba dang thos pa dang bye brag phyed pa dang rnam par shes pa'i don rnams la mtshan mar bzung nas mthong ba la sogs pa la mthong ngo / / thos so / / bye brag phyed do / / rnam par shes so zhes 'jig rten pa'i tha snyad pa 'jug ste / / de'i phyir tshor ba dang 'du shes nyid so sor phung por byas kyi / / sems las byung ba gzhan rnams ni ma yin no; /
yadivedanāsañjñābhyām anye sparśādayo vicārāntāś caitasikādharmāś cittaviprayuktāś ca prāptyādayaḥsaṃskāraskandhasaṅgṛhītāḥ evaṃ sati sūtravirodhaḥ
# gal te tshor ba dang 'du shes las gzhan pa reg pa la sogs pa sems las byung ba'i chos spyod pa la thug pa rnams dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa thob pa la sogs pa 'du byed kyi phung por bsdu na / / de lta na 'o na ni mdo dang 'gal te /
uktaṃ hi sūtre saṃskāraskandhaḥ katamaḥ
# mdo las ni 'du byed kyi phung po gang zhe na /
ṣaṭ cetanākāyāiti / nāstivirodhaḥ prādhānyena tannirdeśāt
# sems pa'i tshogs drug go zhes gsungs so zhe na / / de ni gtso bo bstan pa'i phyir 'gal ba med de /
cetanā hicittābhisaṃskaraṇe pradhānaṃanuvartante manaskārādaya iticetanaiva saṃskāraskandhatvenoktā
# sems pa ni sems mngon par 'du byed pa ni gtso bo yin la / / yid la byed pa la sogs pa ni de'i rjes su 'brang ba yin pas sems pa nyid 'du byed kyi phung por gsungs te /
tathā hi kuśale cittaṃprerayaty akuśale 'py avyākṛte 'pi sukhaduḥkhādyavasthāsv api cittaṃ prerayatīti
# 'di ltar gang dge ba la yang sems 'jug par byed / / mi dge ba dang lung ma bstan pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyi gnas rnams la yang sems 'jug par byed pa'i phyir ro /
saṃskāravac caitasikā api dharmā navijñāyanta iti praśnaḥ / ye dharmāś cittena / samprayuktā iti vyākaraṇam
# 'du byed bzhin du sems las byung ba'i chos rnams kyang mi shes pa'i phyir dris pa dang chos gang dag sems dang mtshungs par ldan pa rnams so zhes bya bas bstan to /
te tu na vijñāyanta ity ataḥpṛcchati / vyākaraṇaṃ sparśo manaskāra iti vistaraḥ
# de dag kyang mi shes pas de'i phyir dris pa dang reg pa dang yid la byed pa dang zhes rgya cher smos so /
ete / 'pi sparśādayo vicārāntāḥ pañcabhir āśrayālambanākārakāladravyasamatāprakāraiś cittānuvartanātsamam prayuktā iti samprayuktāḥ
# reg pa la sogs pa dpyod pa la thug pa de dag kyang gnas dang dmigs pa dang rnam pa dang dus dang rdzas mtshungs pa nyid rnam pa lngas sems kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i phyir mtshungs par ldan pas mtshungs par ldan pa rnams so /
cittena samprayuktā ity aviśeṣābhidhānāt sarveṣāṃ sarvacittasamprayogaḥ prasakta ititannirdhāraṇārtham āha eṣāṃpañca sarvatragāḥ / jpañca pratiniyataviṣayāḥ / ekādaśa kuśalāḥ / ṣaṭ kleśāḥ
# sems dang mtshungs par ldan pa bye brag med pa'i phyir thams cad kyang sems thams cad dang mtshungs par ldan par thal bar 'gyur ba de bsal ba'i phyir / / de rnams las lnga ni kun du 'gro ba'o / / lnga ni yul so sor nges pa'o / / bcu gcig ni dge ba'o / / drug ni nyon mongs pa'o /
avaśiṣṭā upakleśāḥ
# lhag ma rnams ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o /
kaukṛtyādyāścatvāro 'nyathāpīti
# 'gyod pa la sogs pa bzhi ni gzhan du yang ngo zhes bya ba smos so /
eṣāṃ ya ādyāḥsparśo manaskāro / vedanā sañjñā cetanāca ete sarvatragāḥ
# 'di dag gi nang nas dang po'i reg pa dang yid la byed pa dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa gang yin pa de dag ni kun du 'gro ba ste /
ete hipañcadharmāḥ sarvaṃ cittam anugacchantīti sarvatragaḥ
# chos lnga po 'di dag ni sems thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro bas kun du 'gro ba'o /
tathā hyetekuśalena traidhātukenānāsraveṇa casamprayujyante / akuśalena kāmāptena kliṣṭāvyākṛtābhyāṃ catraidhātukābhyāṃsamprayujyante / avaśyaṃ hi sarvacittapravṛttiṣutrikasannipātena bhavitavyam trikasannipātaś casparśāvyabhicārīty ataḥ sparśasya sarvatragatvam
# 'di ltar 'di dag ni khams gsum pa'i dge ba dang zag pa med pa'i sems dang yang mtshungs par ldan la / / 'dod par gtogs pa'i mi dge ba dang khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa can dang lung du mi ston pa dang yang mtshungs par ldan no / / sems kyi 'jug pa thams cad la gdon mi za bar gsum 'dus pa 'byung ste / / gsum 'dus pa yang reg pa las 'khrul pa med pas / / de'i phyir reg pa ni kun du 'gro ba nyid do /
nirābhogasya cittasyālambane pravṛttyabhāvān manaskāro 'pisarvatragaḥ
# sems kyi 'jug pa med par dmigs pa la 'jug pa mi srid pas yid la byed pa yang kun du 'gro ba nyid do /
niranubhavasya nimittodgrahaṇanirapekṣasya cacittasyābhāvād vedanāsañjñayor api sarvatragatvam
# myong ba med pa dang mtshan mar 'dzin pa la mi ltos pa'i sems med pas na tshor ba dang 'du shes kyang kun du 'gro ba nyid do /
cetanā tumanaskarmaiveti tayāpy avaśyaṃ sarvatra cetasi bhavitavyamity ata ete pañca dharmāḥ sarvatragāḥ
# sems pa ni yid kyi las nyid yin pas de yang gdon mi za bar sems thams cad la 'byung bas de'i phyir chos lnga po 'di dag ni kun du 'gro ba'o /
pañca pratiniyataviṣayā iti pratiniyato viṣaya eṣāṃ na sarva itipratiniyataviṣayāḥ
# lnga ni yul so sor nges pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'di dag yul so sor nges pa yin gyi thams cad la ma yin pas yul so sor nges pa'o zhes bya ba'o /
te punaśchando 'dhimokṣaḥ smṛtiḥsamādhiḥ prajñā / ekādaśa kuśalāḥ
# de dag kyang 'dun pa dang mos pa dang dran pa dang ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab bo / / bcu gcig ni dge ba ste /
te punaḥ śraddhādayo'vihiṃsāvasānāḥ
# de dag kyang dad pa la sogs pa nas rnam par mi 'tshe ba la thug pa yan chad do /
ete hy āśraddhyādivipakṣatvātkuśalamūlasamprayogāc ca kuśalāḥ / etair eva ca samprayuktaṃ cittaṃ kuśalam
# de dag ni ma dad pa la sogs pa'i gnyen po yin pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir dge ba rnams te / / de dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i sems kyang dge ba'o /
ṣaṭ kleśāḥ rāgaḥ pratighomāno 'vidyā dṛṣṭir vicikitsā ca
# nyon mongs pa drug ni 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang nga rgyal dang ma rig pa dang lta ba dang the tshom ste /
ete hi cittaṃ kliśnantīti kleśāḥ
# de dag ni sems nyon mongs par byed pas nyon mongs pa rnams so /
avaśiṣṭā upakleśāḥ / te punaḥ krodhādyā asamprajanyāntāḥ
# lhag ma rnams ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o zhes bya ba ni de dag kyang khro ba nas shes bzhin ma yin pa la thug pa yan chad do /
kaukṛtyādyāś catvāro 'nyatheti vacanād upakleśā avaśiṣṭā ityaviśeṣābhidhāne 'py asamprajanyāvasānāḥ eveti gamyate
# 'gyod pa la sogs bzhi ni gzhan du yang ngo zhes 'byung ba de'i phyir lhag ma rnams ni nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'o zhes khyad med par brjod kyang shes bzhin ma yin pa'i mthar thug pa kho na yin par mngon no /
kleśāṅgikatvāc cittakleśakaratvāc ca kleśasamīpe vartanta ityupakleśāḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i char gtogs pa dang sems nyon mongs par byed pa dang nyon mongs dang nye ba'i phyir nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams so /
kaukṛtyādyāś catvāra iti kaukṛtyaṃ middhaṃ vitarko vicāraś ca
# 'gyod pa la sogs pa bzhin ni zhes bya ba ni 'gyod pa dang gnyid dang rtog pa dang dpyod pa'o /
anyathāpīti na kevalam ete upakleśā evakiṃ tarhi kuśalā apy avyākṛtā apīti / sa eṣa caitasikānāṃ piṇḍaḥsamāsata ekapañcāśad bhavati / eṣāṃ tu pratyekaṃ svarūpaṃ na prajñāyata iti praśnaḥ sparśaḥ katamaḥ / manaskāraḥ katama ityādi / iha / caitasikānāṃ lakṣaṇata eva nirdeśo na karmato yathānyatrasaṅkṣepasya vivakṣitatvāt
# gzhan du yang ngo zhes bya ba ni 'di dag nye ba'i nyon mongs pa 'ba' zhig yin par ma zad kyi / / dge ba yin pa dang lung du mi ston pa yang yin pa'i phyir ro / / sems las byung ba rnams kyi sdom 'di ni bsdu na lnga bcu rtsa gcig go / / 'di dag gi so so'i rang gi ngo bo mi shes pas / / reg pa gang zhe na / / yid la byed pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa dris so / / 'dir ni mtshan nyid kho na bstan gyi mdor bsdu bar 'dod pas gzhan nas 'byung ba bzhin du las ni ma yin no /
vayaṃ tu karmāpy eṣāṃnirdekṣyāmaḥ sukhāvabodhārtham / tatra pūrvaṃ svarūpameva nirdiṣṭam prāguddiṣṭatvāt / evam anyatrāpiyathāsambhavaṃ vācyam
# bdag gis ni bde blag tu rtogs par bya ba'i phyir ro / / las kyang bshad par bya'o / / de la rang gi ngo bo ni sngar bstan pa'i phyir sngar bshad de / / de bzhin du gzhan yang ji ltar mthun mthun du brjod par bya'o /
trikasamavāyaparicchedaiti prakṛtamndriyaviṣayavijñānāni trīṇy eva trikaṃ / tasyakāryakāraṇabhāvena samavasthānaṃ samavāyaḥ
# gsum 'dus nas yongs su gcod pa'o zhes bya ba ni skabs yin pas dbang po dang yul dang rnam par shes pa gsum nyid gsum mo / / de rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos pos gnas pa ni 'dus pa ste /
tasmin satitatkālam evendriyasya sukhādivedanotpattyanukūlo yo vikāraḥtena sadṛśo viṣayasya sukhādivedanīyākāraparicchedo yaḥ sasparśaḥ / indriyaṃ punar yena viśeṣeṇasukhaduḥkhādihetutvaṃ pratipadyate sa tasya vikāraindriyavikāraḥ
# de yod na de'i dus nyid na bde ba la sogs pa'i tshor pa 'byung ba dang mthun pa dbang po'i 'gyur ba 'di gang yin pa de dang 'dra ba bde ba la sogs pa myong bar 'gyur pa'i yul gyi rnam pa yongs su gcod pa gang yin pa de reg pa'o / / dbang po yang bye brag gang gis bde ba dang sdug bsngal ba la sogs pa'i rgyur gyur pa de ni de'i 'gyur ba ste /
sādṛśyenendriyaṃ spṛśatīndriyeṇa vā spṛśyataiti sparśaḥ
# dbang po 'gyur ba dang 'dra bas dbang po la reg pa'am dbang pos reg pas reg pa'o /
vedanāsanniśrayatvam asya karma
# 'di'i las ni tshor ba'i rten byed pa'o /
evaṃ hy uktaṃsūtre sukhavedanīyaṃ sparśaṃ pratītyotpadyate sukhāvedaneti
# de skad du mdo las kyang bde ba myong bar 'gyur ba'i reg pa la brten nas bde ba'i tshor ba 'byung ngo zhes gsungs so /
manaskāraḥ katamaḥ / u vcetasa ābhogaiti / ābhujanam ābhoga
# yid la byed pa gang zhe na / / sems kyi 'jug pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'jug par byed pas 'jug pa ste /
ālambane yena cittam abhimukhīkriyatesacittasyābhogaḥ
# dmigs pa la gang gis sems mngon du phyogs par byed pa de sems kyi 'jug pa'o /
sa punarālambane cittadhāraṇakarmakaḥ / cittadhāraṇaṃ punas tatraivālambane punaḥ punaścittasyāvarjanaṃ
# de ni dmigs pa la sems 'dzin pa'i las can te / / sems 'dzin pa ni dmigs pa de nyid la yang dang yang gtod pa'o /
etac ca karma cittasantaterālambananiyamena viśiṣṭaṃ manaskāram adhikṛtyoktam na tuyaḥ praticittakṣaṇaṃ
# las de yang sems kyi rgyun gyi dmigs pa nges pas yid la byed pa bye brag can gyi dbang du byas te bshad kyi / / de sems kyi skad cig re re la ni ma yin te /
yad apy atra nidarśanam ucyate samādhilābhī manaskāralābhīty ucyataiti tatraviśiṣṭamanaskāralābhād eva manaskāralābhīty ucyate
# yid la byed pa thob pa ni ting nge 'dzin thob pa'o zhes gang smos pa ni 'dir dper brjod pa ste / / der yang yid la byed pa khyad par can thob pas yid la byed pa thob pa'o zhes brjod do; /
anyathā hi sarvasattvā eva manaskāralābhinaḥ syuḥ sarveṣāṃpraticittakṣaṇaṃ manaskārabhāvāt / cetanā katamā
# gzhan du na ni thams cad kyi sems kyi skad cig re re la yid la byed pa thob pa'i phyir sems can thams cad kyis yid la byed pa thob pa nyid du 'gyur ro / / sems pa gang zhe na /
guṇato doṣato nobhayataś / bcittābhisaṃskāromanaskarmeti guṇataḥ / dkuśaleṣudharmeṣu doṣato'kuśaleṣuanubhayato'vyākṛteṣu / atha vā guṇata ity upakariṣu doṣata ity apakāriṣu anubhayata iti madhyastheṣu / cittābhisaṃskāra iti manaśceṣṭā / yasyāṃsatyām ālambanaṃ prati cetasaḥ praspando bhavatiayaskāntavaśād ayaspraspandavat
# yon tan dang nyes pa dang gnyi ga ma yin pa la sems mngon par 'du byed pa yid kyi las so zhes bya ba la / / yon tan ni dge ba'i chos rnams so / / nyes pa ni mi dge ba rnams so / / gnyi ga ma yin pa ni lung du ma bstan pa rnams so / / yang na yon tan ni phan 'dogs pa rnams so / / nyes pa ni gnod par byed pa rnams so / / gnyi ga ma yin pa ni bar ma do rnams so / / sems mngon par 'du byed pa zhes bya ba ni yid gyo bar byed pa ste / / gang yod na khab len gyi dbang gis lcags gyo ba bzhin du dmigs pa la sems gyo bar byed pa'o /
āha ca kṣaṇāntarānavasthānaṃ nirvyāpāraṃ yayā manaḥ
# skad cig gzhan du mi gnas shing / / byed med yid kyang gang gis ni /
savyāpāram ivākhyāti sā manaskarma cetanāiti
# byed dang bcas ltar snang byed pa / / sems pa de ni yid kyi las /
cittābhisaṃskāra ity ukte manaskarmeti kimartham / sarvaireva caitasikaiś cittam abhisaṃskriyate
# zhes gsungs so / / sems mngon par 'du byed pa zhes de skad ces bstan na / / yid kyi las zhes ci'i phyir bya zhe na /
tebhyovyavacchedārthaṃ manaskarmety āha vijñānasya parispandaiva yo dharmaḥ sa eva cetanā nānya iti jñāpanārtham
# sems las byung ba thams cad kyis kyang sems mngon par 'du byed pas de'i phyir gzhan dag las rnam par dbye ba'i don du yid kyi las zhes bya ba smos so / / rnam par shes pa kun du gyo ba ltar byed pa'i chos gang yin pa de ni sems pa yin gyi / / gzhan ni ma yin no zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir ro /
guṇatodoṣato 'nubhayataś cittābhisaṃskāra iti karmanirdeśaḥ
# yon tan dang nyes pa dang gnyi ga ma yin pa la sems mngon par 'du byed pa zhes bya ba ni las bstan pa'o /
manaskarmeti cetanāyāḥ svarūpanirdeśaḥ
# yid kyi las so zhes bya ba ni sems pa'i rang gi ngo bo bstan to /
chandaḥ katamaḥ / abhiprete vastuny
# 'dun pa gang zhe na / / bsam pa'i dngos po la 'dod pa'o zhes bya ba la /
abhilāṣaity abhipretagrahaṇam anabhipretechandābhāvajñāpanārtham / evaṃ ca cchandasyapratiniyataviṣayatvaṃ jñāpitam bhavati
# bsams pa smos pa ni ma bsams pa la 'dun pa med do zhes shes par bya ba'i phyir te / / de ltar na 'dun pa yul so sor nges pa nyid du bstan pa yin no /
darśanaśravaṇādikriyāviṣayatvena yad abhimataṃ vastu tadabhipretam
# lta ba dang mnyan pa la sogs pa'i bya ba'i yul du gyur pa la bsam pa'i dngos po gang yin pa de ni bsam pa'o /
tatra darśanaśravaṇābhilāṣaḥ prārthanā
# de la lta ba dang mnyan par 'dod pa ni don du gnyer ba'o /
yadyabhilāṣātmakaś chandaḥ tṛṣṇāchandayoḥ kaḥ prativiśeṣaḥ
# gal te 'dun pa 'dod pa'i bdag nyid yin na de'i tshe sred pa dang 'dun pa gnyis bye brag ci yod ce na /
tṛṣṇā abhiṣvaṅgalakṣaṇā
# sred pa ni mngon par chags pa'i mtshan nyid yin la /
chando 'bhilāṣalakṣaṇa ity astiviśeṣaḥ / sa cavīryārambhasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / adhimokṣaḥ katamaḥ / niścite vastuni
# 'dun pa ni 'dod pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas bye brag yod de / / 'di ni brtson 'grus rtsom pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / mos pa gang zhe na /
tathaivāvadhāraṇamiti niścitagrahaṇam / adhimokṣasya sarvaviṣayāsattvaprajñāpanārtham
# nges pa'i dngos po la de bzhin du nges par 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba la nges pa smos pa ni mos pa'i yul yang thams cad ma yin par shes par bya ba'i phyir te /
na hy aniścite vastuni tathaivāvadhāraṇasambhavo 'stīti
# nges pa med pa'i dngos po la de bzhin du nges par 'dzin mi srid do /
yuktitaāptopadeśād vā yad vastu niḥsandigdhaṃ tan niścitam
# rigs pa'am yid ches pa'i lung gi dngos po de la the tshom med pa gang yin pa de nges pa ste /
yenaivākāreṇa tan niścitam anityaduḥkhādyākāreṇa tenaivākāreṇa tadvastunaś cetasi niveśanamevam evaitannānyathety avadhāraṇam adhimokṣaḥ / saāsaṃhāryatākarmakaḥ
# mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa gang gis de rnam par nges pa'i rnam pa de nyid kyis dngos po de la sems 'jog pa ste / / 'di ni de bzhin te /
adhimuktipradhāno hi svasiddhāntātparapravādibhir apahartuṃ na śakyate / smṛtiḥ katamā / saṃstute vastuny / asampramoṣaś cetaso'bhilapanatti saṃstuta ity
# gzhan du ma yin no zhes nges par 'dzin pa ni mos pa'o / / 'di ni mi 'phrogs pa nyid kyi las can te / / mos pa gces su byed pa ni phas kyi rgol ba rnams kyis rang gi grub pa'i mtha' las 'phrog par mi nus so / / dran pa gang zhe na / / 'dris pa'i dngos po ma brjed pa ste / / sems kyi mngon par brjod pa nyid do zhes bya ba la /
asaṃstute smṛtyabhāvapradarśanārtham
# 'dris pa ni ma 'dris pa la dran pa med do zhes bstan pa'i phyir ro /
aṃstutaṃ ca vastupūrvānubhūtam
# 'dris pa'i dngos po ni sngon myong ba'o /
asampramoṣaālambanagrahaṇāvipraṇāśakāraṇam / tat pūrvagṛhītasyavastunaḥ punaḥ punar ālambanākārasmaraṇam abhilapanatā / abhilapanam ivābhilapanamabhilapanam evābhilapanatā
# ma brjed pa ni dmigs pa la 'dzin pa chud mi za bar byed pa'i rgyu ste / / de ni sngon bzung ba'i dngos po la dmigs pa'i rnam pa yang dang yang dran pa'o / / mngon par brjod pa nyid ni mngon par brjod pa dang 'dra bas mngon par brjod pa'o /
sāpunarālambanābhilapane sati na cittasyālambanāntareākārāntare vā vikṣepo bhavatīty ato'vikṣepakarmikā / samādhiḥ katamaḥ / upaparīkṣye vastuni / cittasyaikāgratty upaparīkṣya iti nānyatra
# mngon par brjod pa kho na mngon par brjod pa nyid do / / de ni dmigs pa mngon par brjod pa yod na dmigs pa gzhan nam rnam pa gzhan la sems gyeng ba med pas de'i phyir mi gyeng ba'i las can no / / ting nge 'dzin gang zhe na / / brtag pa'i dngos po la sems rtse gcig pa nyid do zhes bya ba la / / brtag pa zhes bya ba ni gzhan du ma yin te /
evaṃ ca / samādheḥ pratiniyataviṣayatvam uktaṃ bhavati / upaparīkṣyevastuni guṇato doṣato vā / cittasyaikāgrateti ekālambanatā
# de ltar na ting nge 'dzin kyang yul so sor nges pa nyid du bstan pa yin no / / brtag pa'i dngos po ni yon tan dang nyes pa'o / / sems rtse gcig pa ni dmigs pa gcig pa nyid de /
agraṃ hy atrālambanam ucyate / ñānasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥsamāhite citte yathābhūtaparijñānāt / upaparīkṣyaṃ vastusatyacatuṣṭayam / guṇato nirodhasatyaṃmārgasatyaṃ ca
# 'dir rtse gcig ni dmigs pa la bya'o / / sems mnyam par bzhag na yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du / / yongs su shes pa'i phyir shes pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / de la rtag pa'i dngos po ni bden pa bzhi ste /
nirodhasatyaṃśāntādyākārair upaparīkṣyaṃ / mārgasatyaṃnairyāṇikādyākāraiḥ
# 'gog pa'i bden pa la zhi ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang lam gyi bden pa la nges par 'byin pa la sogs pa'i rnam par brtags pas 'gog pa'i bden pa dang lam gyi bden pa ni yon tan no /
duḥkhasamudayasatye doṣataḥ / duḥkhamanityādyākāraiḥ hetvādyākāraiḥ samudayaḥ
# sdug bsngal gyi bden pa ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang kun 'byung ba'i bden pa la ni rgyu la sogs pa'i rnam par brtags pas sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bden pa ni nyes pa'o /
tathā navānāṃbhūmīnām adharāṃ doṣataḥ ūrdhvāṃguṇataḥ
# de bzhin dus dgu la 'og ma la ni nyes par lta gong ma la ni yon tan du'o /
evam anyeṣvapi sāmānyālambaneṣu yathāsambhavaṃ vaktavyam / prajñā katamā / tatraiva pravicayo
# de bzhin du rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid kyi dmigs pa gzhan rnams la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du brjod par bya'o / / shes rab gang zhe na / / de dag nyid la rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ste /
yogāyogavihito 'nyathā cti tatraivetyupaparīkṣya / eva vastuni
# rigs pa dang rigs pa ma yin pas bskyed pa dang gzhan pa'o zhes bya ba la / / de dag nyid la zhes bya ba ni brtag pa'i dngos po nyid la ste /
evaṃ ca samādhivat prajñāpi pratiniyataviṣayetyuktaṃ bhavati / pravicinotīti pravicayaḥ / saṃyag mithyā vāsaṅkīrṇasvasāmānyalakṣaṇeṣv iva dharmeṣu vivekāvabodhaḥ
# de ltar na ting nge 'dzin bzhin du shes rab kyang yul so sor nges pa nyid du bstan pa yin no / / rab tu rnam par 'byed pas kyang rab tu rnam par 'byed pa ste / / rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid 'dres pa lta bu'i chos rnams la yang dag pa'am / / log par so sor rtog pa'o /
yuktir yogaḥ āptopadeśaḥ anumānam pratyakṣaṃ ca
# rigs pa ni bshad ba ste / / yid ches pa'i lung dang; rjes su dpag pa dang mngon sum mo /
tena triprakāreṇa yo janitaḥ sa yogavihitaḥ / sa punaḥ śrutamayaścintāmayo bhāvanāmayaś ca
# rnam pa de gsum gyis bskyed pa gang yin pa de ni rigs pas bskyed pa'o / / de yang thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba dang bsgoms pa las byung ba ste /
tatrāptavacanaprāmāṇyajo 'vabodhaḥśrutamayaḥ
# de la yid ches pa'i gsung rab las skyes pa'i rtog pa ni thos pa las byung ba'o /
yuktinidhyānajaś cintāmayaḥ / samādhijo bhāvanāmayaḥ
# rigs pa nges par bsam pa las skyes pa ni bsams pa las byung ba'o / / ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa ni bsgoms pa las byung ba'o /
ayogaḥ punar anāptopadeśo 'numānābhāsomithyāpraṇihitaś ca samādhiḥ
# rigs ba ma yin pa ni yid ches pa ma yin pa'i lung dang rjes su dpag ba ltar snang ba dang log par bsam pa'i ting nge 'dzin te /
tena yo janitaḥ so'yogavihitaḥ
# rigs pa ma yin pa des bskyed pa ni rigs pa ma yin pas bskyed pa'o /
tatra sāṅkhyavaiśeṣikādīnāṃ śrutamayaścintāmayaś cānāptopadeśajanitatvāt kutarkajanitatvādayogavihitaḥ
# de la grangs can dang bye brag pa la sogs pa'i thos pa las byung ba dang bsams pa las byung ba ni yid ches pa ma yin pa'i lung gis bskyed pa dang rtog gi ngan pas bskyed pa'i phyir rigs pa ma yin pas bskyed pa'o /
vītarāgānāṃ tu śāśvatocchedavādināmekatyaśāśvatikādīnāṃ camithyāpraṇihitasamādhijanitatvād ayogavihitaḥ
# 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams kyi rtag pa dang chad par smra ba rnams kyi dang kha cig rtag pa rnams kyi yang log bar bsam pa'i ting nge 'dzin las skyes pa'i phyir rigs pa ma yin pas bskyed pa'o /
upapattipratilambhikolaukikavyavahārāvabodhaś canaiva yogavihito nāyogavihitaḥ
# skye bas thob pa dang 'jig rten pa'i tha snyad shes pa ni rigs pas bskyed ba yang ma yin / / mi rigs pas bskyed pa yang ma yin pa'o /
eṣa casaṃśayavyāvartanakarmakaḥ
# 'di ni som nyi bzlog pa'i las can te /
saṃśayavyāvartanaṃ tuprajñayā dharmān pravicinvato niścayalābhāt / śraddhā katamā
# som nyi bzlog pa ni shes rab kyis chos rab tu rnam par phye nas nges par thob pa'i phyir ro / / phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa'i bye brag tu bshad pa / / ba ma po gnyis pa / / dad pa gang zhe na /
karmaphalasatyaratneṣv / mabhisampratyayo 'bhilāṣaś cetasaḥ prasād / iti karma trividham puṇyam apuṇyam āniñjyaṃ ca
# las dang 'bras bu dang bden pa dang dkon mchog la mngon par yid ches pa dang 'dod pa dang sems dang ba'o zhes bya ba la las ni rnam pa gsum ste / / bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'o /
tatrāpuṇyaṃ kāmāptam eva akuśalamūlasamprayogāt
# de la bsod nams ma yin pa ni mi dge ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir 'dod par gtogs pa nyid do /
puṇyamapi vipākaniyamāt kāmāptam eva / karmavipākaṃ pratyaniñjanādāniñjyam / apuṇyasya kāmadhātāv aniṣṭo vipākaḥpuṇyasyeṣṭaḥ / aniñjasya rūpārūpadhātvor iṣṭa eva vipākaḥ / tatra karmaphalayor astīty abhisampratyayākārā śraddhā
# bsod nams ni rnam par smin pa nges ba med pa'i phyir 'dod par gtogs pa nyid do / / rnam par smin par 'gyur ba la gyo ba med pa'i phyir mi gyo ba'o / / bsod nams ma yin pa'i rnam par smin pa ni 'dod pa'i khams na mi 'dod pa'o / / bsod nams kyi ni 'dod pa'o / / mi gyo ba'i rnam par smin pa ni gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams na 'dod pa nyid do / / de la las dang 'bras bu gnyis yod par mngon par yid ches pa'i rnam pa'i dad pa ni las dge ba dang mi dge ba yod pa dang de yang 'bras bu 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dang go rims bzhin no /
astikuśalam akuśalaṃ ca karma tac ca yathākramamiṣṭāniṣṭaphalam tad api kuśalākuśalakarmahetukamneśvarādinirmitam iti ya evaṃ karmaphalasvarūpe 'viparīte cakarmaphalavipākayor hetuphalasambandhe 'bhisampratyayaḥiyaṃ karmaphalayor astitvasampratyayākārā śraddhā
# de yang dge ba dang mi dge ba'i las kyi rgyu las byung ba ste / / dbang phyug la sogs pas sbrul pa ni ma yin no zhes de ltar las dang 'bras bu'i rang gi ngo bo phyin ci ma log pa las dang 'bras bu'i rnam par smin pa gnyis rgyu dang 'bras bur 'brel bar mngon par yid ches ba gang yin pa de ni las dang 'bras bu gnyis yod pa nyid du yid ches pa'i rnam pa'i dad pa'o /
duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgāḥ satyāni
# bden pa ni sdug bsngal ba dang kun 'byung ba dang 'gog pa dang lam rnams te /
āryāṇāṃpratikūlatvād anityatvāditvenāvitathatvāc ca phalabhūtāḥpañcopādānaskandhā duḥkhasatyam
# 'phags pa rnams dang mi mthun pa dang mi rtag pa la sogs pa nyid du ma nor ba'i phyir 'bras bur gyur pa nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po dag ni sdug bsngal gyi bden pa'o /
duḥkhahetutvātpratyayādyākāraiś cāviparītatvād dhetubhūtās ta eva pañcopādānaskandhāḥ samudayasatyam
# sdug bsngal gyi rgyur gyur pa dang rkyen la sogs pa'i rnam par phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir rgyur gyur pa'i nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po de dag nyid kun 'byung ba'i bden pa'o /
sahetukaduḥkhopaśamātmakatvāc chāntādyākārāviparītatvāc ca duḥkhanirodho nirodhasatyam
# sdug bsngal rgyu dang bcas pa nye bar zhi ba'i bdag dang zhi ba la sogs pa'i rnam par phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir sdug bsngal 'gog pa ni 'gog pa'i bden pa'o /
duḥkhanirodhaprāpakatvānnairyāṇikatvādinā 'vitathatvāc cāryāṣṭāṅgamārgo mārgasatyam
# sdug bsngal 'gog pa thob par byed pa dang nges par 'byin pa la sogs pa'i rnam par phyin ci ma log pa'i phyir / / 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa ni 'phags pa'i bden pa'o /
tatra duḥkhasamudayasatyayor asti duḥkham asti samudaya ity abhisampratyayākāraiva śraddhā
# de la sdug bsngal dang kun 'byung ba'i bden pa gnyis la sdug bsngal yod do / / kun 'byung ba yod do zhes yod par mngon par yid ches pa'i rnam pa nyid dang ba'o /
nirodhamārgasatyayor abhilāṣākārā śraddhāśakyo mayāprāptuṃ nirodho mārgaś cotpādayitumiti
# 'gog pa dang lam gyi bden pa gnyis la bdag gis 'gog pa thob par bya ba dang lam bskyed par nus so snyam du 'dod pa'i rnam pa ni dad pa'o /
ratnāni trīṇi buddhadharmasaṅghāḥ
# dkon mchog ni gsum ste / / sangs rgyas dang chos dang dge 'dun rnams so /
durlabhatvānmahārghatvāt prītikaratvād upakārakaratvād amānuṣādyupaghātapratipakṣatvāc ca ratnānīva ratnāni
# dkon pa nyid dang rin che ba nyid dang dga' bar byed pa dang phan 'dogs pa dang mi ma yin pa la sogs pa gnod pa byed pa'i gnyen por gyur pa'i phyir rin po che dang 'dra bas na dkon mchog go /
tatradurlabhatvaṃ bhavabhogeṣv asaktaiḥ kāyajīvitanirapekṣairbodhisattvair nairantaryeṇa bodhisambhāreṣu pravartamānaistribhiḥ kalpāsaṅkhyeyair buddhatvaṃ prāpyata iti durlabham
# de la dkon pa nyid ni byang chub sems dpa' srid pa dang longs spyod la ma chags pas lus dang srog la mi lta ba rgyun mi chad par byang chub kyi tshogs la zhugs pa rnams kyis kyang sangs rgyas nyid bskal pa grangs med pa gsum gyis thob par bya ba yin pas na dkon pa nyid do /
ata evodumbarapuṣpaprādurbhāvavad durlabho buddhotpādaucyate / buddhotpādasya ca durlabhatvāddharmasaṅgharatnayor api durlabhatvaṃbuddhotpādapratibaddhatvāt
# de'i phyir sangs rgyas 'byung ba nyid ni au dum b'a ra'i me tog 'byung ba dang 'dra bar dkon pa zhes bya'o / / sangs rgyas 'byung ba la rag las pa'i phyir chos dang dge 'dun dkon mchog kyang dkon pa nyid do /
mahārghatvaṃ punaḥprāptaprakāmaprakarṣāvasthaiḥ puṇyajñānobhayasambhāraiḥprāpyatvāt
# rin che ba nyid ni 'dod dgu mthar phyin pa'i gnas thob pa rnams kyis bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs gnyis kas thob par bya ba yin pa'i phyir ro /
tatra puṇyasambhāro dānaśīlakṣāntipāramitāstisraḥ
# de la bsod nams kyi tshogs ni sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang gsum mo /
jñānasambhāraḥ prajñādhyānapāramite
# ye shes kyi tshogs ni shes rab dang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o /
puṇy ajñā nasa mbhā rāṅg abhā vaga manā dvīryapāramitobhayasambhāraḥ
# bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi yan lag gi dngos por gyur pas brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshogs gnyi gar gtogs pa'o /
dharmaratnam apisarvasaṃskṛtaparityāgena prāpyatvāt mahārgham
# chos dkon mchog ni 'dus byas thams cad yongs su btang bas thob par bya ba yin pa'i phyir rin che ba'o /
saṅgharatnam api sāṃsārikaphalanirvartakaviśiṣṭābhyāṃpuṇyajñānābhyāṃ prāpyata iti mahārgham
# dge 'dun dkon mchog ni 'khor ba'i 'bras bu 'grub pa las khyad par du gyur pa'i phyir / / bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs gnyis kyis thob par bya ba yin pas rin che ba'o /
ratnatrayaṃ hidarśanaśravaṇānusmaranaiḥ prītihetutvāt prītikaram
# dkon mchog gsum ni mthong ba dang thos pa dang rjes su dran na dga' bar byed pa'i phyir dga' ba'i rgyur 'gyur bas dga' bar byed pa'o /
tathāabhigamanādhyupāsanānveṣaṇaparijñānaiḥ sattvānāmupakārakaram
# 'di ltar bsu ba dang bsnyen bkur bya ba dang brtsal ba dang yongs su shes par bya ba rnams kyis sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa yin pas phan 'dogs pa ste /
yathoktam śrīkaraṃ te 'bhigamanam śaṅkaram adhyupāsanam / anveṣaṇaṃ matikaram parijñānaṃ viśodhanaṃiti
# ji skad du / / khyod la bsu bas dpal du byed / / bsnyen bkur byas na bde bar byed / / kun du tshol bas blo gros byed / / yongs su shes byed rnam par sbyong / / zhes bya ba brjod pa lta bu'o /
amānuṣādyupaghātapraśamanaṃ punar yathoktaṃ sūtre saced bho bhikṣavo 'raṇyagatānāṃ veti vistareṇa yāvad yat tadbhaviṣyati bhayaṃ vā chambhitatvaṃ vā romaharṣo vā tatpratigamiṣyatīti
# mi ma yin pa la sogs pa gnod par byed pa zhi bar byed pa ni mdo las ji skad du / / dge slong dag gal te khyod dgon pa na gnas kyang rung zhes bya ba nas / / 'jigs sam bag tsha ba'am sbu zing zhes byed pa'i bar du 'gyur ba de zhi bar 'gyur ro zhes rgya cher gsungs pa lta bu'o /
evaṃ dharmaratnānusmaraṇesaṅgharatnānusmaraṇe ca vaktavyam
# de bzhin du chos dkon mchog rjes su dran pa dang dge 'dun dkon mchog rjes su dran pa la yang brjod bar bya'o /
tatra sarvasmiñ jñeye'saktāpratihatajñānaśaktilābhād āśrayaparāvṛttir buddhaḥ
# de la shes bya thams cad la chags pa med cing thogs pa med par mkhyen pa'i mthu brnyes pas gnas gyur pa ni sangs rgyas te /
sā punaḥ sarvasāsravadharmabījāpagatāsarvānāsravadharmabījapracitā anantaprabhāvaparigrahā cintāmaṇiratnavad anābhogenāśeṣasattvārthakaraṇasamartheti
# de ni zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad kyi sa bon dang bral ba zag pa med pa'i chos thams cad kyi sa bon rgyas pa / / mthu stobs mtha' yas pas yongs su bzung ba'i phyir yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che ltar lhun gyis grub par sems can ma lus pa'i don mdzad par spyod pa'o /
dharmas trividhaḥ
# chos ni rnam pa gsum ste /
deśanādharmaḥ sūtrageyādikaḥ / pratipattidharma āryāṣṭāṅgo mārgaḥ sopacāraḥ / paramārthadharmo nirvāṇam / sa ca dviprakāraḥ sopadhiśeṣonirupadhiśeṣaś ca
# bstan pa'i chos mdo'i sde dang dbyangs kyis bsnyad pa'i sde la sogs pa dang sgrub pa'i chos 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad pa 'khor dang bcas pa dang don dam pa'i chos mya ngan las 'das pa'o / / de yang rnam pa gnyis te / / phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'o /
tatra kleśavisaṃyogākhyaḥ sopadhiśeṣaḥ
# de la nyon mongs pa dang bral ba zhes bya ba ni phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa'o /
vartamānajanmanirodhe 'nāgatajanmānutpādo nirūpadhiśeṣaḥ
# da ltar gyi skye ba 'gags nas ma 'ongs pa'i skye ba mi 'byung ba ni phung po'i lhag ma med pa'o /
aṣṭau puruṣapudgalāḥ saṅghaḥ catvāraḥ pratipannāś catvāraśca phalasthāḥ
# dge 'dun ni skyes bu gang zag brgyad de / / 'jug pa bzhi dang 'bras bu la gnas pa bzhi'o /
parasparataḥ śāstṛtaś cābhedyārthena saṅghaḥ
# phan tshun mi phyed pa dang ston pa mi phyed pa'i phyir dge 'dun no /
sarvaguṇadoṣaprakarṣāpakarṣaniṣṭhāgatatvād buddhebhagavati romāñcāśrupātādisūcitā prasādalakṣaṇā śraddhā
# yon tan dang nyes pa thams cad mchog tu phyin pa dang bsal ba'i mthar phyin pa'i gnas pa yin pa'i phyir / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de la spu zing zhes byed pa dang mchi ma 'byung ba la sogs pas mtshon pa'i dang ba'i mtshan nyid ni dad pa'o /
sarvasahetukaduḥkhopaśamātmakatvāt prāpakatvāttaddyotakatvāc ca dharme prasādalakṣanaiva śraddhā
# rgyu dang bcas pa'i sdug bsngal thams cad zhi ba'i bdag nyid dang thob par byed pa dang gsal bar byed pa'i phyir dang ba'i mtshan nyid ni chos la dad pa'o /
saṃsārapaṅkottīrnatvāt saṃsārapaṅkottaraṇamārgāvasthitatvācca saṅghe 'pi prasādātmikaiva
# 'khor ba'i 'dam rdzab las rgal ba dang 'khor ba'i 'dam rdzab las rgal ba'i lam la gnas pa'i phyir / / dge 'dun la dang ba'i bdag nyid ni dad pa'o /
śraddhā hi trividhā pravartate
# dad pa ni rnam pa gsum du 'gyur te /
sati vastuni guṇavaty aguṇavativā sampratyayākārā sati guṇavati ca prasādākārā satiguṇavati ca prāptum utpādayituṃ śakye 'bhilāṣākārā
# dngos po yod pa yon tan can nam yon tan can ma yin pa la yid ches pa'i rnam pa dang yod pa'i yon tan can la dang ba'i rnam pa dang yod pa yon tan can thob pa'am / / skyed nus pa la 'dod pa'i rnam pa'o /
nanvevam abhilāṣākāratvāt tṛṣṇācchandayor anyatarā bhavati / naitad evam
# de ltar na 'dod pa'i rnam pa yin pa'i phyir sred pa'am / / 'dun pa gang yang rung ba zhig tu mi 'gyur ram / / de ni de lta ma yin te /
kuśalaviṣayatvān na tṛṣṇā śraddhāpūrvakatvācchandasya na cchandaḥ
# dge ba yul yin pa'i phyir sred pa ma yin no / / 'dun pa ni dad pa sngon du 'gro ba yin pas 'dun pa ma yin no /
cetasaḥ prasāda iti śraddhā hicittakāluṣyavairodhikīty atas tatsamprayogekleśopakleśamalakāluṣyavigamāc cittaṃ śraddhām āgamyaprasīdatīti cetasaḥ prasāda ucyate / udakaprasādakamaṇisthānīyaṃ dharmāntaraṃ caitasikaṃśraddhā na rūpaprasādātmiketi pradarśanārtham āha cetasaḥprasāda iti / cetasaḥ prasādo na rūpasyeti / sā punaśchandasanniśrayadānakarmikā / hrīḥ katamā / ātmānaṃ dharmaṃ / vādhipatiṃ kṛtvāvadyena lajjā / yatpratibaddhā / yasya kriyāsu pravṛttir nivṛttir vā sa tasyādhipatiḥ svāmītyarthaḥ
# sems dang ba zhes bya ba la dad pa ni sems kyi rnyog pa dang mi mthun pa ste / / de'i phyir de dang mtshungs par ldan na nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i rnyog pa mi 'byung ste / / dad pa la brten nas sems dang bar 'gyur bas sems dang ba zhes bya ste / / chu dang bar byed pa'i nor bu dang 'dra ba'i chos gzhan sems las byung ba la dang ba zhes bya'o / / gzugs dang pa'i bdag nyid ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir sems dang ba zhes bya ba smos te / / gzugs ni ma yin no / / de ni 'dun pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / ngo tsha shes pa gang zhe na / / bdag gam chos kyi dbang du byas te / / kha na mtho bas 'dzem pa'o zhes bya ba ni gang la brten nas su zhig bya ba rnams la 'jug pa dang ldog pa de ni de'i dbang du byed pa ste / / bdag por byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ātmānaṃ dharmaṃ vādhipatiṃ svāminaṃ kṛtvāsadbhir vigarhitatvād aniṣṭavipākatvāc ca pāpam evāvadyam tenāvadyena kṛtenākṛtena vā cittasyāvalīnatā lajjā
# dam pa rnams kyis smad pa dang rnam par smin pa mi 'dod pa yin pas sdig pa nyid kha na ma tho ba ste / / byas kyang rung ma byas kyang rung bdag gam chos kyi dbang bdag por byas nas / / kha na ma tho ba des sems bag 'khums pa ni 'dzem pa'o /
kulajñānādibhir guṇaiḥ pāpakriyāyām ātmānam ayogyaṃ matvā kathaṃ hi sā mama yaivaṃvidhenaivaṃ pāpaṃ kṛtaṃkriyate kariṣyate vā dharme 'py etad aniṣṭavipākatvātparopaghātapravṛttatvāc ca garhitam ity evaṃ yātmānaṃ dharmaṃ cāvekṣamāṇasyāvadyena lajjāsā hrīḥ / iyaṃ caduścaritasaṃyamanasanniśrayadānakarmikā / apatrāpyaṃ katamat / lokam adhipatiṃ / kṛtvāvadyena lajjā / loke hy etad garhitam māṃ
# rigs dang shes rgya la sogs pa'i yon tan rnams kyis sdig pa bya bar mi rigs par shes pas bdag 'di lta bur gyur pas sdig pa 'di lta bu ga la bya zhe'am / / byed par 'gyur ba lta ga la rung snyam pa dang mi 'dod pa'i rnam par smin par 'gyur ba dang gzhan la gnod par byed par zhugs pa'i phyir / / chos las kyang smad pa'o / / zhes de ltar ji tsam du bdag gam chos la lta zhing kha na ma tho bas 'dzem pa gang yin pa de ngo tsha shes pa'o / / 'di ni nyes par spyod pa yang dag par sdom pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / khrel yod pa gang zhe na / / 'jig rten gyi dbang du byas te kha na ma tho bas 'dzem pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten na 'di ni smad pa ste /
caivaṅkarmāṇaṃ viditvā vigarhiṣyantīty aślokādibhayād avadyena lajjate
# bdag la las 'di lta bu rigs na smod par 'gyur ro zhes tshigs su bcad pa ma yin pa la sogs pa'i 'jigs pas kha na ma tho ba la 'dzem pa'o /
idam apiduścaritasaṃyamanasanniśrayadānakarmakameva / duścaritādvirati saṃyamanam / lajjamānasyāpatrapamāṇasya vā kṛte 'piduścarite 'vaśyaṃ tadviramaṇād anayostatsanniśrayadānakarmakatvam / alobhaity ayam akāras triṣv artheṣu vartate / abhāve
# 'di yang nyes par spyod pa yang dag par sdom pa'i rten byed pa'i las can nyid do / / ngo tsha shes pa de ni nyes par spyod par byas na yang gdon mi za ba spong bas yang dag par sngom pa yin no / / ngo tsha shes pa dang khrel yod pa ni nyes par spyod pa byas na yang gdon mi za bar de spong bas yang dag par sdom pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / khrel yod pa ni nyes par spyod par ma byas na yang dag par sdom pas 'di gnyis ni de'i rten byed pa'i las can te / / sngon du 'dren pa nyid do / / ma chags pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba la ma chags zhes bya ba ni don rnam pa gsum la 'jug ste /
'nyasmin pratipakṣe ca
# med pa dang gzhan pa dang gnyen po la'o /
atra pratipakṣa eva vartate nānyasminnābhāva iti pradarśanārtham āha lobhapratipakṣa iti / evam adveṣe amohe ca vaktavyam / nirvid anāgraha ititatsvarūpanirūpaṇam
# 'dir ni gnyen po nyid la 'jug gi med pa dang gzhan la ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir / / chags pa'i gnyen po ste zhes bya ba smos so; / / zhe sdang med pa dang gti mug med pa la yang de bzhin du brjod par bya'o / / yid 'byung zhing mi len pa'o zhes bya ba ni de'i rang gi ngo bo la rtog pa mdzad pa'o /
lobho nāma bhave bhavopakaraṇeṣu caāsaktiḥ prārthanā ca
# chags pa zhes bya ba ni srid pa dang longs spyod rnams la kun du chags pa dang smon pa gang yin pa'o /
tatpratipakṣo 'lobhobhavebhavopakaraṇeṣu cānāsaktirvaimukhyaṃ ca
# de'i gnyen po ni ma chags pa ste / / srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad rnams la chags pa dang mi phyogs pa'o /
nirvidbhavabhogādīnāṃ parijñānād bhave bhavopakaraṇeṣu cavaimukhyam
# yid byung ba ni sred pa dang longs spyod kyi nyes dmigs yongs su shes pa'i phyir srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad rnams la mi phyogs pa'o /
anāgraho bhavabhavabhogayor asaktiḥ
# mi len pa ni srid pa dang longs spyod gnyi ga la ma chags pa'o /
athavānāgrahaviśeṣaṇārthaṃ nirvidgrahaṇaṃ bhavebhavopakaraṇeṣu ca vaimukhyākāro yo 'nāgraho 'yam alobhaiti / ayaṃ caduścaritāpravṛttisanniśrayadānakarmakiti / adveṣaḥ katamaḥ
# yang na mi len pa'i bye brag gi phyir yid byung ba smos te / / srid pa dang srid pa'i yo byad rnams la mi phyogs pa'i rnam pa gang yin pa'i mi len pa de ma chags pa zhes bya'o / / 'di ni nyes par spyod pa la mi 'jug pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / zhe sdang med ba gang zhe na /
dveṣapratipakṣo maitrī
# zhe sdang gi gnyen po ste /
dveṣo hi sattveṣu duḥkhe duḥkhasthānīyeṣu ca dharmeṣvāghātaḥ
# byams pa'o zhes bya ba la zhe sdang ni sems can rnams dang sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi gnas kyi chos rnams la kun nas mnar sems pa ste /
tatpratipakṣo 'nāghātaḥ
# de'i gnyen po ni kun nas mnar sems pa med pa'o /
dveṣasyānye 'pi pratipakṣāḥsantīty ata āha maitrī
# zhe sdang gi gnyen po ni gzhan dag kyang yod pas de'i phyir byams pa smos te /
maitrātmako dveṣasya yaḥ pratipakṣaḥ so 'dveṣaḥ nānya iti
# zhe sdang gi gnyen po byams pa'i bdag nyid gang yin pa de ni zhe sdang med pa ste /
ayam apiduścaritāpravṛttisanniśrayadānakarmakaiti
# gzhan ni ma yin no / / nyes par spyod pa la mi 'jug pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
amohaḥ katamaḥ / mohapratipakṣo / bhūtasampratipattiḥ
# gti mug med pa gang zhe na gti mug gi gnyen po ste / / yang dag pa la yang dag par rtogs pa'o zhes bya ba la /
sarva eva hi kuśalā dharmāḥkliṣṭānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ samudācāravirodhāt pratipakṣa ity ata āha bhūtasampratipattir iti / saṃyagaviparītapratipattibhedāt / sā punar dvividhājñānaṃ pratisaṅkhyā ca
# dge ba'i chos thams cad ni nyon mongs pa can gyi chos rnams kun du 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa yin pas gnyen po yin te / / de'i phyir yang dag pa la yang dag par rtogs pa'i zhes bya ba smos te / / yang dag par phyin ci ma logs par rtogs pa'o / / de yang bye brag gis rnam pa gnyis te / / shes pa dang so sor rtog pa'o /
punaś caturvidhā vipākāgamacintādhigamanimittā
# shes pa yang rnam par smin pa dang lung dang bsam pa dang rtogs pa'i rgyu'i bye brag gis rnam pa bzhi'o /
pratisaṅkhyā tu prajñaivadhairyasahitā
# so sor rtog pa ni shes rab bstan pa dang bcas pa nyid do /
dhairyam iti prajñāvīryasamādhaya ucyante
# bstan pa zhes bya ba ni shes rab dang brtson 'grus dang ting nge 'dzin rnams la bya'o /
tatra dvayoḥ prajñādravyayoḥ samavadhānāsambhavād vīryeṇa samādhinā vā samprayuktā prajñā pratisaṅkhyety ucyateyadbalenānuddhṛtānupahatakleśabījo 'pi kleśānām avakāśan nadadati / ayamatra vākyārthaḥ
# de la shes rab kyi rdzas gnyis 'grogs mi srid pas brtson 'grus sam / / ting nge 'dzin dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i shes rab la so sor rtog pa zhes bya ste / / gang gi stobs kyis nyon mongs pa'i sa bon ma bton ma bcom yang nyon mongs pa rnams kyi skabs mi 'byed pa'o / / 'dir tshig gi don ni 'di yin te /
yathābhūtajñānātmakaḥpratisaṅkhyātmakaś ca jñānaviśeṣo 'moha ity ucyate
# yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du shes pa'i bdag nyid dang so sor rtog pa'i bdag nyid kyi shes pa khyad par can ni gti mug med pa zhes bya ste /
ataevāmohoduścaritāpravṛttisanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / vīryaṃ katamat / kausīdyapratipakṣaḥ / jkuśalecetaso 'bhyutsāhaḥj k i / kutsitaṃ sīdatīti / kusīdaḥ / tadbhāvaḥ kausīdyam / ālasyam ity arthaḥ / tac cakuśalākuśalayoś cittasyānutsāhaḥ
# de'i phyir gti mug med pa ni nyes par spyod pa la mi 'jug pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / brtson 'grus gang zhe na / / le lo'i gnyen po ste / / dge ba la sems mngon par spro ba'o zhes bya ba la sbyor ba dman pa ni le lo ste / / snyom las byed ces bya ba'i tha tshig go de ni dge ba dang mi dge ba la sems mi spro ba'o / / de'i gnyen po ni brtson 'grus yin pas /
tatpratipakṣaś ca vīryam ityataḥ kausīdyavad ubhayaprasaṅge vyavacchedārtham āha kuśale cetaso 'bhyutsāho vīryamna tu kliṣṭa iti / kliṣṭe tūtsāhaḥkutsitatvāt kausīdyam eva
# de'i phyir le lo bzhin du gnyi gar thal bar 'gyur ba rnam par gcad pa'i phyir / / brtson 'grus ni dge ba la sems mngon par spro ba'o zhes bya ba smos te / / nyon mongs pa can la spro ba ni ma yin no / / nyon mongs pa can la spro ba ni smad pa yin pa'i phyir le lo nyid do /
nanu ca kliṣṭaṃ svabhyastatvātsvarasenaiva pravartatekiṃ tatrotsāhena / prāyeṇaivam
# nyon mongs pa can la shin tu goms pa'i phyir / / rang gi ngang gis 'jug bzhin du de la spro bar bya ci dgos she na phal cher ni de lta mod kyi /
asti tukiñcid yatrotsāho 'py apekṣyate
# gang du spro ba la ltos pa yang cung zad yod do /
tat punar yatsamprayogātsannāhe prayoge vāalīnatve vāvyāvṛttau vāsantuṣṭau vākuśaleṣu dharmeṣu cetaso 'bhyutsāhaḥ tad vīryam
# de yang gang dang mtshungs par ldan na go cha dang sbyor ba dang; mi 'god pa dang mi ldog pa dang chog par mi 'dzin pa dang dge ba'i chos gzhan rnams la yang sems mngon par spro ba de ni brtson 'grus te /
kuśalapakṣaparipūraṇapariniṣpādanakarmakaṃ
# dge ba'i phyogs yongs su rdzogs par byed pa dang yongs su sgrub pa'i las can no /
paripūraṇaṃyathā maulapraveśaḥ
# yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ni ji ltar dngos gzhi la 'jug pa lta bu'o /
pariniṣpādanaṃ tasyaivaparikarmakṛtatvaṃ / prasrabdhiḥ katamā / auṣṭhulyapratipakṣaḥ
# yongs su sgrub pa ni de nyid legs par yongs su sbyang bar byas pa'o / / shin tu sbyangs pa gang zhe na / / gnas ngan len gyi gnyen po ste /
kāyacittakarmaṇyatā
# lus dang sems las su rung ba nyid do zhes bya ba la /
dauṣṭhulyaṃ kāyacittayor akarmaṇyatā sāṅkleṣikadharmabījāni ca
# lus dang sems kyi gnas ngan len ni las su mi rung ba nyid dang kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos kyi sa bon rnams ti go rims bzhin no /
tadapagameprasrabdhisadbhāvāddauṣṭhulyapratipakṣaḥ
# de med na ni shin tu sbyangs pa yod pa'i phyir gnyen po'o /
lakṣaṇaṃ tuprasrabdheḥ kāyacittakarmaṇyatā
# shin tu sbyangs pa'i mtshan nyid ni lus dang sems las su rung ba nyid do /
tatra kāyakarmaṇyatākāyasya svakāryeṣu laghusamutthānatā yato bhavati
# de la lus las su rung ba ni lus kyi rang gi bya ba rnams la ldang ba yang ba gang las byung ba'o /
cittakarmaṇyatā samyaṅmanasikāraprayuktasya hlādalāghavanimittaṃ yac caitasikaṃ dharmāntaram
# sems las su rung ba ni yang dag pa'i yid la byed pa la zhugs pa'i sems kyi sim pa dang yang bar 'gyur ba'i rgyu sems las byung ba'i chos gzhan du gyur pa gang yin pa ste /
tadyogāccittam asaktam ālambane pravartata ity atas taccittakarmaṇyatety ucyate
# de dang ldan na dmigs pa la sems thogs pa med par 'jug pas de'i phyir sems las su rung ba zhes bya ba'o /
kāyasya punaḥ spraṣṭavyaviśeṣa evaprītyāhṛtaḥ kāyaprasrabdhir veditavyā
# lus kyi reg bya'i khyad par dga' bas zin pa la lus shin tu sbyang bar rig par bya ste /
prītamanasaḥ kāyaḥprasrabhyataiti sūtre vacanāt
# yid dga' na lus shin tu sbyangs par 'gyur ro zhes mdo las gsungs pa'i phyir ro /
atra caitasikādhikārād acaitasiky api kāyaprasrabdhiḥprasrabdhisambodhyaṅgatvenoktākāyakarmaṇyatā vācittakarmaṇyatām āvāhayatīty ato'caitasiky api kāyakarmaṇyatātroktā
# 'dir lus shin tu sbyangs pa sems las byung ba ma yin du zin kyang sems las byung ba'i skabs yin pas shin tu sbyangs pa yang dag byang chub kyi yan lag tu bshad do / / yang na lus las su rung ban yid ni sems las su rung ba sgrub par byed pa'i phyir te / / de'i phyir sems las byung ba ma yin du zin kyang /
iyaṃ catadbalenāśrayaparāvṛttito'śeṣakleśādyāvaraṇaniṣkarṣaṇakarmikāapramādaḥ katamaḥ / pramādapratipakṣo 'lobho yāvad vīryam / yān niśrityākuśalān / dharmān prajahāti / tatpratipakṣāṃścakuśalān dharmān bhāvayatīti / pramādo hi yena
# 'dir lus las su rung ba nyid du brjod do / / 'di ni de'i dbang gis gnas 'gyur bas nyon mongs pa la sogs pa'i sgrib ba ma lus pa sel ba'i las can no / / bag yod pa gang zhe na / / bag med pa'i gnyen po ste / / ma chags pa nas brtson 'grus kyi bar de dag la gnas nas mi dge ba'i chos spong zhing de'i gnyen po dge ba'i chos rnams kyang bsgom pa'o zhes bya ba la bag med pa ni /
kleśebhyaś cittaṃ na rakṣati kuśalaṃ ca hāpayati
# gang gis nyon mongs pa rnams las sems mi srung zhing dge ba rnams 'bri bar byed pa'o /
apramādenapunaḥ kleśān prajahātipratipakṣāṃś ca dharmān bhāvayatītyato 'pramādaḥ pramādapratipakṣa uktaḥ / alobho yāvad vīryamity alobhādveṣāmohāḥ saha vīryeṇa gṛhyante
# bag yod pa ni nyon mongs pa rnams spong zhing de'i gnyen po'i chos rnams kyang bsgom pa ste / / de'i phyir bag yod pa ni bag med pa'i gnyen por bstan pa'o / / ma chags pa nas brtson 'grus kyi bar zhes bya ba ni ma chags pa dang zhe sdang med pa dang gti mug med pa dang brtson 'grus dang bcas par gzung /
yān alobhādīnvīryaparyantān niśrityāgamya prāpyākuśalān dharmānprajahātīty anena sarve alobhādayo 'pramāda ity uktaṃ bhavati
# ma chags pa la sogs pa nas brtson 'grus la thug pa'i bar de dag la gnas pa ni brten pa dang gnas bcas nas mi dge ba'i chos rnams spong ba ste / / 'dis ni ma chags pa la sogs pa thams cad bag yod par bstan pa yin no /
akuśalā dharmā āsravā āsravasthānīyāś ca viṣayā veditavyāḥ
# mi dge ba'i chos rnams ni zag pa dang zag pa'i gnas yul rnams su rig par bya'o /
tatra āsravāṇām vinodanaviṣkambhaṇabījasamuddhārātmakaṃ prahāṇam
# de la zag pa rnams sel ba dang rnam par gnon pa dang sa bon yang dag pa 'don pa'i bdag nyid ni spong ba'o /
viṣayāṇāṃ punaḥ parivarjanena prahāṇam
# yul rnams ni yongs su spangs pas spong ngo /
tatpratipakṣā ity akuśaladharmapratipakṣāḥ
# de'i gnyen po zhes bya ba ni mi dge ba'i chos kyi gnyen po rnams te /
te punaḥkuśalasāsravā anāsravāś ca
# de dag kyang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa rnams so /
teṣām abhyāso bhāvanāpaunaḥpunyena sammukhīkaraṇam
# sgom pa ni de dag goms par byed pa ste / / yang dang yang mngon du byed pa'o /
yasmād vīryasahītān alobhādīn niśrityākuśalān dharmān prajahāti tatpratipakṣāṃśca dharmān bhāvayati tasmāt savīryeṣv alobhādiṣv apramādaḥprajñapyata ity anena sādhiṣṭhānā sakāraṇā cāpramādasyaprajñaptir uktā
# 'di ltar brtson 'grus dang bcas pa'i ma chags pa la sogs pa la brten nas mi dge ba'i chos rnams spong zhing de'i gnyen po dge ba'i chos kyang sgom pa'i phyir / / brtson 'grus yan chad dang bcas pa'i ma chags pa la bag yod pa gdags te / / 'dis ni gnas dang bcas pa'am / / rgyu dang bcas pa la bag yod pa gdags par bstan pa yin no /
sa punaḥsarvalaukikalokottarasampattiparipūraṇakarmakaḥ
# 'di ni 'jig rten pa dang; 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phun sum tshogs pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i las can no /
tatra laukikasampattir bhavabhogaviśeṣalābhaḥ lokottarāśrāvakādibodhyadhigamaḥ
# de la 'jig rten pa'i phun sum tshogs pa ni srid pa dang longs spyod kyi khyad par rnyed pa'o / / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phun sum tshogs pa ni nyan thos la sogs pa'i byang chub thob pa'o /
upekṣā katamā
# btang snyoms gang zhe na /
sa evālobho yāvad vīryam / ityādi apramāda ivātrāpi vyākhyānam
# ma chags pa nas brtson 'grus kyi bar de dag nyid la gnas shing zhes bya ba la sogs pa bag yod pa bzhin du 'dir yang bshad par bya'o /
cittasamatādibhistribhiḥ padair upekṣāyā ādimadhyāvasānāvasthādyotitā
# sems mnyam pa nyid dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa tshig gsum gyis ni btang snyoms kyi thog ma dang bar dang tha ma'i dus bstan to /
tatra layauddhatyaṃ cetaso vaiṣamyam / tasyābhāvād ādaucittasyasamatā
# de la bying ba dang rgod pa ni sems mi mnyam pa ste / / de med pas thog mar sems mnyam pa nyid do /
tato 'nabhisaṃskāreṇāprayatnena samāhitacetasoyathāyogaṃ samasyaiva pravṛttiḥ praśaṭhatā
# de'i 'og tu mngon par 'du byed pa med cing bsgrim mi dgos par mnyam par gzhog pa'i sems kyis ci rigs par mnyam par 'jug pa ni rnal du 'dug pa'o /
sā punaravasthā layauddhatyāśaṅkānugatā acirabhāvitatvāt
# de'i dus na ni bsgoms nas ring po ma lon pa'i phyir bying ba dang rgod pa 'byung bar dogs pa dang ldan no /
tatobhāvanāprakarṣagamanāt tadvipakṣadūrībhāvāttacchaṅkābhāve layauddhatyapratipakṣanimitteṣv ābhogamakurvato 'nābhogāvasthatācittasyānābhogatā / yayā
# de'i 'og tu bsgom pa khyad zhugs par gyur pas de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs thag ring du gyur pa'i phyir gnyis 'byung du dogs pa med de / / bying ba dang rgod pa'i gnyen po'i rgyu rnams la rtsol ba mi byed pas / / sems lhun gyis grub par gnas so /
nirvāsiteṣu kliṣṭeṣu dharmeṣv iti yayety upekṣaivasambadhyate
# gang gis nyon mongs pa can gyi chos rnams bsal nas zhes bya ba la gang gis zhes bya ba ni btang snyoms nyid dang sbyar ro /
kliṣṭā dharmā rāgādisahitāḥ / teṣāṃ nirvāsanaṃpunaranutpattiḥ
# nyon mongs pa can gyi chos rnams zhes bya ba ni 'dod chags la sogs pa dag dang bcas pa dag go / / de dag bsal na yang mi skye ba'o /
upekṣā hi saṅkliṣṭavihāravairodhikītyavaśyaṃ tayā rāgādipravṛttivibandhevartitavyam ity atas tayānirvāsiteṣv ity uktam
# btang snyoms ni nyon mongs pa can du gnas pa dang mi mthun pas gdon mi za bar des 'dod chags la sogs pa 'byung ba'i gnas med do / / de'i phyir des bsal zhes brjod do /
yataś ca saṅkliṣṭena vihāreṇopekṣāvirūdhyate tenopekṣāvihāryasaṅkliṣṭavihārī / bhavatīti
# 'di ltar nyon mongs pa can du gnas pa ni btang snyoms dang mi mthun pas de'i phyir btang snyoms la gnas ba ni nyon mongs pa can ma yin par gnas pa yin te /
ataś copekṣāsaṅkleśānavakāśasanniśrayadānakarmikā
# de nyid kyi phyir btang snyoms ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i skabs mi 'byed pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
avihiṃsā katamā / vihiṃsāpratipakṣaḥ
# rnam par mi 'tshe ba gang zhe na / / rnam par 'tshe ba'i gnyen po ste /
karuṇeti / vadhabandhādibhir aviheṭhanam adrohaṇaṃsattvānām avihiṃseti vihiṃsāpratipakṣaḥ / kaṃ ruṇaddhītikaruṇā / kam iti sukhasyākhyā / sukhaṃ ruṇaddhīty arthaḥ / kāruṇiko hi paraduḥkhaduḥkhī bhavatīti / iyaṃ cāpramādavat prajñaptita eva na dravyasatīadveṣāṃśaeva prajñapanāt / viheṭhanakarmikā / uktā ekādaśa kuśalāḥ / ṣaṭ kleśā vaktavyāḥ / ta ucyante rāgaḥ katamaḥ / pañcasūpādānaskandheṣu sneho'dhyavasānaṃ / sāsravāṇi
# snying rje ba'o zhes bya ba la gsod pa dang 'ching ba la sogs pas tho mi 'tshams shing sems can rnams la gnod pa mi byed pa ni rnam par mi 'tshe ba'o / / rnam bar 'tshe ba'i gnyen po ni snying rje ba ste / / bsod nyams bsrel ba'o / / bsod nyams zhes bya ba ni bde ba ste / / bde ba bsrel zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / snying rje can gyi pha rol sdug bsngal na sdug bsngal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / 'di yang bag yod pa bzhin du btags pa nyid do / / zhe sdang med pa'i cha la btags ba'i phyir rdzas su yod pa ni ma yin no / / tho mi 'tshams pa'i las can no / / dge ba bcu gcig bshad zin to / / nyon mongs pa drug brjod par bya ba de dag brjod par bya'o / / 'dod chags gang zhe na /
rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānāni pañca rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānopadānaskandhāḥ / tatrarūpopādānaskandho dvaidhātukaṃ rūpam
# nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga la zhen pa dang lhag par chags pa'o zhes bya ba la zag pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa lnga ni gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams so /
vedanādyupādānaskandhāś catvāras traidhātukā vedanādayaḥ / upādīyate 'nayā tṛṣṇayā tribhavotpattiḥ paunarbhavikaṃ vākarmeti tṛṣṇāyāupādānākhyā
# de la gzugs nye bar len pa'i phung po ni khams gnyis kyi gzugs tshor ba la sogs pa nye bar len pa'i phung po bzhi ni khams gsum pa'i tshor ba la sogs pa'o / / 'dis srid pa gsum du srid pa skye ba'am / / yang srid pa'i las len pas na /
upādānasambhūtatvādupādānavidheyatvād upādānāni vā tebhyaḥ sambhavantītyupādānaskandhāḥ / sneha iva snehaḥ / yathā hi tailādikaḥ sneho vastrādikam āśrayam anupraviśya vyāpnoti mahatāpi cayatnena svāśrayād durvivecyaḥ evaṃ rāgo 'pi svālambanamanupraviśyaiva vyāpnoti mahatāpi ca prayāsena tasmādālambanāt durvivecya iti sneha ucyate / adhyavasānaṃtanmayatā
# sred pa la nye bar len pa zhes bya'o / / nye bar len pa las byung ba dang nye bar len pa la rag lus pa dang de dag las nye bar len pa rnams 'byung bas nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams so / / 'jen pa dang 'dra bas zhen pa ste / / ji ltar 'bru mar la sogs pa'i snum ras la sogs pa'i gnas la zhugs te mched pa shin tu bsgrims kyang rang gi gnas nas dbyung bar dka' ba de bzhin du / / 'dod chags kyang rang gi dmigs pa la zhugs nas mched pa ni 'bad pa chen pos kyang dmigs pa de dang dbral bar dka' bas zhen pa zhes bya'o /
athavā spraṣṭavyaviśeṣo 'pi sneha itivyavacchedārtham āha adhyavasānam iti
# lhag par chags ba ni de'i rang bzhin nyid do / / yang na reg bya'i khyad par la yang snum pa zhes bya ba yod pa de dang rnam par dbye ba'i phyir lhag par chags pa zhes bya ba smos so /
sa punarduḥkhasañjananakarmakaḥ / triduḥkhatāyogādyathāsambhavaṃ traidhātukāḥpañca skandhā duḥkhamabhipretam tasya ca duḥkhasyakāmarūpārūpyatṛṣṇāvaśenābhinirvṛttito rāgasyaduḥkhasañjananaṃ karmanirdiśyate / pratighaḥ katamaḥ
# 'di ni sdug bsngal kun bskyed pa'i las can no / / sdug bsngal nyid gsum dang ldan pa'i phyir ji ltar mthun mthun du khams gsum pa'i phung po lnga ni sdug bsngal du brjod de / / sdug bsngal de yang 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i sred pa'i dbang gis mngon par 'grub pa de'i phyir 'dod chags kyi las ni sdug bsngal kun bskyed par bshad do / / khong khro ba gang zhe na /
m nsattveṣv āghātaity āghātaḥ / sattveṣu rūkṣacittatā yenāviṣṭaḥ sattvānāṃ vadhabandhādikamanarthaṃ cintayati
# sems can rnams la kun nas mnar sems pa'o zhes bya ba la kun nas mnar sems pa ni sems can rnams la sems rtsub pa ste / / des non na sems can rnams la gsod pa dang bcing ba la sogs pa'i gnod pa bya bar sems pa'o /
sa punarasparśavihāraduścaritasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ
# 'di ni reg par mi gnas pa dang nyes par spyod pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
sparśaḥsukham / tena sahito vihāraḥ sparśavihāraḥ
# reg pa ni bde ba ste / / de dang lhan cig gnas pa ni reg par gnas pa'o /
na sparśavihāro'sparśavihāraḥ duḥkhasahita ity arthaḥ / āghātacittasyāvaśyaṃdaurmanasya samudācārāc cittaṃ tapyate
# reg par gnas pa ma yin ba ni reg par mi gnas pa ste / / sdug bsngal dang lhan cig ces bya ba'i tha tshig go / / kun nas mnar sems kyi sems yod na gdon mi za bar yid mi bde ba kun du 'byung ba'i phyir sems la gdung bar 'gyur ro /
cittānuvidhānāc cakāyo 'pi tapyata eveti
# sems kyi rjes su 'gyur ba'i phyir lus la yang gdung bar 'gyur ba nyid de /
sarveryāpatheṣu saduḥkhasavighāto 'syavihāro bhavati
# de ltar de spyod lam thams cad du sdug bsngal dang bcas shing phongs pa dang bcas par gnas par 'gyur ro /
pratihatacittasya ca na kiñcid duścaritaṃ vidūraiti pratigho'sparśavihāraduścaritasanniśrayadānakarmakauktaḥ / mānaḥ katamaḥ
# zhe 'gras pa'i sems dang ldan pa ste / / nyes par spyod pa gang dang yang ring ba ma yin pas khong khro ba ni reg par mi gnas ba dang nyes par spyod pa'i rten byed pa'i las can du bshad do /
sapta mānāiti / māno hi sarva eva
# nga rgyal gang zhe na / / nga rgyal rnam pa bdun te zhes bya ba la /
ssatkāyadṛṣṭisanniśrayeṇa pravartate cittasya connatilakṣaṇaḥ
# nga rgyal ni thams cad kyang 'jig tshogs la lta ba la brten nas 'byung ba'i sems khengs pa'i mtshan nyid de /
tathā hy ātmātmīyabhāvaṃ skandheṣv adhyāropyāyam ahamidaṃ mamety ātmānaṃ tena tena viśeṣeṇonnamayati anyebhyo 'dhikaṃ manyate
# 'di ltar phung po lnga po dag la bdag dang bdag gir dngos por sgro btags nas 'di ni bdag go 'di ni bdag gi'o zhes de dang de'i khyad par gyis bdag khengs shing gzhan dag las lhag par rlom sems pa'o /
saāgauravaduḥkhotpattisanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ
# 'di ni mi gus pa dang sdug bsngal 'byung ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
agauravaṃguruṣu guṇavatsu ca pudgaleṣu stabdhatā kāyavācor apasṛtatā
# mi gus pa ni bla ma rnams dang gang zag yon tan can rnams la 'gying zhing lus dang ngag gi sri zhu med pa'o /
duḥkhotpattiḥpunar atra punarbhavotpattir veditavyā
# sdug bsngal 'byung ba ni 'dir yang srid pa 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
sapunaś cittonnatisvabhāvābhede 'pi cittonnatinimittabhedāt saptadhā bhidyatemāno 'timānaity evamādi
# de ni sems khengs pa'i ngo bo nyid du bye brag med kyang sems khengs pa'i rgyu'i bye brag gis rnam pa bdun du tha dad de /
vhīnāt kulavijñānavittādibhiḥ śreyān asmi / kulavijñānavittādibhir iti yā cittasyonnatiḥsadṛśena vākulādibhis tair eva sadṛśo 'smīti yā cittasyonnatiḥ / sa mānaḥ
# nga rgyal ba dang che ba'i nga rgyal dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o / / rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas dma' ba bas rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas bdag che'o snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'am / / rigs la sogs pas mtshungs pa nyid la de dag dang bdag mtshungs so snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa de ni nga rgyal lo /
atimānaḥ kulavijñānavittādibhiḥsadṛśāt / tyāgaśīlapauruṣādibhiḥ śreyān asmi
# che ba'i nga rgyal ni rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas mtshungs pas gtong ba dang tshul khrims dang nyams rtsal la sogs pas bdag che'o snyam pa'am /
śreyasāvākulavittādibhiḥ sadṛśo 'smi vijñānavittādibhir iti yā
# rigs dang nor la sogs pas che ba la shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas bdag dang mtshungs so snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa ste /
cittasyonnatiḥayam atimāna iti
# 'di ni che ba'i nga rgyal zhes bya'o /
mānātimānaḥ / śreyasaḥ kulavijñānavittair aham eva śreyānkulavijñānavittair iti yā cittasyonnatiḥayaṃ / mānātimānaḥ / asmimānaḥ / pañcopādānaskandhān iti chandarāgau hyatropādānam / anāgatātmabhāvābhilāṣaś chandaḥ
# nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal ni rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas che ba bas kyang rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pas bdag che'o snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa ste / / 'di ni nga rgyal las kyang nga rgyal lo / / nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal ni nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams la zhes bya la / / 'dun pa dang 'dod chags ni nye bar len pa ste / / ma 'ongs pa'i lus 'dod pa ni 'dun pa'o /
vartamānādhyavasānaṃ rāgaḥ
# lhag par chags pa ni 'dod chags so /
tatrānāgatātmabhāvaṃchandamukhenopādatte
# de la ma 'ongs pa'i lus ni 'dun pa'i sgo nas len pa'o /
vartamānaskandhānrāgamukhenāparityāgata upādatte
# da ltar gyi phung po rnams la ni 'dod chags kyi sgo nas yongs su mi gtong bar lan to /
ata etad eva dvayamupādānam ity ucyate
# de'i phyir 'di gnyis ni nye bar len pa zhes bya ste /
tena yuktāḥ skandhā upādānaskandhāḥ
# 'di dag dang ldan pa'i phung po rnams ni nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams so /
teṣūpādānaskandheṣv ātmātmīyarahiteṣv ātmātmīyābhiniveśādyā cittasyonnatirayam asmimānaḥ / abhimāno
# nye bar len pa'i phung po bdag dang bdag gi dang bral ba de dag la bdag dang bdag gir mngon par zhen nas sems khengs pa gang yin pa ni nga'o snyam pa'i nga rgyal lo; / / mngon pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na /
'prāptauttariviśeṣādhigame prāpto mayetiyā cittasyonnatiḥb y / manuṣyadharmārāgadveṣamohādayaḥ tatpravartitaṃ ca kāyavāṅmanaskarma
# gong ma'i khyad par thob par bya ba ma thob par bdag gis thob po snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la mi'i chos ni 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug la sogs pa dang des bskyed pa'i lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las so /
tatpratipakṣabhūtaṃ yad dhyānasamāpattyādikaṃ tanmanuṣyadharmebhya uttariviśeṣa ucyate
# de'i gnyen por gyur pa ni bsam gtan dang snyoms par 'jug pa la sogs pa gang yin pa ste /
tasminviśeṣādhigama'prāptesatiprāpto mayā uttariviśeṣādhigama itiyā cittasyonnatiḥ so 'bhimānaḥ / c dūnamāno
# de dag ni mi'i chos rnams las gong ma'i khyad par zhes bya'o / / de dag thob par bya ba ni rnyed par bya ba'o / / khyad par thob par bya ba rnyed par bya ba de med par bdag gis gong ma'i khyad par thob par bya ba 'thob bo snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa de ni mngon pa'i nga rgyal lo /
ebahvantaraviśiṣṭātkulavidyāvittādibhiralpāntarahīno 'smikulādibhir iti yā / cittasyonnatiḥ
# cung zad snyam pa'i nga rgyal ni rigs dang shes rgya dang nor la sogs pa khyad ches 'phags pa bas rigs la sogs pas bdag cung zad cig gis chung ngo snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o /
yuktaṃ tāvat samena samaḥ samānād vā viśiṣṭaḥ viśiṣṭād vā viśiṣṭa ity unnatisthānatvān mānaḥātmānaṃ tu nyūnaṃ paśyataḥ kim unnatisthānaṃ yatas tasyamāna ucyate
# re zhig mtshungs pa dang mtshungs so snyam pa dang mtshungs pa bas khyad par du 'phags so snyam pa'am / / khyad par can bas kyang 'phags so snyam pa ni khengs pa'i gnas yin pas nga rgyal du rigs na / / bdag chung bar mthong ba khengs pa'i gnas su ci'i phyir 'gyur na 'di ltar de la nga rgyal zhes bya zhe na /
etad evonnatisthānaṃ bahvantaraviśiṣṭādalpāntarahīno 'sminayathābahvantarahīnād iti
# khyad ches 'phags pa bas bdag cung zad gcig gis dma' bar 'dzin gyi ji ltar khyad che ba bzhin du / / dma' bar ni mi 'dzin pa'i phyir de nyid khengs pa'i gnas so /
apica santikecid ye prakṛṣṭe ca sattvarāśau hīnam apy ātmānaṃ bahu manyante / mithyāmāno'guṇavato guṇavān / asmīti yā cittasyonnatiḥ / guṇā / dānaśīlakṣāntyādayaḥ / te yasya na vidyante so 'guṇavān / athavā'guṇā dauḥśīlyādayaḥ
# yang gang dag sems can mchog dam pa'i tshogs kyi nang na bdag dma' bar 'gyur na'ang tha gi'o snyam du sems khengs pa dag kyang yod do / / log pa'i nga rgyal gang zhe na / / yon tan ma yin pa dang ldan pa la bdag yon tan dang ldan no snyam du sems khengs pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la / / yon tan ni sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bzod pa la sogs pa ste / / de dag su la yon tan dang mi ldan pa'o / / yang na yon tan ma yin pa ni 'chal ba'i tshul khrims la sogs pa ste / / su la yod pa de yon tan ma yin pa dang ldan pa'o /
te yasya santi so 'guṇavān / tasmādaguṇavato guṇavān asmi
# de lta bas na yon tan ma yin pa dang ldan pa la bdag yon tan dang ldan no snyam pa'o /
aguṇavata ityanena hidānaśīlādyabhāve guṇavattvam abhyupagataṃ bhavatīty atonirvastukatvān mithyāmāna ucyate / avidyā katamā / karmaphalasatyaratneṣv / ajñānam / sā punaḥ sahajā parikalpitā ca / tatra / sahajānyakleśāsamprayogād āveṇikī / parikalpitāvicikitsāmithyādṛṣṭiśīlavrataparāmarṣādikleśasamprayuktā
# yon tan ma yin pa dang ldan zhes bya ba 'dis ni sbyin pa dang tshul khrims la sogs pa med par yon tan dang ldan pa nyid du khas blangs pa yin te / / de'i phyir dngos po med pas na log pa'i nga rgyal zhes bya'o / / ma rig pa gang zhe na / / las dang 'bras bu dang bden pa dang dkon mchog rnams mi shes pa ste / / de yang lhan cig skyes pa dang kun du brtags pa'o zhes bya ba de la lhan cig skyes pa ni nyon mongs pa gzhan dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin gyi ma 'dres pa'o / / kun brtags pa ni the tshom dang log par lta ba dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'o / / las mi shes pa ni bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang me gyo ba'i las yod par mi shes pa gang yin pa ste / / mi rtogs pa dang khong du mi chud pa'o /
karmaṇy ajñānaṃ puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyakarmāstitve yad ajñānamapratipattir anavabodhaḥ iyaṃ sahajā avidyā
# 'di ni lhan cig skyes pa'i ma rig pa'o / / bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i las yod pa nyid la the tshom za ba'am /
puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyakarmāstitve vicikitsato vāpavadato vā nāstipuṇyam apuṇyam āniñjyaṃ cetipaśubandhāgnipraveśādinivartane puṇye'puṇyasañjñināmpaśubandhāgnipraveśādike vāpuṇye puṇyasañjñināṃ yāvicikitsāmithyādṛṣṭisamprayuktā avidyā sā parikalpitā / sādharmeṣSumithyāniścayavicikitsāsaṅkleśotpattisanniśrayadānakarmikā
# bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i las med do zhes skur pa 'debs pa dang bsod nams la bsod nams ma yin par 'du shes pa rnams / / phyugs gsod cing mer 'jug pa la sogs pa byed pa dang bsod nams ma yin pa la bsod nams su 'du shes pa rnams phyugs gsod cing mer 'jug par byed pa dang the tshom za ba dang log par lta ba dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i ma rig pa gang yin pa de ni / / kun du brtags pa'o / / 'di ni chos rnams la log par nges pa dang the tshom dang kun nas nyon mongs pa 'byung ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / rtog pa'i bdag nyid kyi shes rab ni lta ba zhes bya ste /
prajñā nitīrikātmikā dṛṣṭir ucyata ity atolaukikīsaṃyagdṛṣṭyādiprasaṅge dṛṣṭir iti satkāyadṛṣṭyādikāḥpañca dṛṣṭaya ihābhipretā iti pradarśann āha pañca / dṛṣṭaya iti
# de'i phyir 'jig rten pa'i yang dag par lta ba la sogs pa la yang lta ba thal bar 'gyur bas / / 'dir ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba la sogs pa lta ba lnga la bya bar bzhed par bstan pa'i phyir / / lta ba lnga ste zhes bya ba smos so /
tāsāṃkliṣṭatvāviśeṣe 'py ālambanākārabhedādbhedapradarśanārthaṃ punar apy āha satkāyadṛṣṭirantagrāhadṛṣṭir iti vistaraḥ / nsīdatīti sat / cayaḥ kāyaḥ
# de dag kyang nyon mongs pa can nyid du bye brag med kyang dmigs pa dang rnam pa'i bye brag gis tha dad par bstan pa'i phyir / / 'jig tshogs la lta ba zhes bya ba rgya cher smos so /
vinaśvare saṅghāteiyaṃ dṛṣṭir / nātmani nātmīye ceti jñāpitaṃ bhavati
# 'jig par 'gyur bas 'jig pa'o / / bsags pas tshogs te / / 'jig pa'i ngang can mang po la lta ba 'di ni bdag dang bdag gi ba med par ming nyid kyis bstan pa yin te /
ātmā hi nityaś caikaś cātmavādibhir abhyupagamyate / iyaṃ cānityānekaviṣayatvānnātmaviṣayety uktaṃ bhavati
# bdag ni rtag pa dang; gcig pu yin par bdag tu smra ba rnams khas len la / / 'di ni mi rtag pa dang du ma'i yul du gyur pa'i phyir bdag yul ma yin par bstan pa yin no /
pañcopādānaskandhānityādi ye kecic chramaṇā vā brāhmaṇā vā ātmānam ātmīyaṃveti samanupaśyantaḥ samanupaśyanti ta imān eva pañcopādānaskandhāniti sūtra uktam / te hi svarūpataḥ kāryato vā ātmānaṃ prajñapayeyuḥ / sāṅkhyāś caitanyasvarūpamātmānaṃ manyante
# nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams la zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni dge sbyong ngam bram ze gang la la dag bdag dang bdag gis rjes su lta bas rjes su lta ba dag ni nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po 'di dag la'o zhes mdo las gsungs so / / de dag gis kyang rang gi ngo bor ram / / 'bras bu'i sgo nas bdag tu 'dogs grang na / / grangs can rnams ni bdag shes pa yod pa'i rang gi ngo bo yin par sems te /
te ca cittacaitasikaprabhede 'vidvāṃsaḥsakalaṃ cittacaitasikakalāpam eva caitanyam ity āhuḥ / atas tecaturaḥskandhān ātmeti pratipannāḥ rūpaskandhamātmīyatvena
# de dag kyang sems dang sems las byung ba'i rab tu dbye ba la mi mkhas pas sems dang sems las byung ba'i tshogs nyid kyi spyir shes pa yod pa zhes zer te / / de'i phyir de dag gi phung po bzhi la ni bdag yin pa dang gzugs kyi phung po la ni bdag gi yin par rtogs so /
na ca buddhivṛttito 'nyac caitanyaṃ svasthacittenaśakyate vaktuṃ pratipattum vā
# blo'i 'jug pa ma gtogs par shes pa yod pa gzhan zhig yod par ni sems kyi nyams tha mal pas brjod pa'am rtogs par mi nus so /
evam vedanādīnām
# tshor ba la sogs pa yang de bzhin no /
ekeṣāṃca nirgranthānāṃ jñānasvarūpa ātmeti teṣām ātmātmīyagrāho'nantaroktaeva draṣṭavyaḥ / vaiśeṣikādayas tu kāryata ātmānaṃvyapadiśanti / yaḥ paśyati yāvan manyate tathā yo vedayateānāti smarati cetayate vijānāti ca sa ātmeti
# gcar bu pa kha cig ni shes pa'i rang gi ngo bo bdag yin no zhes zer te / / de dag gi bdag dang bdag gir 'dzin pa yang gong du bshad pa bzhin du blta bar bya'o / / bye brag pa la sogs pa ni lta ba nas sems pa'i bar gang yin pa dang de bzhin du tshor bar byed pa dang 'dus te shes par byed pa dang dran par byed pa dang sems par byed pa dang rnam par shes par byed pa gang yin pa de dag yin no zhes 'bras bu'i sgo nas bdag tu ston to /
teṣām apicakṣurādiṣv evātmābhimānaḥ
# de dag kyang mig la sogs pa nyid la bdag tu mngon pa'i nga rgyal byed de /
yasmāc cakṣurvyatirikto yaḥpaśyati tasyābhāvaḥ
# ji ltar de med pa'i phyir mig ma gtogs par lta ba gzhan ni med do /
cakṣurvijñāne hi darśanasamākhyā
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la mthong ba la sogs pa zhes bya ste /
tasyāsādharaṇakāraṇatvāc cakṣuḥ paśyatīti vyapadiśyate
# de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir mig gis mthong ngo zhes ston to /
tadyathā nādasyāsādhāraṇakāraṇatvād ghaṇṭā rautīty ucyate
# dper na sgra'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rgyu yin pas dril bu 'khrol lo zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
yatra tarhicakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvā naiva sumanā bhavati naivadurmanāiti tatra katham / tatrāpi yatrātmaprajñaptiḥ samūhesantāne vā sa eva cakṣuṣā rūpāṇi dṛṣṭvety ucyate
# 'o na gang las mig gis gzugs mthong yang yid dga' bar yang mi 'gyur / / yid mi dga' bar yang mi 'gyur zhes 'byung ba de la ji skad bya / / der yang 'dus pa'am rgyud gang la bdag gdags pa de nyid la mig gis gzugs rnams mthong ngo zhes bya'o /
rūpanirbhāsataiva hi rūpadarśanam yasmāt tadbhāvābhāverūpasya darśanādarśane vyavasthāpyete
# gzugs su snang ba nyid la gzugs mthong ngo zhes bya ste / / 'di ltar de yod pa dang med pa la gzugs mthong ba dang mi mthong bar rnam par gzhag go /
evaṃ śravaṇādiṣv apivaktavyam
# thos pa la sogs pa la yang de bzhin du brjod par bya'o /
yatra tūktaṃ vedayata iti vedanā evaṃ yāvad vijānātīti vijñānam / tatra bhāvamātre kartṛvyapadeśaḥvijñānavyatiriktavijñātṛpratiṣedhārtham
# gang nas tshor bar byed pas tshor ba zhes bya ba nas / / de bzhin du rnam par shes par byed pas rnam par shes pa zhes 'byung ba der yang rnam par shes pa ma gtogs par rnam par shes pa po dgag pa'i phyir dngos po tsam la byed pa por bstan to /
evaṃ vedanādiṣv apivaktavyam
# tshor ba la sogs pa la yang de bzhin du brjod par bya'o /
atha vā viṣayanirbhāsatām upādāya kartṛvyapadeśaḥ yathoktaṃ prāk
# yang na ji ltar gong du bstan pa bzhin du yul du snang ba'i phyir byed pa por bstan to /
na cātmalābhavyatiriktākriyā vidyate kṣaṇikatvāt sarvabhāvānāṃ kriyākāle'navasthānāt
# dngos po thams cad ni skad cig ma yin pas byed pa'i dus na mi gnas pa'i phyir bdag thob pa ma gtogs par byed pa gzhan med do /
na cākartṛkā kriyāsti
# byed pa po med par ni bya ba med do /
ātmalābhānantaraṃ cabhāvānāṃ nirhetukatvād yadi vināśo na syāt paścād api nasyāt vinaṣṭur vināśasya ca paścād ātmātiśayābhāvāt
# dngos po rnams bdag thob ma thag tu gal te 'jig par mi 'gyur na ni rgyu med pa'i phyir phyis kyang 'jig par mi 'gyur te / / 'jig pa po dang 'jig pa ni phyis kyang rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa med pa'i phyir ro /
sahetukavināśaparikalpe ca vinaṣṭaiva tadvyatirikto vāvināśahetuḥ parikalpyeta
# 'jig pa rgyu dang bcas pas yongs su rtog na yang 'jig pa po nyid dam / / de las gzhan pa zhig 'jig pa'i rgyur yongs su brtag grang na /
pūrvasmin pakṣaātmalābhānantaraṃbhāvānāṃ vināśaḥ naiva vāsti vināśa iti prasajyate / yo 'nyanirapekṣaḥ pūrvaṃ yasya na kāraṇam sa paścād api tasyanaiva kāraṇam ātmātiśayābhāvāt / itarasminn api pakṣe vināśānāṃ kāraṇaniyamo na syāt / kāryāṇām iva tadvināśānāmapi kāraṇaniyamo bhaviṣyati
# phyogs snga ma ltar na ni dngos po rnams bdag thob ma thag tu 'jig pa'am / / 'jig pa med par thal bar 'gyur te / / gang gzhan la mi ltos pa de ni sngar gang gi rgyur ma gyur pa de rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa med pas phyis kyang de'i rgyur mi 'gyur ba nyid do / / phyogs cig shos ltar na yang 'jig pa'i rgyu nges pa med par 'gyur ro / / 'bras bu bzhin du 'jig pa rnams kyi rgyu la yang nges pa yod do zhe na /
naitad evam kāryāṇāṃ hiparasparato bhinnasvarūpatvāt tatkāraṇānām api śaktibhedātniyamo na virudhyate
# de ni de lta ma yin te / / 'bras bu rnams ni phan tshun tha dad pa'i rang gi ngo bo yin pas de dag gi rgyu rnams kyi nus pa yang tha dad pa nges pa yod par 'gal ba med kyi /
vināśānāṃ tu nirupākhyatvādātmātiśayābhāve kiṅkṛto 'yaṃ niyamaḥ
# 'jig pa ni dngos por brjod pa med pas rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur ba med na nges pa 'di sus byas /
tasmāt sarvaṃ vāvināśakāraṇaṃ sarvavināśasya naiva vā vināśakāraṇam astītipratipattavyam
# de lta bas na 'jig pa thams cad kyi rgyu thams cad yin pa'am / / 'jig pa la rgyu med pa zhig tu shes par bya'o /
vināśaś ca yadi vināśakāraṇāt pūrvam apy astievaṃ sati vināśakāraṇavaiyarthyaṃ prasajyeta / bhāvānāṃ cavināśe saty utpattir iti vinaṣṭānām apy utpattiprasaṅgaḥ
# yang gal te 'jig pa 'jig pa'i rgyu'i snga rol na yod pa de ltar na ni 'jig pa'i rgyu don med pa dang dngos po rnams kyang zhig bzhin du skye bas zhig zin pa rnams skye bar thal bar 'gyur ro /
athavināśakāraṇebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ na vidyate evaṃ sati bhāvavadabhāvasyāpiprāgabhāvaḥ prajyate / yasya ca prāgabhāvaḥtasyacāvaśyaṃ bhāvatvāt pradhvaṃsābhāvenāpi bhavitavyam
# ji ste 'jig pa 'jig pa'i rgyu rnams kyi snga rol na med na de lta na yang dngos po bzhin du dngos po med pa yang snga na med par thal bar 'gyur ro / / gang la snga na med pa yod pa de ni gdon mi za bar dngos po yin pa'i phyir zhig nas med par yang 'gyur ro /
evaṃ bhāvābhāvayor aviśeṣāt sarvaṃ bhāvātmakamabhāvātmakam vā prasajyeta / yadi ca pradhvaṃsābhāvasyāpipradhvaṃsābhāvaḥ evaṃ pradhvaṃsābhāvānām anavasthānāttatkāraṇānām api neṣyateevaṃ satibhāvapradhvaṃsābhāvasyāpi naiveṣṭavyā dvayor apyātmātiśayatvābhāvāt / kriyā ca bhāvebhyo 'nyā 'nanyā vāparikalpyeta / yady ananyā ātmaivātmanaḥ kartā karma ceti nayujyate
# de ltar na dngos po dang dngos po med pa gnyis khyad par med pa'i phyir thams cad dngos po'i bdag nyid dam dngos po med ba'i bdag nyid du thal bar 'gyur ro / / ji ste zhig nas med pa yang zhig nas med par 'gyur na / / de lta na ni zhig nas med pa rnams thug pa med par 'gyur ba'i phyir de'i rgyu rnams kyang 'gyur ro / / de ltar mi 'dod na ni gnyi ga yang rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa med pa'i phyir dngos po zhig nas med par yang 'dod par mi bya'o / / bya ba yang dngos po las gzhan nam gzhan ma yin par brtag grang na / / gal te gzhan ma yin na ni bdag nyid kyi byed pa bo dang las su mi rigs so /
yadi ca labdhātmakaḥ kriyāṃ karoti nāsautasyātmabhūtā / yo hi yena vināpi bhavati na sa tasyātmabhūtoyujyate / kriyāśūnye ca kartṛtvaṃ na yujyate / kriyārahitāc cakriyādhyāsito 'nya eveti kathaṃ kartuḥ karmaṇo vātmabhūtākriyā
# gal te bdag thob nas bya ba byed na de ni de'i bdag nyid du gyur pa ma yin te / / gang zhig gang med par 'byung ba de ni de'i bdag nyid du gyur par mi rung ngo / / bya bas stong na yang byed pa por mi rung ngo / / bya ba dang bral ba ni bya ba dang ldan pa las gzhan nyid yin na bya ba byed pa po'am /
kriyārahitatadadhyāsitayoś ca yaugapadyādarśanātpūrvavināśa uttarasyotpādo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ
# las kyi bdag nyid du ji ltar 'gyur / / bya ba dang bral ba dang de dang ldan pa gnyis cig car du ma mthong ba'i phyir snga ma 'jig la phyi ma skye bar khas blang bar bya'o /
athālabdhātmakaḥ evam api tasya kartṛtvaṃ kriyāyāś catadātmabhūtatvaṃ na yujyate dvayor apy asattvāt
# ji ste bdag ma thob na de ltar na yang byed pa po dang bya ba yang de'i bdag nyid du 'gyur bar mi rung ste /
kiṃcaikasya kriyārahitatvāt dvitīyasya kriyādhyāsitatvātkartṛtvābhāvaḥ kartur abhāvāc ca kriyāyā apy abhāva itievaṃ ca svarasavināśāt kṣaṇikatvam evābhyupagataṃ bhavati
# gnyi ga med pa'i phyir ci yang ma yin no / / gzhan yang gcig ni bya ba dang bral ba yin la cig shos ni bya ba dang ldan pa'i phyir byed pa po med do / / byed pa po med na bya ba yang med do / / de ltar na rang gi ngang gis 'jig pa'i phyir skad cig pa nyid du khas blang ba yin no /
kartṛkarmaṇor anyāpi kriyā naivāsti / kārakair hi kriyā janyate / janyatvāc ca karmaiva bhavati / na ca niḥkriyaṃ karma kartā vāyujyata ity avaśyaṃ tatrānyayā kriyayā bhavitavyam / tatrāpyanyayety anavasthā kriyāṇāṃkartṝṇāṃ ca
# byed pa po dang las gnyis las bya ba gud na yang med de / / byed pa po rnams kyis bya ba skyed la / / bskyed par bya ba yin pas na las nyid yin no / / bya ba med par yang las dang byed pa bor mi rung ste / / gdon mi za bar der bya ba gzhan yong par 'gyur ro / / de la yang gzhan yod par 'gyur bas bya ba dang byed pa po rnams thug pa med par 'gyur ro /
atha kriyākriyāntarām anapekṣā janyate / evaṃ tarhi dravyam eva kriyāntararahitaṃ janyatvena kiṃ neṣyate / kimarthāntarabhūtayādṛṣṭasvarūpasāmarthyayā kriyayāparikalpitayā
# ji ste bya ba gzhan la mi ltos par bya ba skyed do zhe na / / de lta na ni bya ba gzhan dang bral ba'i rdzas nyid skyed par ci'i phyir mi 'dod la / / don gzhan du gyur pa rang gi ngo bo dang nus pa yang ma mthong ba'i bya ba yongs su brtags pas ci zhig bya /
yadi ca kriyā kārakair janyate nadravyam
# gal te yang byed pa po rnams kyis bya ba bskyed kyi rdzas ni ma yin na /
evaṃ prākpradhvaṃsābhāvau kriyāyā eva na dravyasyetisarvadravyāṇi nityāni naiva vā santīty abhyupeyam
# de lta na ni snga na med pa dang zhig nas med pa gnyis bya ba la yod kyi rdzas la med par 'gyur te / / rdzas thams cad ni rtag pa'am med pa nyid du khas blang bar bya'o /
yadi cakārakebhyo 'nyā kriyā kriyārahitaṃ casādhanam evaṃkriyāṇām anavasthānaṃ sādhanābhāvo vā / sādhanābhāvāc cakriyābhāvo 'pi
# gal te yang byed pa po rnams las bya ba gzhan zhig yin na sgrub pa bya ba dang bral bar 'gyur te / / de lta na ni bya ba la thug pa med pa dang sgrub pa yang med par 'gyur ro / / sgrub pa med pa'i phyir bya ba yang med par 'gyur te /
na hy asādhanā kriyāsti
# sgrub ba med na bya ba med do /
yadi ca gantur anyāgatiḥ taṇḍulebhyo 'nyā paciḥ evaṃ sati gantur nadeśāntaraprāptiḥ taṇḍulānām vāpacanaṃpūrvāvasthāto'vikṛtatvāt / atha kriyaiva svāśrayasya vikārahetur itipūrvāvasthāto vikṛtatvam apratiṣiddham / vikāro hi pūrvasmādātmātiśayaḥ / sa cānyatvāvinābhāvī
# yang gal te 'gro ba po las 'gro ba gzhan pa dang 'bras rnams las tshos pa gzhan du gyur na / / de lta na ni sngon gyi gnas las 'gyur ba med pa'i phyir 'gro ba po yul gzhan du phyin pa med pa dang 'bras kyang gnas pa med par 'gyur ro / / ji ste yang bya ba nyid rang gi gzhir 'gyur ba'i rgyu yin pas sngon gyi gnas las 'gyur ba ma bkag go zhe na / / 'gyur ba zhes bya ba ni sngon las rang bzhin bye brag tu 'gyur ba yin la / / de yang gzhan du 'gyur ba med par mi 'byung ste /
tasmād avaśyaṃpūrvottarayor yaugapadyābhāvāt pūrvavināśenābhinnakālaṃuttarasyotpādo 'bhyupagantavyaḥ
# de lta bas na snga ma dang phyi ma gnyis cig car yod pa ma yin pas gdon mi za bar sngar zhig la dus tha dad pa med par phyi ma skye bar khas blang bar bya'o /
evaṃ kriyāyā āśrayābhāvādanavasthitatvāt kuto vikārahetutvam
# de ltar na bya gzhi med pa dang mi gnas pa'i phyir 'gyur ba'i rgyur ga la 'gyur /
tasmādātmalābhānantaravināśeṣu nirīheṣv antarvyāpārapuruṣarahiteṣupañcasūpādānaskandheṣv eva sadbhāvamātreṇaprāgabhūtānām anyeṣāṃ skandhānāṃ hetubhāvenavyavasthiteṣu nityakartṛbhoktṛgrāhapūrvako 'yamātmātmīyagrāhaḥ nātmany ātmīye ceti
# de lta bas na bdag thob ma thag tu 'jig pa can gyo ba med pa nang na byed pa'i skyes bu med par nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po nyid yod pa tsam gyis snga ma med pa'i phung po gzhan rnams la rtag pa dang byed pa po dang za ba por 'dzin pa sngon du btang ba'i bdag dang bdag gir 'dzin gyi /
ātmataātmīyatocety antagrāhadṛṣṭito vyavacchinatti
# 'di bdag dang bdag gi la ni ma yin no / / bdag dang bdag gir zhes bya ba ni mthar 'dzin pa'i lta ba rnam par gcod pa'o /
tsamanupaśyataiti niścinvataḥ / yā kliṣṭā prajñeti / na hy amūḍhasyānātmany ātmeti jñānaṃ bhavati
# yang dag par rjes su lta ba zhes bya ba ni rnam par 'byed pa'o / / shes rab nyon mongs pa can gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni rmongs par ma gyur na / / bdag med pa la bdag tu 'du shes par mi 'gyur te /
atomohasamprayogād viparyastatvāc ca kliṣṭā / tatra svasantatipatitān ātmatvena samanupaśyati parasantatipatitāanupāttāṃś cātmīyatvena / yadāpi svasantatipatitānāmekadeśam ātmatvena tadā itarān apy ātmīyatvena
# de'i phyir gti mug dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang phyin ci log tu gyur ba'i phyir nyon mongs pa can no / / de la rang gi rgyud du gyur pa rnams la ni bdag tu yang dag par rjes su lta / / gzhan gyi rgyud du gyur pa dang ma zin pa rnams la ni bdag gir yang dag par rjes su lta'o / / gang gi tshe bdag gi rgyun du gyur pa rnams kyi phyogs gcig la bdag tu lta ba'i tshe gzhan la ni bdag gir lta'o /
iyaṃ casarvadṛṣṭigatasanniśrayadānakarmikā
# 'di ni lta ba thams cad kyi rten byed pa'i las can no /
tām evādhipatiṃ kṛtvetisatkāyadṛṣṭim
# de nyid kyi dbang du byas nas zhes bya ba ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba ste /
