satkāyadṛṣṭibalena tadutpatteḥ satkāyadṛṣṭis tasyā adhipatiḥ
# 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i stobs kyis de'i 'byung ba'i phyir 'jig tshogs la lta ba ni de la dbang byed do /
śāśvatata ucchedato veti / yat satkāyadṛṣṭyātmatvena / vastv ālambitam tad eva śāśvatata iti nityataḥ ucchedata ityucchedo 'trāpratisandhiko vināśaḥ
# rtag pa'am chad pa zhes bya ba ni 'jig tshogs la lta bas dngos po gang la bdag tu dmigs pa de nyid la ste / / rtag pa ni ther zug go / / chad pa zhes bya ba la chad pa ni 'dir nying mtshams sbyor ba med par 'jig pa'o /
samanupaśyato yākliṣṭā prajñeti pūrvavad vācyam
# yang dag par rjes su lta ba'i shes rab nyon mongs pa can gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni snga ma bzhin du brjod par bya'o /
iyaṃ ca madhyamāpratipanniryāṇaparipanthakarmikā / madhyamāpratipac chāśvatocchedagrāhavarjitaṃpratītyasamutpādajñānaṃ / hetum vāpavadataḥ phalaṃ vā kriyāṃ vā
# 'di ni dbu ma'i lam gyi nges par 'byung ba'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no / / dbu ma'i lam ni rtag pa dang chad par 'dzin pa spangs nas rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba shes pa'o /
sad vā vastu nāśayataityādi / sucaritādikamsugatidurgatī mātādikriyām arhadādikaṃ ca yathākramaṃhetv ādik a ṃ / kuśalamūlasamucchedakarmikākuśalamūladṛḍhatāsanniśrayadānakarmikāceyam / sā tu viśiṣṭaiva na sarvā
# rgyu'am 'bras bu'am byed pa la skur pa 'debs pa dang yod pa'i dngos po 'jig pa ste zhes bya ba la sogs pa de yang khyad par can la bya'i / / thams cad la ni ma yin no / / 'di ni dge ba'i rtsa ba gcod pa'i las can dang mi dge / / ba'i rtsa ba dam du 'dzin pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ katamaiti dṛṣṭyādīn / paratvenāmṛśatīti dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ
# lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba ni lta ba la sogs pa la dam par 'dzin pas lta ba mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
tām eva catrividhāṃ dṛṣṭim itisatkāyadṛṣṭim antagrāhadṛṣṭiṃmithyādṛṣṭiṃ ca / tadāśrayāṃśca skandhāniti
# lta ba rnam pa gsum po de dag nyid ces bya ba ni 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba dang; log par lta ba'o zhes bya ba ni lta ba po'i lus zhes bya ba gang yin pa dag ste /
ye / draṣṭur ātmabhāvasaṃśabditāḥ yān āśritya dṛṣṭayaḥpravartantete tadāśrayāagrataḥ śreṣṭhatoviśiṣṭataḥ paramataity ete 'grādayaḥ śabdās tulyārthā / apy uttarottaravyākhyānatvenopāttāḥ / ayaṃāsad dṛṣṭ yabhi nive śasa nniśrayadān akar maka ḥ
# gang dag la brten nas lta ba rnams 'byung ba'o / / de'i gnas la mchog dang gtso bo dang khyad par du 'phags pa dang dam pa zhes bya ba ni mchog la sogs pa'i sgra de dag don mtshungs mod kyi / / gcig gis gcig bshad pa'i phyir smos so / / 'di ni lta ba ngan pa la mngon par zhen pa'i rten byed pa'i las can te /
dṛṣṭilakṣaṇasyābhiniveśasya guṇarūpeṇa grahaṇāttadaparityāgamukhena sarvadṛṣṭīnām ayaṃ sanniśraya ityuktaṃ bhavati
# lta ba'i mtshan nyid la mngon par zhen pa yon tan gyi ngo bor 'dzin pas de yongs su mi gtong ba'i sgro nas 'di ni lta ba thams cad kyi rten byed par bshad pa yin no; /
śīlaṃ vrataṃ tadāśrayāṃśca skandhān iti
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs dang de'i gnas phung po rnams la zhes bya ba la /
dauḥśīlyaviratiḥ śīlam veśavṛttakāyavākpravṛttirniyamo vratam
# 'chal ba'i tshul khrims spong ba ni tshul khrims so / / cha byad dang tshul dang lus dang ngag gi 'jug pa nges par byed pa ni brtul zhugs so /
yān āśritya skandhāñchīlaṃ vrataṃ vā pravartate te śīlavratāśrayāḥ skandhāḥ
# phung po gang dag la brten nas tshul khrims sam brtul zhugs 'byung ba'i phung po de dag tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs kyi gnas so /
kutsitāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ guṇato gṛhītvātatpūrvakaṃ śīlaṃ vrataṃ vā paratvenāmṛśatītiśīlavrataparāmarśaḥ
# lta ba ngan pa la yon tan du bzung nas de mngon du 'gro ba'i tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs la dam par 'dzin pa ni tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
ata eva śīlavrataparāmarśāddṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ pūrva uktaḥ
# de'i phyir tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pas mchog tu 'dzin pa sngar bshad do /
śudhyate 'nena vā pāpācayanāt?? śīlena vratena ceti śuddhiḥ
# tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs 'dis sdig pa'i dri ma sel zhing dag par byed pas dag pa'o /
mucyate 'nena kleśabandhād itimuktiḥ
# 'dis nyon mongs pa'i 'ching ba las grol bar byed pas grol ba'o /
niryāty anena saṃsārād iti niryāṇam
# 'dis 'khor ba las nges par 'byin par byed pas nges par 'byung ba'o /
niryāṇam evanairyāṇiko mokṣamārga ity arthaḥ / samanupaśyata / iti nirūpayataḥ
# nges par 'byin pa ni thar pa'i lam zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / yang dag par rjes su lta ba zhes bya ba ni rtog pa'o /
śīle vrate vā śuddhyādyākārair abhiniveśātmikāprajñā śīlavrataparāmarśaḥ
# tshul khrims sam brtul zhugs bdag po la sogs pa'i rnam par mngon par zhen pa'i bdag nyid kyi shes rab ni tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
kliṣṭā tu viparītālambanatvāt
# nyon mongs pa can ni phyin ci log tu dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
ayaṃ caśramavaiphalyasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / vicikitsā katamā
# 'di ni ngal ba 'bras bu med pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / the tshom gang zhe na /
satyādiṣu yā vimatiriti / ādiśabdena karmaphalaratnāni gṛhyante / dvidhā matir vimatiḥ syān na syād iti
# bden pa la sogs pa la gang yin gnyis za ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa zhes bya bas ni las dang 'bras bu dang dkon mchog rnams bsdu'o / / yin nam ma yin zhes som nyi yod pa ni yid gnyis za ba'o /
prajñātaś ceyaṃ jātyantaram evadraṣṭavyā / sākuśalapakṣāpravṛttisanniśrayadānakarmikā
# 'di shes rab las rang bzhin tha dad par blta bar bya ste / / 'di ni dge ba'i phyogs la mi 'jug pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
kleśānāṃ ca rāgādīnāṃ kati parikalpitā eva kati sahajāḥparikalpitāś cety āha tisro dṛṣṭayaḥparikalpitāḥ
# 'dod chags la sogs pa'i nyon mongs pa rnams la du zhig ni kun du brtags pa kho na yin / / du zhig lhan cig skyes pa dang kun du brtags pa yin zhe na /
eveti / tās tu pūrvā api santīty ata āha paścimā iti
# lta ba gsum po de dag ni gong ma la yang 'gol bas de'i phyir 'og ma zhes bya ba smos so /
tāḥ punarmithyādṛṣṭir dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaś ca
# de dag kyang log par lta ba dang lta ba la mchog tu 'dzin pa dang tshul khrims dang brtul zhugs mchog tu 'dzin pa'o /
nakevalam etā eva parikalpitāḥ kiṃ tarhi vicikitsā caparikalpitā
# 'di dag nyi tshe kun du brtags pa yin par ma zad kyi / / the tshom yang kun du brtags pa'o /
śeṣāḥ sahajāḥ parikalpitāś cetyubhayathā / ke punaḥ śeṣāḥ / rāgapratighamānāvidyāḥsatkāyadṛṣṭir antagrāhadṛṣṭiś ca / uktāḥ kleśāḥ upakleśā vaktavyāḥ / ta ucyante / vartamānaṃpratyutpannam nānāgatam atītam vā / qapakāram āgamyety apakāraṃ gṛhītvety anenakrodhasya viṣayaṃ nirūpayati / krodho hy apakāravastuny evavartamāna eva pravartate nānyatreti / cetasaāghātaity
# lhag ma ni lhan cig skyes pa dang kun du brtags pa'o zhes bya ba ni gnyi ga'o / / lhag ma rnams gang zhe na / / 'dod chags dang khong khro ba dang gti mug dang nga rgyal rnams dang 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang mthar 'dzin par lta ba'o / / nyon mongs pa rnams bshad zin to / / nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams brjod dgos pas de dag bshad par bya'o / / 'phral du zhes bya ba ni da ltar byung ba la bya ste / / ma 'ongs pa dang 'das pa la ni ma yin no / / gnod par byed pa la gnas te zhes bya ba ni gnod par byed pa gzung ste / / 'dis ni khro bo'i yul bstan to / / khro bo ni de ltar nyid gnod par byed pa'i dngos po la 'jug gi / / gzhan du ni ma yin no /
atrāpi vijñānasambandhitvaṃ svarūpaṃ ca nirūpitam
# sems kyi kun nas mnar sems pa'o zhes bya ba 'dis ni rnam par shes pa dang 'brel ba can dang rang gi ngo bo yang bstan to /
ayaṃ cāghātasvarūpatvāt pratighān na bhidyate kiṃ tarhi pratighāṃśika eva pratighasyāṃśe viśeṣe prajñaptatvāt
# 'di ni kun nas mnar sems pa'i rang bzhin yin pas khong khro ba dang tha dad pa ma yin mod kyi / / 'di ni khong khro ba'i cha'i khyad par la btags pa'i phyir khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa nyid de /
vartamānam apakāram adhikṛtya yaś cetasa āghātaḥsattvāsattvaviṣayodaṇḍādānādisanniśrayadānakarmakaśca sakrodha iti prajñapyate
# 'phral du gnod par byed pa'i dbang du byas nas sems can dang sems can ma yin pa'i yul la sems kyi kun nas mnar sems pa'o / / dbyug pa len pa la sogs pa'i rten byed pa'i las can gang yin pa de khro ba zhes gdags so /
krodhād ūrdhvaṃ mamānenedam apakṛtam ity etasya vairātmakasyāśayasyānubandho 'nutsargaḥ / prabandhena pravartanam upanāhaḥ / akṣāntisanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / akṣāntir apakārāmarṣaṇaṃpratyapakāracikīrṣety arthaḥ
# khros pa'i 'og tu 'dis bdag la gnod pa 'di byas so zhes shar gnyer ba'i bdag nyid de'i mdud par 'dzin pa mi gtong bar rgyun du 'byung pa ni kho na du 'dzin pa ste / / mi bzod pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / mi bzod pa ni gnod par byed pa la ji mi snyam par mi byed kyi / / phyir gnod pa byed 'dod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
ayaṃ ca krodhavatpradveṣāvasthāviśeṣe prajñapyata iti prajñaptisan veditavyaḥ
# 'di yang khro ba bzhin du zhe sdang gi gnas kyi khyad par la btags pa yin pas btags pa'i yod par rig par bya'o /
chandadveṣabhayādīṃs tiraskṛtya kāle taddhitaiṣiṇā codakenatvam evaṅkārīty anuyuktasyamohāṃśikyavadyapracchādanāmrakṣaḥ / mohāṃśikatvaṃ tu / mrak ṣasy āvac chād anāk ārat vāt
# 'chags pa ni 'dun pa dang zhe sdang dang 'jigs ba la sog pa bsal te / / de la phan par 'dod pa'i gleng bar byed pas dus su khyod 'di lta bu byed pa'o zhes bsnyad pa la gti mug gi char gtogs pas kha na ma thob ma khyud pa'o / / 'chab pa ni kha na ma tho ba mkhyud pa'i rnam pa yin pas gti mug gi char gtogs pa nyid de /
kaukṛtyāsparśavihārasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / dharmataiṣāyad avadyaṃ pracchādayataḥ kaukṛtyam
# 'di ni 'gyod pa dang reg par mi gnas pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / 'di ni chos nyid yin te / / 'di ltar kha na ma tho ba mkhyud na 'gyod par 'gyur ro /
kaukṛtyāc cāvaśyaṃdaurmanasyenasamprayogād asparśavihāra iti / caṇḍaṃ vacaḥ pragāḍhaṃ pāruṣyaṃ marmaghaṭṭanayogena / daśanaśīlo dāśī / tadbhāvo dāśitā / ayaṃ ca bhāvapratyayaḥsvārthikaḥ / caṇḍena vacasā pradaśatīti caṇḍavacodāśitā
# 'gyod na gdon mi za bar yid mi bde ba dang mtshungs par ldan par 'gyur bas reg par mi gnas so / / tshig brlang po zhes bya ba ni mtshang 'bru ba'i tshul gyis zhe gcod pa dang tshig rtsub po zher 'debs par byed pa'i ngang tshul ni zher 'debs pa ste / / de'i dngos po ni zher 'debs pa nyid do / / tshig brlang pos za ba dang 'dra bar tshig brlang por zher 'debs pa nyid ni 'tshig pa'o /
pradāśaḥ / ayaṃ cakrodhopanāhapūrvaṅgamaś cetasaāghātasvabhāva iti pratighāṃśikaeveti na dravyato vidyate
# 'di yang khro ba dang kho na du 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba sems kyi kun nas mnar sems pa'i rang bzhin yin pas khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa nyid de / / rdzas su yod pa ni ma yin no /
ayaṃ cavāgduścaritaprasavanakarmakaḥasparśavihārakarmakaśca / tadvataḥ pudgalasyaduḥsaṃvāsatvāt
# 'di ni ngag gi nyes par sbyong ba skyed pa'i las can dang reg par mi gnas pa'i las can te de dang ldan pa'i gang zag dang 'grogs par dka' ba'i phyir ro /
ābhasatkārakulaśīlaśrutādīn guṇān upalabhya dveṣāṃśikaś hcetaso vyāroṣa īrṣyā / svam āśayaṃ vyāpya roṣo
# phrag dog ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang tshigs su bcad pa dang rigs dang tshul khrims dang thos pa la sogs pa'i yon tan mthong nas zhe sdang gi char mngon par gtogs pa'i sems khong nas 'khrugs pa ste /
vyāroṣaḥ / daurmanasyasamprayogāt tatpūrvakaścāsparśavihāra itidaurmanasyāsparśavihārakarmikā
# rang gi bsam pa la khyab par 'khrugs pas khong nas 'khrugs pa'o / / 'di ni yid mi bde ba dang reg par mi gnas pa'i las can no /
upāttaṃ vastu dharmāmiṣakauśalātmakaṃ yena pūjānugrahakāmyayārthine 'narthine vā dīyate taddānam / tasmin sati dānābhāvāt tadvirodhīty ucyate
# zin pa'i dngos po chos dang zang zing dang mkhas pa'i bdag nyid rnams gang gi phyir mchod pa dang phan 'dogs par 'dod pas 'dod pa'am / / mi 'dod pa la yang rung ste sbyin par byed pa de ni sbyin pa'o / / de yod na sbyin pa med par 'gyur ba'i phyir de dang mi mthun pa zhes bya'o /
lābhasatkārādhyavasitasya jīvitopakaraṇeṣu rāgāṃśikaścetasa āgraho'parityāgecchā mātsaryam
# rnyed pa dang bkur sti la zhen nas 'tsho ba'i yo byad rnams la 'dod chags kyi shas kyis sems kyis kun tu 'dzin pa dang yongs su mi gtong bar 'dod pa ni ser sna'o /
idaṃāsaṃlekhasanniśrayadānakarmakaṃ
# 'di ni yo byad ma bsnyungs pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
asaṃlekhaḥ punarmātsaryeṇānupayujyamānānām apy upakaraṇānāṃ sannicayādveditavyaḥp j
# yo byad ma bsnyungs pa ni ser snas yo byad mi mkho ba rnams kyang sogs pa'i phyir ro / / rgyu gang zhe na /
māyā paravañcanāyāabhūtārthasandarśanā / lābhasatkārādhyavasitasya paravañcanābhiprāyeṇānyathāvyavasthitasya śīlāder arthasyānyathā prakāśanā
# gzhan la slu ba'i yang dag pa ma yin pa'i don ston pa'o zhes bya ba ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par chags pas gzhan la slu ba'i bsam pas tshul khrims la sogs pa'i don gzhan du gnas la gnas gzhan du ston pa ste /
iyaṃ cayābhyāṃ rāgamohābhyām abhūtān guṇān prakāśayate tayoḥsamuditayoḥ prajñapyata iti krodhādivat prajñaptita eva nadravyataḥ / mithyājīvasanniśrayadānakarmikā
# 'di ni 'dod chags dang gti mug gnyis kyis yang dag pa ma yin pa'i yon tan ston pas na de gnyis 'dus pa la gdags te / / khro bo la sogs pa bzhin du btags pa nyid yin gyi / / rdzas su ni med do / / log pas 'tsho ba'i rten byed pa'i las can te /
kāyavākkuhanopāttāḥ śayyāsanādaya upajīvyante na cavyāyāmalabdhā iti mithyājīva ucyate / śāṭhyaṃ katamat / svadoṣapracchādanopāyasaṅgṛhītaṃcetasaḥ kauṭilyaṃ
# lus dang ngag gi tshul 'chos pas zin pa'i mal cha la sogs pa nye bar 'tsho'i / / yang dag pa'i rtsol bas rnyed pas ni ma yin pa ni log pas 'tsho ba zhes bya'o / / g yo gang zhe na / / bdag gi nyes pa bcab pa'i thabs bzung ba ste /
svadoṣapracchādanopāyaḥ / paravyāmohanam / tat punar anyenānyat pratisarati kṣipatyaparisphuṭaṃ vā pratipadyate / ata eva śāṭhyaṃ mrakṣādbhidyate / sa hi parisphuṭam eva pracchādayati / svadoṣapracchādanopāyasaṅgrahas tannimittatvāt
# sems gya gyu ba'o zhes bya ba la bdag gi nyes pa bcab pa'i thabs ni gzhan mgo rmongs par byed pa ste / / de yang gzhan nas gzhan du bsgyur zhing gtam rlung skur ba dang bsal bar mi byed pa'o / / de'i phyir gyo dang 'chab pa gnyis tha dad de / / de ni dngos su mkhyud par byed pa'o / / 'di ni bdag gi nyes pa bcab pa'i thabs bzung ba ste / / de'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
cetasaḥ kauṭilyaṃ vaṅkatā yasya yogāc cittam ṛjumārgaṃ napratipadyate
# sems gya gyu ba ni mi drang ba ste / / de dang ldan na sems lam drang por mi 'jug go /
idaṃ calābhasatkārādhyavasito yābhyāṃrāgamohābhyāṃsvadoṣapracchādanārthaṃ paramohanāya pravartate tayor eva sahitayos tat prajñapyate
# 'di ni rnyed pa dang bkur sti la lhag par chags nas 'dod chags dang gti mug de gnyis kyi bdag gi nyes pa bcab pa'i phyir mgo rmongs par byed pas de gnyis 'dus pa la de gdags so /
idaṃ ca zsaṃyagavavādalābhaparipanthakarmakaṃ
# 'di ni yang dag pa'i gdams ngag rnyed pa'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no /
saṃyagavavāde yolābho yoniśo manaskāraḥ tasyāntarāyaṃ karotīti
# yang dag pa'i gdams ngag ni gang rnyed na tshul bzhin yid la byed pa ste / / de'i bar chad byed pa'o /
madaḥ svasampattau raktasyoddharṣaś
# rgyags pa gang zhe na / / bdag gi phun sum tshogs pa la chags pa'i bar du dga' ba ste /
cetasaḥ paryādānam / kulārogyarūpayauvanabalaiśvaryabuddhimedhādiprakarṣaḥ svasampattiḥ
# sems yongs su 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba ni rigs dang nad med pa dang gzugs dang lang tsho la bab pa dang stobs dang phyug pa dang blo dang yid gzhungs pa la sogs pa mchog tu gyur pa ni rang gi phun sum tshogs pa'o /
uddharṣo harṣaviśeṣaḥ
# rab tu dga' ba ni dga' ba'i bye brag go /
harṣaviśeṣam evavyācaṣṭe cetasaḥ paryādānam iti
# sems yongs su 'dzin pa zhes bya bas ni dga' ba'i bye brag nyid ston te /
yena harṣaviśeṣeṇa cittamasvatantrīkṛtaṃ tena tad ātmatantrīkaraṇāt paryāttaṃ bhavatītyata uktam cetasaḥ paryādānam iti
# dga' ba'i bye brag gang gis sems rang dbang med par byed pa des de bdag gi dbang du bya ba byed pas yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur te / / de'i phyir sems yongs su 'dzin pa zhes bshad do /
eṣasaṅkṣepo harṣaviśeṣasahitas tṛṣṇāprakāro mada iti
# 'dir ni mdor na dga' ba'i bye brag dang ldan pa'i sred pa'i rnam pa la rgyags pa zhes bya'o /
ayaṃ ca esarvakleśopakleśasanniśrayadānakarmakaḥ
# 'di ni nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi rten byed pa'i las can no /
vividhair vadhabandhanatāḍanatarjanādibhiḥ sattvānāṃ hiṃsāvihiṃsā
# rnam par 'tshe ba ni / / gsad pa dang bcing ba dang brdeg pa dang bsdigs pa la sogs pa gnod pa sna tshogs kyis / / sems can rnams la 'tshe bas rnam par 'tshe ba ste /
viheṭhyante 'nayā sattvā vadhabandhanādibhir / duḥkhadaurmanasyotpādanād iti viheṭhanā
# 'dis gsad pa dang bcing ba la sogs pas sems can rnams la rnam par tho 'tshams pas sdug bsngal dang yid mi bde ba skyed pa'i phyir / / rnam par tho 'tshams pa'o /
sā punaḥpratighāṃśikā nirghṛṇatāniṣkaruṇatā nirdayatāca
# de ni khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa ste / / snying brtse ba med pa dang snying rje med pa dang brtse ba med pa'o /
etāś canirghṛṇatādayaḥ svayaṃ vadhādiṃ kurvataḥ kārayataḥ paraiśca kriyamāṇān dṛṣṭvā śrutvā vānumodataś ca yathākramaṃboddhavyāḥ uttarottaravyākhyānato vā
# snying brtse ba med pa la sogs pa 'di dag kyang gsod pa la sogs pa bdag nyid kyis byed pa dang byed du 'jug pa dang gzhan dag byed pa mthong ngam; thos na rjes su yi rang ba rnams dang go rims bzhin du sbyar bar shes par bya'o / / yang na gcig gis gcig bshad do /
eṣa tu saṅkṣepaḥ pratighāṃśikāsattveṣu cittarūkṣatā sattvaviheṭhanakarmikāvihiṃsety ucyate / nāsya hrīr astīty ahrīḥ / sa yadyogād evam ucyatehrīvipakṣabhūtaṃ tad āhrīkyam / tasmin karmaṇy / ātmanam ayogyamavekṣyamāṇasyāpiāvadyenālajjāsāhrīkyaṃ / apatrapate 'nayety apatrāpyam / tadviparītamanapatrāpyam / lokaśāstraviruddham etan mayā kriyata / ity evam avagacchato 'pi yānayā pāpakriyayālajjāsānapatrāpyaṃ / etac ca dvayam apisarv akle śopa kleś asāh āyya karm akaṃ / rāgadveṣamohaprakāreṣu sarvasatkāyaprasavahetuṣurāgadveṣayor ayaugapadyād yathāsambhavaṃ prajñapyate na svatantre sta iti / styānaṃcittākarmaṇyatā / paryāyāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe / rstaimityam iti
# 'di ni mdor na khong khro ba'i char gtogs pa ste / / sems can rnams la sems rtsub pa dang sems can rnams la rnam par tho 'tshams ba'i las can ni rnam par 'tshe ba zhes bya'o / / ngo tsha med pa ni 'di la ngo tsha med pa ste / / de gang dang ldan na de skad ces bya ba de ngo tsha shes pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs su gyur pa ni ngo tsha med pa ste / / las de bdag gi cha ma yi na shes kyang gang kha na mtho pas mi 'dzem pa de ngo tsha med pa'o / / 'dis khrel ltas byed pas khrel yod pas te / / de las bzlog pa ni khred med pa'o / / 'di gnyis ni nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi grogs byed pa'i las can no / / bya ba ngan pa thams cad kyi rgyu 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug gi rnam pa rnams ji ltar mthun mthun du gdags te / / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang gnyis cig car mi 'byung ba'i phyir ro / / 'di gnyis ni rang gi rgyud ni med do / / rmugs pa gang zhe na / / sems las su mi rung ba ste /
stimitabhāvaḥ staimityam yadyogāc cittaṃjaḍībhāvāt stimitam iva bhavati nālambanaṃ pratipattum utsahate
# blong ba nyid do zhes bya ba la blong ba nyid ni rnam grangs gzhan gyis bstan pa'o / / blong ba'i dngos po ni blong ba nyid de / / de dang ldan na sems blun par gyur nas mi gyo ba bzhin du dmigs pa rtogs par mi nus pa'o /
etac casarvakleśopakleśasāhāyyakarmakaṃ
# 'di yang nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi grogs byed pa'i las can no /
tmohāṃśeprajñaptatvāc caprajñaptita eva na dravyataḥ / auddhatyaṃcittasyāvyupaśamaḥ / vyupaśamo hi / śamathaḥ / tadviruddho 'vyupaśamaḥ / sa punārāgānukūlaḥ pūrvahasitaramitakriḍitādy anusmaratorāgāṃśikaścetaso 'vyupaśamahetuḥ / yśamathaparipanthakarmakaṃśraddhāvipakṣa iti śraddhāstitvaguṇavattvaśakyatveṣv / abhisampratyayaḥ prasādo 'bhilāṣaś cayathākramam / aśraddhātadviparyayeṇāstitvaguṇavattvaśakyatveṣvasampratyayo'prasādo 'nabhilāṣaś ca / kauśīdyasanniśrayadānakarmakaṃ / aśraddhadhānasya prayogacchandābhāvātkausīdyasanniśrayadānakarmakatvaṃ
# gti mug gi cha la gdags pas btags pa nyid yin gyi rdzas su ni ma yin no / / rgod pa gang zhe na / / sems ma zhi ba'o zhes bya ba la zhi ba ni zhi gnas te / / de dang mi mthun pa ni ma zhi ba'o / / de yang 'dod chags dang mthun pa sngon dgod dgod pa dang rtse rtse ba la sogs pa dran pa'i 'dod chags kyi char gtogs pa sems ma zhi ba'i rgyu ste / / zhi gnas kyi bar du gcod pa'i las can no / / dad pa'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs zhes bya ba la / / dad pa ni yod pa dang yon tan can dang nus pa rnams la mngon par yid ches pa dang dang ba dang 'dod pa'o / / de las bzlog pa ni ma dang pa ste / / dad pa med pa ni sbyor ba la 'dun pa med pas le lo'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
kuśale kāyavāṅmanaḥkarmaṇinidrāpārśvaśayanasukham / āgamya yo mohāṃśikaścetaso 'nabhyutsāhaḥsakausīdyam / kutsitaṃ sīdatīti kusīdaḥ / tadbhāvaḥkausīdyam vīryavipakṣaḥ / vīryavipakṣaiti vīryaṃ hi
# nyal ba dang gnyid pa dang 'phres pa'i bde ba la brten nas gti mug gi char gtogs pas lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las dge ba la sems mi spro ba de ni le lo ste / / ngan pa la sbyor bas ni le lo'o / / brtson 'grus kyi mi mthun pa'i phyogs zhes bya ba la brtson 'grus ni dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor ba la sems mngon par spro ba'o /
kuśalapakṣaprayoge cetaso 'bhyutsāhaḥ tadvipakṣatvātkausīdyam / etac cakuśalapakṣaprayogaparipanthakarmakaṃ / lobhadveṣamohakausīdyeṣu pramādaḥprajñapyate / yathāvyākhyāteṣu / ayaṃcākuśalavṛddhikuśalaparihāṇisaṃniśrayadānakarmakaḥ / muṣitasmṛtitā kliṣṭā smṛtiḥ / kliṣṭeti / lkleśasamprayuktā / kuśalasyānabhilapanateti na hi / kleśasamprayuktā smṛtiḥ kleśenābhinnaviṣayatvātkuśalam abhilapituṃ samarthā / iyaṃ cavikṣepasanniśrayadānakarmikā / vividhaṃ kṣipyate 'nena cittam iti vikṣepaḥ
# de'i mi mthun pa'i phyogs yin pas le lo ste / / dge ba'i phyogs la sbyor ba'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no / / bag med pa ni chags pa dang zhe sdang dang gti mug ji skad du bshad pa rnams la btags te mi dge ba 'phel ba dang dge ba 'grib pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / brjed ngas pa gang zhe na / / dran pa nyon mongs pa can de zhes bya ba la nyon mongs pa zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'o / / dge ba la mi gsal ba zhes bya ba la / / nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i dran pa ni nyon mongs pa dang yul tha dad pa ma yin pas dge ba la sems gsal bar byed mi nus te / / g yeng ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / rnam par gyeng ba ni 'dis sems sna tshogs su gyeng bar byed pa'o / / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug de dag gis sems ting nge 'dzin gyi dmigs pa las phyi rol tu 'phro bar byed pa ste /
yai / prāgadveṣamohaiś cittaṃsamādhyālambanād bahir visāryate teṣuyathāsambhavam upakleśātmako vikṣepaḥ prajñapyate / eṣa cavairāgyaparipanthakarmakaḥ
# de dag la ji ltar mthun mthun du nye ba'i nyon mongs pa'i bdag nyid kyi gyeng ba gdags so / / 'dod chags dang bral ba'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no / / shes bzhin ma yin pa gang zhe na /
samprajanyaṃkleśasamprayuktā prajñā
# nyon mongs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa'i shes rab ste /
yayāsamviditākāyavākcittacaryābhikramapratikramādiṣupravartate
# des lus dang ngag dang yid kyi spyod pa 'gro ba dang ldog pa la sogs pa la mi shes bzhin du 'jug pa ste /
karaṇīyākaraṇīyājñānācāpattisanniśrayadānakarmakaṃ / kaukṛtyaṃcetaso vipratisāraḥ / kutsitaṃ kṛtam iti / kukṛtam / tadbhāvaḥ kaukṛtyam
# bya ba dang bya ba ma yin pa mi shes pas ltung ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no / / phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa / / bam po gsum pa / / 'gyod pa gang zhe na / / yid la gcags pa'o zhes bya ba la ngan pa byas pas 'gyod de de'i dngos po ni 'gyod pa nyid do /
kukṛtaviṣayaś cetaso vilekhaḥkaukṛtyam ucyate caitasikādhikārāt
# ngan pa byas pa'i yul la sems mi dga' ba ste / / sems las byung ba'i skabs yin pas 'gyod pa zhes bya'o /
abhipretam anabhipretaṃkuśalam akuśalam avyākṛtaṃ kāle'kāle yuktam ayuktaṃ cakṛtvākṛtvā vā mohāṃśikaś cetaso vipratisāraḥ kaukṛtyam
# 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa dang dus dang dus ma yin pa dang rang mi rigs pa byas sam ma byas kyang rung ste / / gti mug gi char gtogs pa'i sems kyi yid la gcags pa ni 'gyod pa ste /
ztaccacittasthitiparipanthakarmakaṃ / a babhiratipūrvakaṃ yat kriyatetad abhipretam
# 'di ni sems gnas pa'i bar du gcod pa'i las can no / / mngon par dga' ba sngon du 'gro ba'i byed pa gang yin pa de ni 'dod pa'o /
anabhipretaṃ punaḥ parair balād avaṣṭabhyayat kāryate kleśābhibhavād vāyat karoti
# mi 'dod pa ni gzhan dag gis nan gyis byed du bcug pa gang yin pa dang nyon mongs pa'i zil gyis non nas byed pa gang yin pa'o /
kālo yāvan naviramatiakālas tadūrdhvam / yuktaṃ sthāne ayuktam asthāne
# dus ni ji srid du ma spangs pa'o / / dus ma yin pa ni de las thal ba'o / / rigs pa ni gnas yin pa'o / / mi rigs pa ni gnas ma yin pa'o /
taccāpi trividham kuśalam akuśalam avyākṛtaṃ ca
# de la rnam pa gsum ste / / dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'o /
mohāṃśikam ity upakleśasaṅgṛhītamatra gṛhyate / e fmiddham asvatantravṛttiś cetaso / 'bhisaṅkṣepaḥ / vṛttir ālambane pravṛttiḥ / sāsvatantrācetaso yato bhavati tan middham
# 'dir ni gti mug gi char gtogs pa'i nye ba'i nyon mongs pas bsdus pa kho na gzung ngo / / gnyid gang zhe na / / 'jug pa rang dbang med par sems sdud pa'o zhes bya ba la 'jug pa ni dmigs pa la 'jug pa'o / / de yang sems kyi rang dbang med pa gang las 'byung ba nyid ces bya'o /
kāyasandhāraṇāsamarthāvāvṛttiś cetaso 'svatantrā sā yato bhavati tan middhaṃ / anyato'py asvatantrā vṛttiś cetaso bhavatīty ata āha cetaso'bhisaṅkṣepa iti / anyato'py abhisaṅkṣepaś cetasa ityasvatantravṛttiś cetasa ity āha
# yang na lus 'dzin mi nus pa'i sems kyi 'jug pa rang dbang med pa de gang las byung ba de gnyid ces bya'o / / gzhan gyis kyang sems kyi 'jug pa rang dbang med par 'gyur bas de'i phyir sems sdud pa zhes bya ba smos so / / gzhan gyis kyang sems sdud par 'gyur bas sems kyi 'jug pa rang dbang med pa zhes bya ba smos so /
abhisaṅkṣepaś cetasaścakṣurādīndriyadvāreṇāpravṛttiḥ / sa punaḥkuśalo 'kuśalo'vyākṛtaśca
# sems sdud pa ni mig la sogs pa'i dbang po'i sgo nas mi 'jug pa'o / / de yang dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'o /
middhanimittaṃdaurbalyaśramakāyagauravāndhakāranimittamanasikaraṇādika māgamyamohāṃśikobhavati / kṛtyātipattisanniśrayadānakarmakaṃ
# gnyid kyi rgyu nyi nyams chung ba dang ngal ba dang lus lci ba dang mun pa'i mtshan ma yid la byed pa la sogs pa la brten nas gti mug gi char gtogs pa 'byung ste / / bya ba shor ba'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
atra cākuśala evamohāṃśikaḥ nānyaḥ / vitarkaḥparyeṣako manojalpaś
# 'dir ni mi dge ba nyid gti mug gi char gtogs pa yin gyi gzhan ni ma yin no / / rtog pa gang zhe na / / kun du tshol ba'i yid kyi brjod pa ste /
cetanāprajñāviśeṣaḥ / paryeṣakaḥ kim etad iti nirūpaṇākārapravṛttaḥ
# sems pa dang shes rab kyi bye brag ces bya ba la kun du tshol ba ni 'di ci yin zhes kun du rtog pa'i rnam par zhugs pa'o /
manaḥsvabhāvo jalpo manojalpaḥ
# yid kyi rang bzhin gyi brjod pa ni yid kyi brjod pa'o /
jalpa iva jalpo 'rthakathanā / cetanāprajñāviśeṣa iti cetanāyāścittaparispandātmakatvāt prajñāyāś caguṇadoṣavivekākāratvāt
# brjod pa dang 'dra bas brjod pa ste don brjod pa'o / / sems pa dang shes rab kyi bye brag ces bya ba la sems pa ni gang gis sems kun du gyo bar byed pa'i bdag nyid yin la /
tadvaśena cittapravṛtteḥ kadāciccittacetanayor vitarkaprajñaptiḥ kadācit prajñācetasoḥ yathākramam abhyūhānabhyūhāvasthāyoḥ
# shes rab ni yon tan dang nyes pa 'byed pa'i rnam pa yin pas de'i dbang gis kyang sems 'jug pas na bar 'ga' sems dang sems pa la rtog pa gdags / / 'ga' ni shes rab dang sems la ste /
athavācetanāprajñayor eva vitarkaprajñaptiḥ tadvaśena cittasya tathāpravṛttatvāt
# mngon par mi rtog pa dang mngon par rtogs pa'i dus dang go rims bzhin no / / yang na sems pa dang shes rab nyid la gdags te / / de'i dbang gis de ltar 'jug pa'i phyir ro /
eṣa ca nayo vicāre 'pi draṣṭavyaḥ
# tshul 'di ni dpyod pa la yang blta bar bya'o /
ittasyaudārikateti sthūlatāvastumātraparyeṣaṇākāratvāt
# sems rtsing ba'o zhes bya ba la che long ste / / dngos po tsam kun du tshol ba'i rnam pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
vicāraḥpratyavekṣako manojalpaḥidaṃ tad iti / pūrvādhigatanirūpaṇāt
# dpyod pa gang zhe na / / so sor rtog pa yid kyi dpyod pa ste zhes bya ba ni sngar khong du chud pa la 'di ni 'di'o zhes dpyod pa'i rnam pa yin pa'i phyir ro /
tathaivacittasya / sūkṣmateti / tathaiveti cetanāprajñāviśeṣaḥ
# de bzhin du gang sems zhi ba ba'o zhes bya ba la de bzhin du zhes bya ba ni / / sems pa dang shes rab kyi bye brag go /
paryeṣaṇatovastupratyavekṣaṇākāratvāt sūkṣma ucyate
# dngos po la so sor rtog pa'i rnam pa yin pas zhi ba pa zhes bya'o /
etau casparśāsparśavihārasanniśrayadānakarmakau
# 'di gnyis ni reg par gnas pa dang reg par mi gnas pa'i rten byed pa'i las can no /
anayoścaudārikasūkṣmavyavasthānāt pṛthakkaraṇam
# 'di gnyis ni sems rtsing ba dang zhib par rnam par gnas pa tha dad du dbye'o /
saṃskāraskandho vedanāsañjñāvyatiriktacaitasikātmakaścittaviprayuktasaṃskārātmakaś cety uktam / tatra caitasikāuktāḥ
# 'du byed kyi phung po ni tshor ba dang 'du shes las gzhan pa sems las byung ba'i bdag nyid dang sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed kyi bdag nyid do zhes bshad pa de la sems las byung ba rnams bshad zin to /
cittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārā idānīṃ vaktavyā ity ata āha cittaviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥkatama iti
# da ni sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams brjod dgos pas de'i phyir / / sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams gang zhe na zhes bya ba smos te /
praśnavat sāmānyatas tannirdeśaḥ yerūpacittacaitasikāvasthāsu prajñapyante
# dris pa bzhin du gang dag gzugs dang sems dang sems las byung ba'i gnas skabs la gdags pa ste /
tattvānyatvataś ca na prajñapyante teviprayuktāḥ saṃskārā iti prakaraṇāt sambadhyate
# de nyid dang gzhan du mi gdags so zhes de dag spyir bstan te / / de dag ni mi ldan pa'i 'du byed yin par skabs kyis sbyar ro /
rūpādyavasthāvyatiriktasvarūpābhāvāt te rūpādyavasthāsusaṃvyavahārārthaṃ prajñapyante / ata eva svopādānāt tattvānyatvenāvasthāvan na prajñapyante avasthāvasthāvatorekānekatvaprasaṅgād avasthāvataś cākāryanityatvaprasaṅgāt / sāmānyanirdeśād viśeṣānavagamād viśeṣabubhutsayā praśnaḥ te punaḥ katama iti / prāptir / asañjñisamāpattiriti vistareṇa tadviśeṣanidarśanam / evambhāgīyā evañjātīyāḥ
# gzugs la sogs pa'i gnas skabs pas rang gi ngo bo gud na med pas / / de dag ni gzugs la sogs pa'i gnas skabs la tha snyad gdags pa'i phyir btags pa'o / / de'i phyir rten dang bcas pa yin pas gnas skabs bzhin du de nyid dang gzhan du mi gdags te / / gnas skabs dang gnas skabs can gcig dang du ma nyid du thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir dang gnas skabs can la 'bras bu rtag par thal bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro; / / de ltar spyir bstan nas khyad par khong du chud par 'dod nas / / de dag kyang gang zhe na zhes dris pa dang thob pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang zhes bya ba de dag gi khyad par rgya cher bstan to / / de lta bu'i cha dang mthun pa dag go zhes bya ba ni de lta bu'i rang bzhin can dag ste /
ye 'nye 'pi / rūpacittacaittāvasthāsu prajñapyante teviprayuktāḥ saṃskārāveditavyāḥ / te punaḥ katame
# gzhan gang dag gzugs dang sems dang sems las byung ba'i gnas skabs la gdags pa ste / / de dag kyang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed rnams su rig par bya'o / / de dag kyang gang zhe na /
pravṛttiḥ pratiniyamo yogo javo'nukramaḥ kālo deśaḥ saṅkhyā sāmagrī cety evamādayaḥ
# 'jug pa dang so sor nges pa dang 'byor pa dang mgyogs pa dang go rims dang rus dang yul dang grangs dang tshogs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o /
idānīṃ sāmagryādīnāṃ pratyekaṃ svarūpanirdhāraṇārthaṃpraśnaḥ prāptiḥ katamety evamādiḥ / pratilambhaḥ samanvāgamaityādi / tat kilāyamaprāptapūrvasya prathamataḥ prāptiḥ pratilambhaḥ
# da ni tshogs pa la sogs pa'i rang gi ngo bo so sor dmigs kyis dbye ba'i phyir / / thob pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa dris pa dang rnyed pa dang ldan pa'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so / / sngon ma thob pa thog ma nyid du thob pa ni rnyed pa'o /
prāptānāṃdvitīyādiṣu kṣaṇeṣu prāptiḥ samanvāgamaḥ samanugamaḥsamanvāgama iti kṛtvā
# rnyed pa rnams skad cig gnyis pa la sogs par yod pa ni ldan pa ste / / yang dag par rjes su 'gro ba ni ldan pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ caprāptiśabdaḥ pratilambhesamanvāgame ca vartataiti jñāpitaṃ bhavati
# de ltar na thob pa'i sgra ni rnyed pa dang ldan pa la yang snyegs par bstan pa yin no /
sā punar / bījaṃ vaśitā sammukhībhāvaś ceti tridhābhidyate yathāyogam iti
# de yang sa bon dang dbang dang mngon du gyur pa dang rnam pa gsum du dbye'o / / ci rigs su sbyar ro zhes bya ba de la rigs pa ni 'di yin te /
tatrāyaṃ yogaḥ prathamātkṣaṇād ārabhya prāptir yāvad vaśitāvasthaṃ bījam ucyata itipratilambhasamanvāgamau bījākhyau bhavataḥ vaśitāsammukhībhāvaś ca samanvāgama eva / kiṃ punar bījam
# skad cig dang po thob pa nas brtsams te dbang gi dus kyi bar du sa bon zhes bya ste / / de ltar na sa bon ni rnyed pa dang ldan pa gnyi gar brjod pa yin no / / dbang dang mngon du gyur pa ni ldan pa yin no / / sa bon ci la bya zhe na /
kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtair dharmair āhito vijñāne'nāgatatajjātīyadharmahetuḥ sāmarthyaviśeṣo bījam
# dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i chos rnams kyi rnam par shes pa la ma 'ongs pa na de dang rigs gcig pa'i chos kyi rgyu bskyed pa'i nus pa'i bye brag ni sa bon no /
bīje hilabdhe tadāyattatvād asammukhībhūtamapi yasya tad bījaṃ tatprāptam ucyate
# sa bon rnyed nas de la rag las pa'i phyir mngon du ma gyur kyang de'i sa bon gang yin pa de thob pa zhes bya'o /
vaśitā punas tasya pratyayānapekṣyāpratibandhena svakāryanirvartanāvasthā / sammukhībhāvas tatkāryanirvṛttyavasthā / asañjñā vā samāpattir asañjñisamāpattir asañjñānām vāsamāpattirity asañjñisamāpattiḥ / eśubhakṛtsnavītarāgasyetitṛtīyadhyānavītarāgasyeti / tṛtīyaṃdhyānaṃ parīttaśubhāḥapramāṇaśubhāḥśubhakṛtsnāś ca
# dbang ni de'i rkyen la ltos nas rgyun gyi 'bras bu bsgrub pa'i gnas skabs so / / mngon du gyur ba ni de'i 'bras bu grub pa'i dus so / / 'du shes med pa'am 'du shes med pa rnams kyi ste / / 'du shes med par snyoms bar 'jug pa'am / / 'du shes med pa rnams kyi snyoms par 'jug pa ni / / 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'o / / dge rgyas kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba ni bsam gtan gsum pa'i 'dod chags dang bral ba'o / / bsam gtan gsum pa ni dge chung dang tshad med dge dang dge rgyas so /
tatra yaḥ śubhakṛtsnebhyo vītarāgaḥ satṛtīyād dhyānād vītarāgaḥ
# de la gang dge rgyas las 'dod chags dang bral ba de ni bsam gtan gsum pa las 'dod chags dang bral ba'o /
nordhvaṃtṛtīyād dhyānād / ūrdhvaṃcaturthaṃdhyānam caturthād dhyānād avītarāgasyety arthaḥ
# gong ma ma yin pa ni bsam gtan gsum pa las gong du gyur pa bsam gtan bzhi pa ste / / bsam gtan bzhi pa la 'dod chags dang ma bral zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
niḥsaraṇasañjñāpūrvakeṇetiniḥsaraṇasañjñā pūrvaṃ yasya manasikārasya saniḥsaraṇasañjñāpūrvakaḥ
# 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pa su la yod pa de 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba ste /
āsañjñike mokṣasañjñinaḥsamāpattau vā tanmārgasañjñino 'sañjñisamāpattiṃsamāpadyante
# 'du shes med pa la thar bar 'du shes pa'am / / snyoms bar 'jug pa la de'i lam du 'du shes pa rnams 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug go /
ato niḥsaraṇasañjñā mokṣasañjñātanmārgasañjñā vā
# de'i phyir 'byung ba'i 'du shes ni thar pa'i 'du shes sam / / de'i lam du 'du shes pa'o /
vidūṣaṇākāro 'tra niḥsaraṇasañjñāpūrvakomanasikāro 'bhipretaḥ
# 'dir ni sun 'byin pa'i rnam pa la 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pa zhes bya bar 'dod de /
ata eva sarvacittacaittanirodhe 'pisañjñābhāvoeva nirdiśyate'sañjñisamāpattir iti
# de nyid kyi phyir sems dang sems las byung ba 'gags su zin kyang 'du shes med pa nyid la 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa zhes bstan te /
tathā hisañjñām eva vidūṣayan niravaśeṣacittacaittanirodhaṃ prāpnoti / sthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaitasikānāṃ yo nirodha / iti / sthāvarāḥ pravṛttivijñānasaṅgṛhītāḥsasamprayogāḥṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ / sarvāsv acittikāsv avasthāsv abhāvāt sacittikāsvapy avasthāsu ye na sarvadā bhavanti te'sthāvarāḥ
# 'di ltar 'du shes nyid la sun 'byin pas sems dang sems las byung ba ma lus par 'gag pa'i gnas skabs su 'gyur ro / / sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brten pa ma yin pa rnams gang 'gog pa'o zhes bya ba la brten pa ma yin pa rnams ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes par bsdus pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag ste / / gang gi phyir sems med pa'i dus thams cad na med pa dang sems dang bcas pa'i dus rnams na yang gang gi phyir ni rtag tu yod pa ma yin pa de dag brtan pa ma yin pa rnams so / / brtan pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yid mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa ste / / gtan du yod pa'i phyir ro /
sthāvaramālayavijñānaṃ sasamprayogam sarvadā bhāvāt kliṣṭaṃ camanaḥ anāsravamārgasatyasamāpattyavasthāṃnirodhasamāpattyavasthāṃ tām aśaikṣāvasthāṃ ca hitvānyāsusarvāsv avasthāsu bhāvād ity asthāvarāṇām iti viśeṣaṇam
# zag pa med pa'i lam gyi bden pa la snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus dang 'gog pa la snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus dang mi slob pa'i dus ma gtogs par dus gzhan kun na yod pa'i phyir brtan pa ma yin pa rnams zhes bye brag smos so / / gang 'gog pa zhes bya ba ni snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems kyis byas pa ste /
yonirodha iti samāpatticittakṛtaḥ kālāntaramsthāvaracittacaittasamudācāravirodhy āśrayasyāvasthāviśeṣaḥ / nirudhyate 'nenetinirodhaḥ
# 'dis 'gag par byed pas na 'gog pa'o / / dus gzhan na sems dang sems las byung ba brtan pa ma yin pa kun du 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i lus kyi gnas skabs kyi bye brag la bya ste /
evaṃ cāśrayāvasthāviśeṣeasañjñisamāpattiḥ prajñapyata ity uktaṃ bhavati
# de ltar na lus kyi gnas skabs kyi bye brag la 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la gdags par bstan pa yin no /
samāpatticittenānantaraṃ cittāntarotpattiviruddha āśrayo yaḥ sa samāpatticittena kṛta ity ucyate / niro dhasamā pattir / mākiñcanyāyatanavītarāgasyabhavāgrād / uccalitasyeti / bhavāgrād anuccalito 'py astyākiñcanyāyatanavītarāgaḥpṛthagjana ity ata āha bhavāgrāduccalitasyeti
# snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems kyis de ma thag pa'i sems gzhan skye ba dang mi mthun pa'i lus skyed pa'i phyir snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems kyis byas pa zhes bya'o / / 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa gang zhe na / / ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa'o zhes bya ba ni /
bhavāgrād uccalita ākiñcanyāyatanavītarāgo 'py asti kaścit phalasthaḥ pratipannakaś ca bhavāgrād uccalitaākiñcanyāyatanād avītarāgo 'py asti kaścit phalasthaḥpratipannakaś cety ata āha ākiñcanyāyatanavītarāgasyeti
# srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du ma bskyod kyang ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i so so skye bo'i yang yod pas de'i phyir srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa zhes bya ba smos so / / srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba kha cig / / 'bras bu la gnas pa dang 'jug pa yang yod pas / / de'i phyir ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba zhes bya ba smos so /
upary avītarāgasyety avacanam bhavāgravītarāgasyārhato 'pinirodhasamāpattisambhavāt
# gong ma'i 'dod chags dang bral ba zhes ma brjod pa ni srid pa'i rtse mo'i 'dod chags dang bral ba dgra bcom pa yang 'gog pa la snyoms par 'jug pa yod pa'i phyir ro /
ākiñcanyāyatanavītarāgasyabhavāgrād uccalitasyety ubhayābhidhānenaāryasyaiveyamanāgāmino 'rhato vā samāpattiḥ na pṛthagjanasyeti jñāpitaṃbhavati / na hi pṛthagjano bhavāgrād uccalatibhavāgrapratipakṣasya mārgasyābhāvāt
# ci yang med pa'i skye mched kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba dang srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du bskyod pa zhes bya ba gnyi ga smos pas ni 'di 'phags pa phyir mi 'ong ba'am / / dgra bcom pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa yin gyi / / so so'i skye bo ni ma yin par bstan pa yin no / / so so'i skye bo ni srid pa'i rtse mo las gyen du mi bskyod do / / srid pa'i rtse mo las gnyen po 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lam med pa'i phyir ro /
darśanamārgas tubhavāgrapratipakṣo bhāvanāmārgaś cānāsravaḥ / ata ārya evabhavāgrād uccalitaḥdarśanaprahātavyakleśaprahāṇād cavirajya
# mthong ba'i lam zag pa med pa ni srid pa'i rtse mo'i gnyen po yin te / / de'i phyir 'phags pa nyid mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa spangs pa dang bsgom bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i phyir ma chags pas srid ba'i rtse mo las bskyod pa'o /
vihārasañjñāpūrvakeṇamanasikāreṇeti na hinirodhasamāpattim / asañjñāsamāpattim iva niḥsaraṇasañjñāpūrvakeṇamanasikāreṇa samāpadyante kiṃ tarhi vihārasañjñāpūrvakeṇa
# gnas pa'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pas zhes bya ba la 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ni 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bzhin du 'byung ba'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pas snyoms par 'jug pa ma yin gyi gnas pa'i 'du shes sngon du btang bas so /
nirodhasamāpattir bhavāgrakī na cāryāṇāṃ bhaveniḥsaraṇasañjñā pravartate
# 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa ni srid pa'i rtse mo ba ste / / 'phags pa rnams ni srid pa las 'byung ba'i 'du shes mi 'jug gi /
sañjñāveditaparikhinnastadabhāvān nirodhasamāpattau śāntavihārasañjñī bhavati / vihāra iti sañjñā vihārasañjñā viharaty anena iti vā vihāraḥ / kālāntaraṃ yāpayatīty arthaḥ
# 'du shes dang tshor bas yongs su skyo nas de med pa'i phyir 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la zhi bar gnas pa'i 'du shes su 'gyur ro / / gnas su mnyam pa'i 'du shes ni gnas pa'i 'du shes so / / 'dis gnas par byed pas gnas pa ste / / dus gzhan du sdod ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
nirvāṇasadṛśenasamāpattiviśeṣeṇa vihariṣyāma ity anayā sañjñayā saṃskṛtomanasikāro vihārasañjñāpūrvako manasikāra ucyate
# snyoms par 'jug pa'i khyad par mya ngan las 'das pa dang 'dra bas gnas par bya'o snyam pa'i 'du shes mngon par 'du byed pa'i yid la byed pa ni gnas pa'i 'du shes sngon du btang ba'i yid la byed pa zhes bya'o /
sa punarbhavāgrikaḥ śūkṣmaḥ tadanantaraṃ nirodhasamāpattisammukhībhāvāt
# srid pa'i rtse mo pa de ni phra ba'i phra ba ste / / de ma thag tu 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa mngon du 'gyur ba'i phyir ro /
sthāvarāṇāmitiṣaṇṇāṃ pravṛttivijñānānāṃ caturṇām ekasyakāmarūpārūpyadhātuṣu yathākramaṃ nirodhaṃsamāpadyamānānām
# brtan pa ma yin pa rnams zhes bya ba ni 'gog pa la snyoms par 'jug pa rnams kyi 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug dang bzhi dang gcig 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i khams rnams su go rims bzhin no /
ekatīyānāṃ ca sthāvarāṇāmiti / sthāvarā iti vipākavijñānasaṅgṛhītā api santīty ata āha ekatīyānām iti
# brtan pa rnams las kyang kha cig ces bya ba la brtan pa ni rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes par bsdus pa dag kyang yod pas de'i phyir kha cig ces bya ba smos so /
kliṣṭasya ca manasaḥ sarvasmin sāsrave cāresthānaśīlatvātsthāvaratvam anyatranirodhasamāpattyaśaikṣāvasthayoḥ / nirodhaiti
# nyon mongs pa can gyi yid ni 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang mi slob pa'i dus ma gtogs par zag pa dang bcas pa'i spyod pa thams cad na gnas pa'i tshul can yin pas brtan pa'o / / 'gog pa gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pas byas pa ste /
samāpattivijñānakṛto vipākavijñāne pravṛttivijñānānāṃ kliṣṭasya ca manaso bījopaghātaḥ
# rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i sa bon la gnod pa byed pa gang yin pa ste /
nirudhyate 'nena pravṛttivijñānaṃ kliṣṭaṃ ca manaḥ kālāntaram apravṛttita itinirodha ucyate
# 'dis 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yid dus gzhan na mi 'byung bar 'gog pas 'gog pa zhes bya'o /
evaṃ cālayavijñānasyasamāpatticittenopahatabījāvasthāyāṃ nirodhasamāpattiḥprajñapyate
# de ltar na snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems kyis kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la sa bon nyams par byas pa'i gnas skabs la 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa gdags so /
āsañjñikam asañjñisamāpatteḥ phalam / tasañ jñisattveṣu
# 'du shes med pa gang zhe na / / 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i 'bras bu ste /
deve ṣūpa pann asyā sthā varāṇāṃcittacaitasikānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yo nirodhaḥ / ubṛhatphalā nāma devāś caturthe dhyāne tṛtīyaṃ sthānāntaraṃ
# 'du shes med pa'i sems can lha rnams kyi nang du skyes pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brtan pa ma yin pa rnams gang 'gog pa'o zhes bya ba la lha de dag ni 'bras bu che ba zhes bya ba rnams te / / bsam gtan bzhi pa'i gnas gzhan gsum pa'o /
teṣāṃ parigaṇā ivopary asañjñisattvānāṃ devānāṃ sthānaṃtatropannasyāsañjñisamāpattivipākaphalam
# de dag gi gong na khang khyim lta bur 'du shes med pa'i sems can lha rnams kyi gnas yod pa der skyes pa'i 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i rnam par smin pa'i 'bras bu'o /
asthāvarāṇāṃcittacaittānāṃ yo nirodha iti tatsvarūpāvadhāraṇam
# sems dang sems las byung ba'i chos brtan pa ma yin pa rnams gang 'gog pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'di'i rang bzhin nges par bzung ba ste /
tatra hyupapannasyāsthāvarāś cittacaittāḥsvāśrayesvajātīyacittacaittabījopaghāte vartamānāḥ kṣāmakṣāmatarāutpadyante yāvad ante 'tikṣāmatāṃ gatāś cittāntaraṃsambandhuṃ na śaknuvanti svāśrayasyopahatabījatvāt
# der skyes pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba chos bstan pa ma yin pa rnams rang gi gnas la rang gi rigs kyi sems dang sems las byung ba'i sa bon la gnod par byed pa ni srab pa bas kyang ches srab bar 'gyur zhing tha mar shin tu srab pa'i bar du gyur nas rang gi gnas la sa bon nyams par byas pa'i phyir sems gzhan dang sbyor mi nus so /
ataścāsthāvarāṇāṃ cittacaittānāṃ tatkālāśrayeṇāpravṛttiḥ / tasyāṃcopahatabījāvasthāyām āśrayasyāsañjñikaṃ prajñapyate
# de'i phyir sems dang sems las byung ba'i brtan ba ma yin pa rnams de'i tshe gnas las mi 'byung ste / / sa bon nyams par gyur ba'i dus de na gnas la 'du shes med pa gdags so /
evam āśrayasyāvasthāviśeṣa eva nirudhyate 'neneti nirodhaḥ / jīvitendriyaṃnikāyasabhāgeṣu
# de ltar na gnas kyi dus nyid la bya ste / / 'dis 'gog par byed pas na 'gog pa'o / / srog gi dbang po gang zhe na /
pūrvakarmāviddho yaḥ saṃskārāṇāṃ sthitikālaniyamaiti / jīvyate 'neneti jīvitam
# ris mthun pa rnams su sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs pas gang 'du byed rnams kyi gnas ba'i dus nges pa'o zhes bya ba ni 'dis 'tsho bar byed pas srog go /
tad evanikāyasabhāgasthityādhipatyād indriyam / nikāyaḥsattvasamūhaḥ
# ris mthun pa de nyid du gnas bar dbang byed pa'i phyir dbang po zhes bya'o / / ris ni sems can gyi tshogs so /
samāno bhāga iti sabhāgaḥ sadṛśa ity arthaḥ / nikāyasya sabhāgāḥ
# skal ba mtshungs pa ni mthun pa ste / / 'dra zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / ris mthun pas ris mthun pa ste /
teṣu ca nikāyasabhāgeṣu gatibhedenakarmabhedena ca bhinneṣu pratyekam ekajānmiko yaḥ skandhasantānaḥsa nikāyasabhāgākhyaḥ
# 'gro ba tha dad pa dang las tha dad pas tha dad par gyur pa'i ris mthun pa de dag tu so so'i tshe gcig gi phung po'i rgyun gang yin pa de ris mthun pa zhes bya'o /
tasyapūrvopacitakuśalākuśalāniñjyakarmāviddhaḥ karmajanitaḥ / yaḥ sthitikālaniyama iti abhinnanikāyasabhāgasaṅgṛhītānāṃsaṃskārāṇāṃ pravṛttiḥ sthitiniyama ucyate / tasyāḥsthiteḥkālaniyama iyantaṃ kālam anenāsmin nikāyasabhāgesthātavyaṃ varṣaśataṃ varṣasahasraṃ vetyayaṃsthitikālaniyamaḥ / evaṃ ca sthitikālaniyamasvabhāvam āyurity uktaṃ bhavati
# de yang sngon bsags pa'i dge ba dang mi dge ba dang mi gyo ba'i las kyis 'phangs pa ni las kyis bskyed pa'o / / gang gnas pa'i dus nges pa zhes bya ba ni tha dad pa ma yin ba'i ris mthun pas bsdus pa'i 'du byed rnams kyi 'jug pa la gnas pa zhes bya'o / / gnas pa de'i dus nges pa ni 'dis ris mthun pa der lo brgya'am / / lo stong ngam / / dus ji srid du gnas par 'gyur ba de gnas pa'i dus nges pa'o /
adhiṣṭhānaṃ tu tasya sthāvarāḥ saṃskārāālayavijñānapūrvakāḥ pūrvajanmopacitenakarmaṇākṣiptasāmarthyaviśeṣāiti / nikāyasabhāgoyā sattvānām
# de ltar na gnas pa'i dus nges pa'i rang bzhin la tshe zhes bstan pa yin no / / de'i gnas ni sngon bsags pa'i las kyis 'phangs pas nus pa'i khyad par can gyi 'du byed brtan pa kun gzhi rnam par shes pa sngon du 'gro ba rnams so /
ātmabhāvasabhāgatā / sattvā devamanuṣyādayaḥpañcagatiparyāpannāḥ / teṣām ātmeti bhāvo yatra sa sattvānāmātmabhāvaḥ
# ris mthun pa gang zhe na gang sems can rnams kyi lus 'dra ba'o zhes bya ba la sems can ni lha dang mi la sogs pa 'gro ba lngar gtogs pa rnams so / / de dag gi bdag gi dngos por gang la 'dzin pa de / / sems can rnams kyi lus yin te /
sa punaḥ pañcopādānaskandhātmakaścatuḥskandhātmako vā / sabhāgatā sādṛśyam
# de yang nye bar len pa'i phung po lnga po nyid dam / / phung po bzhi'i bdag nyid do / / 'dra zhes bya ba ni mtshungs pa'o /
etad uktaṃbhavati gatisthānātmabhāvādibhedena bhinnānāṃ sattvānāṃgatisthānātmabhāvabhedanibandhanaṃ sattvānāṃ yaparaspareṇātmabhāvasādṛśyam tatra nikāyasabhāga itiprajñaptiḥ / jātirnikāyasabhāge yaḥ saṃskārāṇām / abhūtvā bhāvaḥ / nikāyasabhāgagrahaṇaṃ na / saṃskāramātrasyotpādo jātiḥ kiṃ tarhi nikāyasabhāgavartino ye saṃskārāḥ / teṣām evābhūtvā bhāvo jātiḥ na sarveṣām itijñāpanārtham
# de ni 'di skad du 'gro ba dang gnas dang lus la sogs pa tha dad pas tha dad pa ni sems can rnams kyi 'gro ba dang gnas dang lus tha dad pa'i gzhi sems can rnams kyi lus phan tshun 'dra ba gang yin pa de la ris mthun pa gdags so zhes bstan pa yin no / / skye pa gang zhe na / / ris mthun par gang 'du byed rnams ma byung ba las byung ba'o zhes bya ba la / / ris mthun pa smos pa ni 'du byed tsam gyi 'byung ba la skye ba zhes mi bya'i / / ris mthun par gyur pa'i 'du byed gang yin pa de dag nyid ma byung ba las byung ba la skye ba zhes bya ste / / thams cad ni ma yin no zhes bstan pa'i phyir ro /
ye bhāvānām anutpannāvinaṣṭānāmarthāntarabhūtāṃ jātiṃ kāritrataś cādhvavyavasthāṃpratipannāḥ tanmatanirāsārtham āha abhūtvā bhāva iti
# gang dag dngos po la skyes pa med pa dang zhig pa med pa rnams kyi skye ba don gzhan du 'gyur pa dang byed pa las dus rnam par gzhag par 'dzin pa rnams kyi 'dod pa de bsal ba'i phyir / / ma byung ba las byung ba zhes bya ba smos te /
svarūpasyaiva hi saṃskārāṇām abhūtvā bhāvo jātiḥ nārthāntarabhūtā na ca kāritrato 'dhvavyavastheti / jarā tathaivateṣāṃ prabandhānyathātvaṃ
# 'du byed rnams kyi rang bzhin ma byung ba las byung ba ni skye ba zhes bya'o / / don gzhan gyur pa yang med / / byed pa las dus rnam par gzhag pa yang ma yin no / / rga ba gang zhe na /
tathaivateṣām iti nikāyasabhāgapatitānām eva saṃskārāṇām
# de ltar de dag gi rgyun gzhan du 'gyur ba'o zhes bya ba la de ltar de dag gi zhes bya ba ni ris mthun par gyur pa'i 'du byed rnams nyid kyi'o /
prabandhānyathātvam ity upapattibhavād yāvanmaraṇabhavaḥ
# rgyun gzhan du 'gyur ba'o zhes bya ba ni skye ba'i srid pa nas 'chi ba'i srid pa'i bar du ste /
tatrāntare hetuphalabhāvenāvasthitānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ nairantaryeṇotpādaḥ prabandha ucyate
# bar der rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos por gnas pa'i 'du byed rnams rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ba la rgyun ces bya'o /
tasyānyathā cānyathā ca bhāvo 'nyathātvam / tathā hikalalāvasthāto 'rbudāvasthety evaṃ yāvan vṛddhāvasthā
# de'i gzhan dang gzhan du gyur pa'i dngos po ni gzhan du 'gyur ba ste; 'di ltar nur nur po'i dus las mer mer por 'gyur ba'i dus dang de bzhin du dar la bab pa'i dus las rgas pa'i dus kyi bar du'o /
kalalādyavasthāsv api pūrvasmād uttarasya pratikṣaṇamnyathābhāvo vācyaḥ / evaṃ ca prabandhānyathātvejarāprajñaptiḥ naikasya kṣaṇasya nāpy arthāntarabhūteti
# nur nur po la sogs pa'i dus rnams la yang snga ma las phyi mar 'gyur ba'i skad cig re re la gzhan du 'gyur ba zhes brjod do / / de ltar na rgyun gzhan du 'gyur ba la rga ba gdags te / / skad cig gcig la yang ma yin pa don gzhan du 'gyur ba yang med do /
sthitis tathaivateṣāṃ prabandhānuvṛttiriti
# gnas pa gang zhe na / / de ltar de dag gi rgyun rgyud chags pa'o zhes bya ba la /
tathaivety ekasmin nikāyasabhāge
# de ltar zhes bya ba ni ris mthun pa gcig na'o /
ā maraṇāt saṃskārāṇāṃprabandhavṛttau sthitir iti prajñaptiḥ naikasya kṣaṇasya nāpyarthāntarabhūteti jñāpitaṃ bhavati / nityatā tathaivateṣāṃ prabandhoparamaḥ
# shi ba la thug gi bar du 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun rgyud chags pa la gnas pa gdags te / / skad cig gcig la yang mi bya zhing don gzhan du gyur pa yang med par bstan pa yin no /
tathaiva teṣām ity ekasmin nikāyasabhāge saṃskārāṇāṃprabandhoparame 'nityatā prajñapyate / na pratikṣaṇaṃ nāpyarthāntarabhūte tad bhavati
# mi rtag pa nyid gang zhe na / / de ltar de dag ni rgyun 'chad pa'i zhes bya ba la de ltar de dag gi zhes bya ba ni ris mthun pa gcig tu 'du byed rnams kyi rgyun chad pa la mi rtag pa gdags te / / skad cig re re la yang ma yin zhing don gzhan du gyur pa yang med par bstan pa yin no /
prabandhoparamas tv atramaraṇaṃ veditavyam
# rgyun chad pa ni 'dir 'chi ba la bya bar rig par bya'o /
nanu ca bāhyasyāpi rūpasyajātijarāsthityanityatāḥ santi
# phyi rol gyi gzugs la yang skye ba dang rga ba dang gnas pa dang mi rtag pa nyid yod par nges na /
tat kimarthaṃ nikāyasabhāga evasaṃskārasantānasya jātyādaya uktāḥ na bāhyasya rūpasyeti
# ci'i phyir ris mthun pa nyid kyi 'du byed kyi rgyun la skye ba la sogs par bshad kyi / / phyi rol gyi gzugs kyi ni ma yin zhe na /
yānīmāni bhagavatā saṃskṛtalakṣaṇānīty uktāni jātir jarāsthitir anityatā ca tāni sattvākhyān eva saṃskārān ādhikṛtya nabāhyān iti jñāpanārtham
# bcom ldan 'das kyis 'du byas kyi mtshan nyid skye ba dang rga ba dang gnas pa dang mi rtag pa nyid gang dag bshad pa de dag ni sems can du brjod pa nyid kyi 'du byed kyi dbang du mdzad pa yin gyi /
kasmāt punar bhagavatā ubhayeṣāmapi tulye jātisattveupāttān eva saṃskārān adhikṛtyasaṃskṛtalakṣaṇāny uktāni
# phyi rol gyi ma yin par bstan pa'i phyir ro / / gnyi ga la yang skye ba la sogs pa yod par mtshungs na zin pa'i 'du byed kyi dbang du mdzad de / / bcom ldan 'das kyis 'du byed kyi mtshan nyid bshad pa ci'i phyir zhe na /
bāhyaṃ hi rūpaṃ saṃvartavivartaprabhāvitam ādhyātmikās tu saṃskārājātijarādiprabhāvitāḥ
# phyi rol gyi gzugs ni 'jig pa dang chags bas rab tu phye ba yin la / / nang gi 'du byed rnams ni skye ba dang rga ba la sogs pas rab tu phye ba'i phyir ro /
etad uktaṃ bhavati vināśotpādaubāhyasya rūpasya saṃvartavivartaśabdena loke prasiddhāv itibhagavatāpi lokam anuvartamānena tathaivoktau na jātyādiśabdena
# de ni 'di skad du 'jig rten na phyi'i gzugs kyi 'jig pa dang skye ba la 'jig pa dang chags pa'i sgrar grags pas bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'jig rten dang mthun par de skad du bshad de / / skye ba la sogs pa'i sgrar ni ma yin no / / nang gi 'du byed rnams ni skyes so / / rgas so /
ādhyātmikās tu saṃskārā jātijarādiprabhāvitāḥ jātā jīrṇāḥ sthitā vinaṣṭā iti teṣāṃ bhagavatāpilokānuvṛttyotpādādayo jātyādiśabdena nirdiṣṭā iti / nāmakāyādharmāṇāṃ
# gnas so / / zhig go zhes skye ba dang rga ba la sogs pas rab tu phye ba yin te / / bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'jig rten dang mthun par de dag gi 'byung ba la sogs pa la skye ba la sogs pa'i sgrar bstan to zhes bshad pa yin no / / ming gi tshogs gang zhe na /
svabhāvādhivacanāni / abhidheyam abhidheyaṃ pratijñānaṃ nāmayatīti nāma / tat punar artheṣu kṛtāvadhivarṇasamudāyaḥ
# chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid kyi tshig bla dags so zhes bya ba ni brjod par bya ba dang brjod pa la rnam par shes pa gzhol bar byed pas ming ngo / / de yang don rnams la brda sprod ba'i yi ge 'dus pa ste /
nāmnāṃ varṇānāṃ vā samudāyonāmakāyaḥ / dharmāṇāṃ svarūpasyānākhyeyatvād adhyāropyavacanam adhivacanam / svabhāvaḥ svalakṣaṇam
# ming ngam yi ge rnams 'dus pa la ming gi tshogs zhes bya'o / / chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid brjod du med pa'i phyir sgro btags pa'i tshig la tshig bla dags zhes bya'o /
yenānabhilapyasvarūpāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ svarūpaṃ dyotyatetad abhidhānaṃ nāmety ucyate tadyathā cakṣuḥ śrotraṃrūpaṃ śabda iti
# ngo bo nyid ni rang gi mtshan nyid do / / chos rnams kyi rang gi ngo bo brjod du med kyang gang gis rang gi ngo bo gsal bar byed pa'i brjod pa de ming zhes bya ste / / dper na mig rna ba gzugs sgra zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
padakāyādharmāṇāṃ viśeṣādhivacanāni / padyate 'nena saviśeṣo 'rtha iti padam
# tshig gi tshogs gang zhe na / / chos rnams kyi khyad par gyi tshig bla dags so zhes bya ba ni 'dis khyad par gyi don shes par byed pas tshig ste /
evaṃ nāmno laukikācca padāt padaṃ viśeṣitaṃ bhavati
# de lta na ming dang 'jig rten pa'i tshig las tshig bye brag tu byas pa yin no /
nāmapadayoḥvarṇasamudāyātmakatvāviśeṣe 'py arthaviśeṣād viśeṣaḥ / dharmāṇāṃ svabhāvādhivacanaṃ nāma viśeṣādhivacanaṃpadam / svabhāvādhiṣṭhānatvād viśeṣasya pūrvaṃsvabhāvādhivacanam / viśeṣaḥ punar anityatādiko'nuvṛttivyāvṛttyātmakaḥ / anyatrāvartamānaṃ svabhāvaṃviśinaṣṭīti viśeṣaḥ tadyathā anityāḥ sarvasaṃskārāḥsarvadharmā anātmānaḥ śāntaṃ nirvāṇam
# ming dang tshig gnyis yi ge 'dus pa'i bdag nyid yin par bye brag med kyang don gyi bye brag gis bye brag tu dbye ste / / chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid kyi tshig bla dags ni ming yin la / / khyad par gyi gzhi ni ngo bo nyid yin pas sngar ngo bo nyid kyi tshig bla dags smos so / / khyad par ni mi rtag pa la sogs pa'o / / 'jug pa dang ldog pa'i bdag nyid dang gzhan du mi snyegs pa'i ngo bo nyid las bye brag tu byed pa ni khyad par te / / dper na 'du byed thams cad ni mi rtag pa'o / / cho thams cad ni bdag med pa'o / / ya ngan las 'das pa ni zhi ba'o zhes bya ba lta bu'o /
etad uktaṃ bhavati vastusvabhāvābhidhānamātraṃ nāmaviśiṣṭavastusvabhāvābhidhānaṃ padam iti / śeṣaṃ tunāmavyākhyānato vijñeyam / vyañjanakāyāakṣarāṇi / tadubhayābhivyañjanatām upādāya / vyajyate'neneti vyañjanam
# de ni 'di skad du dngos po'i ngo bo nyid brjod pa tsam ni ming yin la / / dngos po'i ngo bo nyid kyi khyad par brjod pa ni tshig yin no zhes bstan pa yin no / / lhag ma ni ming bshad pa bzhin du shes par bya'o / / yi ge'i tshogs gang zhe na / / yi ge rnams te de gnyi ga gsal bar byed pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni 'dis gsal bar byed pas yi ge'o /
vyañjanānāṃ kāyo vyañjanakāyaḥkāyagrahaṇaṃ sarvavyañjanopādānārtham / tacchabdāt kevalādanantarasyaiva sambandha āśaṅkyeta / ubhayaśabdād api kevalāt katamasyobhayasyeti na vijñāyate / ataubhayābhidhānaṃ tadubhayam iti
# yi ge rnams kyi tshogs ni yi ge'i tshogs so / / tshogs smos pa ni yi ge thams cad bsdu ba'i phyir ro / / de zhes bya ba'i sgra 'ba' zhig smos na ni gong ma nyid la sbyor du dgos la / / gnyi ga zhes bya ba nyi tshe smos na yang gnyi ga gang la bya bar gtol med de / / de'i phyir de gnyi ga zhes gnyi ga smos so /
evam anantarasyaivanāmnaḥ padasya cābhivyañjakatvād vyañjanam ity uktaṃbhavati
# de ltar na bshad ma thag pa'i ming dang tshig gsal bar byed pa'i phyir yi ge zhes bshad pa yin no /
kathaṃ punar akṣarair nāmapadayor abhivyañjanam
# ji ltar na yi ge rnams kyis ming dang tshig gsal bar byed ce na /
akṣareṣu samuditeṣu svabhāvaviśeṣādhivacanāvasthāṃ gateṣu nāmapadaprajñapanāt
# ngo bo nyid dang khyad par gyi tshig bla dags kyi gnas skabs su gyur pa'i yi ge 'dus pa rnams la ming dang tshig gdags pa'i phyir te /
evam akṣarair nāmapadābhivyañjanāakṣarāṇi na vāgvijñaptisvabhāvāni
# de ltar na yi ge rnams kyis ming dang tshig gsal bar byed do / / yi ge rnams kyi ngag gi rnam par rig byed kyi ngo bo nyid ma yin te /
akārādayovarṇā itiprasiddhaṃ loke
# yi ge la sogs pa ni brjod pa'o zhes 'jig rten na grags so; /
te punarnāmapadāśrayatvenārthasaṃvarṇanād varṇā / ucyante / yadavastheṣv artheṣu vyutpādyante tadavastheṣv eva nāmapadayoḥ prajñaptir iti te tadāśrayatvenocyante
# de dag ni ming dang tshig gnas kyis don yang dag par brjod pa'i phyir brjod pa zhes bya'o / / don gyi gnas gang dag la bstan pa'i gnas de dag la ming dang tshig gdags pas de dag ni de'i gnas zhes bya'o /
akṣaratvaṃ punas teṣāṃ paryāyākṣaraṇatām
# yi ge yang de dag gi rnam grangs su gtogs pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar byed pa'i phyir te /
upādāya / tathā hi cakṣurnetrādiparyāyāntareṣukṣarati / abhidheyatvena paryāyāntarair gamyata ity arthaḥ / na punarevam akārasya paryāyāntaram asti yenākārābhidhānaṃmuktvākāro gamyeta
# 'di ltar mig dang 'dren byed ces bya ba la sogs pa ni rnam grangs su gtogs pa gzhan dag tu 'gyur ba ste / / brjod par bya ba nyid rnam gangs su gtogs pa gzhan rnams kyis shes so zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / gang gis aa zhes brjod pa ma gtogs par aa zhes bya ba shes par 'gyur ba aa zhes bya ba'i rnam grangs de lta bu gzhan med do /
etāvac ca sarvaṃ yad uta svabhāvoviśeṣas tadubhayavyavahāraś ca
# thams cad ni 'di lta ste / / ngo bo nyid dang khyad par dang de gnyi ga'i tha snyad tsam du zad de /
tat sarvam ebhiranuvyavahriyata ity ata ete nāmapadavyañjanakāyāvyavasthāpitā iti
# de dag thams cad ni 'di dag gis rjes su tha snyad gdags pa yin pas de'i phyir ming dang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs de dag rnam par gzhag go; /
evam anyeṣām api viprayuktānāṃnāmapadavyañjanakāyavat prayojanāpekṣayā vyavasthānaṃveditavyam
# de bzhin du ldan pa ma yin pa gzhan dag kyang tshig dang yi ge'i tshogs bzhin du dgos pa la ltos nas rnam par gzhag par rig par bya'o /
pṛthagjanatvam āryadharmāṇām alābhaiti / yasya dharmasya yogāt pṛthagjana ity ākhyāyate tatpṛthagjanatvam / ārād yātāḥ pāpakebhyo 'kuśalebhyodharmebhya ity āryāḥ / te punaḥ śaikṣā aśaikṣāḥ / teṣāṃ dharmādarśanabhāvanāśaikṣamārgāḥ
# so so'i skye bo nyid gang zhe na / / 'phags pa'i chos rnams ma thob pa'o zhes bya ba ni chos gang dang ldan na so so'i skye bo zhes brjod pa de so so'i skye bo nyid do / / sdig pa mi dge ba'i chos rnams las ring du song bas 'phags pa rnams so / / de dag kyang slob pa dang mi slob pa rnams te / / de dag gi chos rnams ni mthong ba dang bsgom pa dang mi slob pa'i lam rnams te /
teṣām alābhaḥ pṛthagjanatvam
# de dag ma thob pa ni so so'i skye bo nyid do /
alābhaḥ punar atrāryadharmāṇām anutpādaḥ
# ma thob pa ni 'dir 'phags pa'i chos ma skyes pa ste /
tathā hyanutpannāryadharmaḥ sattvasantānaḥ pṛthagjana ity ucyate
# 'di ltar 'phags pa'i chos ma skyes pa'i sems can gyi rgyud la so so'i skye bo zhes bya'o /
āryadharmotpādāt tv ārya iti / pravṛttiḥ katamā / hetuphalaprabandhānupacchedaḥ pravṛttirity ucyate / naikasmin kṣaṇe prabandhoparame vāpravṛttyupacāraḥ / pratiniyamaḥ katamaḥ / hetuphalanānātve pratiniyamavyavasthā
# 'phags pa'i chos skyes pa la ni 'phags pa zhes bya'o / / 'jug pa gang zhe na / / rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyun mi 'chad pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ste / / skad cig gcig la'am / / rgyun chad pa la ni 'jug pa gdags pa ma yin no / / so sor nge pa gang zhe na / / rgyu dang 'bras bu tha dad pa nyid la so sor nges pa rnam par gzhag ste /
hetuphalanānātvaṃ punar iṣṭasya viṣayasya sucaritam aniṣṭasya duścaritam ityādi phalānāṃpṛthag anyonyahetutā / yogaḥ katamaḥ / hetuphalānurūpye yoga iti prajñaptiḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bu tha dad pa yang 'dod pa'i yul gyi ni legs par spyad pa'o / / mi 'dod pa ni nyes par spyad ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i ni 'bras bu so so ba rnams kyi rgyu tha dad pa'o / / 'byor ba gang zhe na / / rgyu dang 'bras bu 'tsham pa la 'byor pa gdags te /
tadyathādānasya bhogasampad anurūpeti yujyate dānasya bhogasampat phalaṃ / sjavaḥ katamaḥ
# dper na sbyin pa ni longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa dang 'tsham par rigs par sbyin pa'i 'bras bu ni longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa lta bu'o / / mgyogs pa gang zhe na /
hetuphalāśupravṛttau java iti prajñaptiḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bu myur du 'byung ba la mgyogs pa zhes gdags so /
anukramaḥ katamaḥ
# go rims gang zhe na /
hetuphalaikaikapravṛttāv anukrama itiprajñaptiḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bu re re nas 'byung ba la go rims zhes gdags te /
kaikatvena pravṛttir ayugapatpravṛttiḥkālaḥ katamaḥ
# re re nas 'byung gi cig car du 'byung ba ni ma yin no / / dus gang zhe na /
hetuphalaprabandhapravṛttau kāla itiprajñaptiḥ / hetuphalayoḥ prabandhena pravṛttau satyāṃ yattatra hetuphalam utpannaniruddham so 'tītaḥ kāla itiprajñapyate
# rgyu dang 'bras bu rgyun du 'byung ba la dus zhes gdags te / / rgyu dang 'bras bu 'byung ba la de las rgyu dang 'bras bu byung nas 'gags pa gang yin pa de 'das pa'i dus zhes gdags so /
yad anutpannaṃ so 'nāgataḥ
# gang ma byung ba de ma 'ongs pa'i dus so /
yadutpannāniruddhaṃ sapratyutpannaḥ kālaḥ / deśaḥ katamaḥ
# gang byung ba ma 'gags pa de da ltar byung ba'i dus so / / yul gang zhe na /
pūrvadakṣiṇapaścimottarādharordhvāsusarvato daśasu dikṣu hetuphala eva deśa iti prajñaptiḥ
# shar dang lho dang nub dang byang dang 'og dang steng dang phyogs bcu thams cad la rgyu dang 'bras bu yod pa nyid la yul zhes gdags te /
hetuphalasya digvyāptau deśopacāraḥ
# rgyu dang 'bras bus phyogs khyab pa la yul zhes gdags so /
rūpasaṅgṛhītaṃ cahetuphalaṃ veditavyam arūpiṇāṃ digvyāpanāsāmarthyāt
# gzugs su bsdus pa ni rgyu dang 'bras bur rig par bya ste / / gzugs med pa rnams ni phyogs la khyab par byed par mi nus pa'i phyir ro /
saṅkhyā katamā
# grangs gang zhe na /
saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyekaśo bhede saṅkhyetiprajñaptiḥ
# 'du byed rnams kyi so so tha dad pa la grangs zhes gdags te /
bheda ity abhinnaikātmakatvedvitīyasaṅkhyānupapatteḥ
# tha dad pa zhes bya ba ni tha dad pa ma yin zhing gcig pa'i bdag nyid la gnyis zhes bya ba grangs mi 'thad pa'i phyir ro /
sāmagrī katamā / hetupratyayasamavadhāne sāmagrītiprajñaptiḥ
# tshogs pa gang zhe na / / rgyu dang rkyen 'dus pa la tshogs pa zhes gdags so /
evam ete cittaviprayuktāḥsaṃskārā dharmāṇāmavasthāviśeṣeṣu prajñapyanta iti prajñaptisanto veditavyāḥ / uktaḥ saṃskāraskandhaḥ
# de ltar na sems dang ldan pa ma yin pa'i 'du byed 'di dag ni chos rnams kyi gnas skabs kyi khyad par la gdags pas rtags yod par rig par bya'o / / 'du byed kyi phung po bshad zin to /
saṃskāraskandhānantaraṃvijñānaskandho veditavya ity ata āha vijñānaskandhaḥ
# 'du byed kyi phung po'i 'og tu rnam par shes pa'i phung po bshad par bya ste / / de'i phyir rnam par shes pa gang zhe na /
katama iti / ālambanavijñaptirity ālambanaṃ cittacaittaviṣayaḥ
# dmigs pa rnam par rig pa'o zhes bya ba smras so / / dmigs pa ni sems dang sems las byung ba'i yul te /
sa punaḥṣaṭprakāraḥ rūpaṃ yāvad dharmāḥ
# de yang gzugs nas chos kyi bar du rnam pa drug go /
tasya vijñaptirgrahaṇam avabodhaḥ pratipattir ityarthaḥ
# de yang rnam par rig pa ni 'dzin pa dang rtog pa dang khong du chud pa zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
sā punaḥṣaṭ pravṛttivijñānāni cakṣurvijñānaṃ yāvanmanovijñānaṃ
# de ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug ste mig gi rnam par shes pa nas yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o /
tatracakṣurvijñānaṃ cakṣurindriyāśrayārūpaprativijñaptiḥ
# de la mig gi rnam par shes pa ni mig gi dbang po la brten nas yul so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
evaṃ yāvan manovijñānaṃmanaindriyāśrayā sarvadharmaprativijñaptiḥ
# de bzhin du yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i bar du yang yid kyi dbang po la brten nas chos thams cad so sor rnam par rig pa'o /
vijñānasvarūpam uktvā tatparyāyapradarśanārtham āha cittaṃ mano 'pitad iti / tad vijñānaṃ cittam apy ucyate / mana ity apīti / paryāyārthapradarśanārtham āha citratāṃ manaḥsanniśrayatāṃ copādāyeti / citratāmupādāya cittam ity ucyate / samanantaracittasanniśrayatāmupādāya mana iti
# rnam par shes pa'i rang gi ngo bo bshad nas / / de'i rnam grangs bstan pa'i phyir / / sems dang yid kyang de yin te / / zhes bya ba smos te / / rnam par shes pa de ni sems zhes kyang bya / / yid ces kyang bya'o / / rnam grangs kyi don bstan pa'i phyir / / sna tshogs pa dang yid rten byed pa'i phyir zhes bya ba smos te / / sna tshogs pa'i phyir sems zhes bya'o / / de ma thag pa'i sems kyi rten byed pas yid ces bya'o /
tatrapravṛttivijñānasyālambanaprativijñaptisvarūpatvādālambanasya ca prativijñānam anekākāratvācakṣurādivijñānaṃ citram utpadyate
# de la 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa so sor rig pa'i rang bzhin yin pa dang dmigs pa so sor rnam par rig pa yang rnam pa du ma yin pa'i phyir / / mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa ni sna tshogs zhes bya'o /
ata eva tadindriyāśrayeṇāpy utpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ vijānātīty ucyatenendriyam
# de'i phyir de'i dbang po la brten nas 'byung ba na yul rnam par shes pa zhes bya'i / / dbang po rnams ni ma yin no /
tathāṣaṇṇāṃ cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ yad yannirudhyatetat tad anantarasyavijñānasyotpadyamānasyāśrayabhāvena vyavatiṣṭhata ity ataḥsamanantaracittasanniśrayatām upādāya mana ity ucyate
# 'di ltar mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa drug po gang dang gang 'gags pa de dang de ni de ma thag pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rten gyi dngos por gnas te / / de'i phyir de ma thag pa'i sems kyi rten byed pas yid ces bya'o /
yadetac citratvāc cittam ity uktam taj jātim adhikṛtya nalakṣaṇam
# sna tshogs pa'i phyir sems zhes bya'o zhes gang bshad pa de ni rigs kyi dbang du byas pa yin gyi skad cig la ni ma yin no /
lakṣaṇaṃ tu pratiniyatālambanākāratvān na citramiti na tat prādhānyena cittam / prādhānyena punaś / cittam ālayavijñānam
# skad cig ni dmigs pa so sor nges pa'i rnam pa yin pas sna tshogs zhes mi bya ste / / de ni dngos su sems ma yin no / / dngos su na sems ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ste /
atraiva kāraṇam āha tathāhitac citaṃ sarvasaṃskārabījairiti
# 'dir rgyu bstan pa'i phyir / / 'di ltar de'i 'du byed thams cad kyi sa bon bsags pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
pratikṣaṇaṃ / lsarvasaṃskārabījaiś citatvāc cittam itiprādhānyena tad evacittam
# skad cig re re la 'du byed thams cad kyi sa bon bsags pas sems zhes bya ste / / dngos su na de nyid sems so /
cayas tu paunaḥpunyena bījaparipoṣaḥsaṃskārabījānusyūtir vā
# bsags pa ni yang dang yang sa bon yongs su gsos pa'am / / 'du byed kyi sa bon rjes su 'brel ba'o /
saṃskāro 'tra sāsravā dharmāabhipretāḥ / teṣāṃ punar utpattiś caturbhyaḥ pratyayebhyaḥ
# 'du byed rnams ni 'dir zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos rnams su 'dod de / / de dag kyang rkyen bzhi las 'byung ngo /
tatra hetupratyaya ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā vāsanā
# de la rgyu'i rkyen ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa'i bag chags te /
paunaḥpunyena saṃskārāṇāṃ samudācārād bījapuṣṭir vāsanety ucyate
# yang dang yang 'du byed rnams kun du 'byung bas sa bon brtas pa la bag chags zhes bya'o /
adhipatipratyayaś cakṣurādīnīndriyāṇi / samanantarapratyayaḥ samanantaraniruddhaṃ vijñānam
# bdag po'i rkyen ni mig la sogs pa'i dbang po rnams so / / de ma thag pa'i rkyen ni rnam par shes pa 'gags ma thag pa'o /
ālambanapratyayo rūpādikaḥ
# dmigs pa'i rkyen ni gzugs la sogs pa'o /
tathā hi sūtre 'py uktam cakṣuraparibhinnaṃ bhavati rūpāṇy ābhāsagatāni tajjaś camanasikāraḥ pratyupasthito bhavati evaṃ tajjasya cakṣurvijñānasya prādurbhāvo bhavatīti
# 'di ltar mdo las kyang mig nyams par ma gyur la gzugs rnams kyang snang bar gyur pa dang de skyed pa yid la byed pa yang nye bar gnas par gyur na de las byung ba'i mig gi rnam par shes pa 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so /
evaṃśrotrādivijñāneṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vācyam
# de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la yang ji ltar mthun mthun du brjod par bya'o /
hetupratyayastu sadā sannihitatvād durvijñeyatvāc ca noktaḥ
# rgyu'i rkyen rtag tu gnas pa dang shes par dka' ba'i phyir ma smos so / / de'i 'og tu kun du tshol ba'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa'o /
tadanantaraṃ paryeṣakaṃ manovijñānamparyeṣakād anantaraṃvyavasthāpakam evaṃ vyavasthāpakānantaraṃ vikalpakaṃ manovijñānam utpadyate / tatra ca viṣayāt saṅkliśyatevyavadāyate vā / tadavasthaś ca puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyānsaṃskārāṃś cetanātmakān abhisaṃskaroti
# kun du tshol ba'i 'og tu rnam par 'jog pa'o / / rnam par 'jog pa'i 'og tu rnam par rtog pa'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa 'byung ste; de'i tshe yul las kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bar 'gyur ro / / de'i tshe bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i 'du byed sems pa'i bdag nyid can rnams mngon par 'du byed do /
te 'bhisaṃskṛtānirudhyamānāālayavijñāne vipākavāsanāṃ vā puṣṇantiniṣyandavāsanāṃ vā
# mngon par 'du byas pa de dag 'gag pa na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rnam par smin pa'i bag chags so / / rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags gso bar byed do /
tatra niṣyandavāsanāmāgamyālayavijñānāt puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyāḥ saṃskārāḥpravartante
# de la rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags la brten nas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las bsod nams dang bsod nams ma yin pa dang mi gyo ba'i 'du byed rnams 'byung ngo /
vipākavāsanām āgamyālayavijñānānnikāyasabhāgāntareṣv ālayavijñānam eva vipākātmakaṃnirvartate
# rnam par smin pa'i bag chags la brten nas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid rnam par smin pa'i bdag nyid du 'grub bo /
tatra ye 'py anye 'kuśalāḥ kuśalasāsravāś ca dharmāsteṣām apy ayam eva nayaḥ
# de la mi dge ba dang dge ba zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos gzhan gang yin pa de dag la yang tshul 'di nyid do /
avyākṛtās tu niṣyandavāsanām evapuṣṇanti na vipākavāsanām teṣām avipākatvāt
# lung du ma bstan pa ni rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags nyid gso bar byed kyi / / rnam par smin pa'i bag chags ni ma yin te / / de dag la rnam par smin pa med pa'i phyir ro /
tad evamālayavijñānaṃ dviprakāram
# de ltar na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa de rnam pa gnyis te /
niṣyandavāsanām upādāyakāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca
# rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags la brten nas rgyu dang 'bras bu ste /
tathā hi sarvasaṃskārāḥ svabījādhānevartamānā ālayavijñānātmātiśayahetubhāvena vyavatiṣṭhantaitisarvasaṃskārāṇāṃ tat kāryam
# 'di ltar 'du byed thams cad rang gi sa bon bskyed pa ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa rang bzhin bye brag tu 'gyur ba'i rgyu'i dngos por gnas pas de ni 'du byed rnams kyi 'bras bu'o /
sarvasaṃskārāś catadbījopādānād ālayavijñānād utpadyanta itisarvasaṃskārāṇām ālayavijñānaṃ kāraṇam
# 'du byed thams cad de dag gi sa bon nye bar len pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las 'byung ba'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed thams cad kyi rgyu yin no /
vipākavāsanāṃ tvadhikṛtya kuśalākuśalānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ kāryam eva tatnakāraṇam
# rnam par smin pa'i bag chags kyi dbang du byas te / / dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'du byed rnams kyi 'bras bu yin gyi rgyu ni ma yin no /
kāraṇaṃ tu tad vipākavāsanām upādāyanikāyasabhāgāntareṣu vipākavijñānasyaiveti
# rgyu ni rnam par smin pa'i bag chags la brten nas ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa'i rgyu'o /
pravṛttivijñānaṃ hi rūpaśabdādyālambanatvātsvasāmānyalakṣaṇākāratvāc caparicchinnālambanaṃ paricchinnākāraṃ ca
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa la dmigs pa dang rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid kyi rnam pa yin pa'i phyir dmigs pa yongs su chad pa dang rnam shes yongs su chad pa'o /
ālayavijñānaṃ punaraparicchinnālambanākāram
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa ste /
na hy asyālambanaṃ paricchettuṃ śakyatenākāraḥ / kiṃ kāraṇam
# 'di'i dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su gcad par mi nus so / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
yasmādālayavijñānaṃ dvābhyām ālambanābhyāṃ pravartate
# 'di ltar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni dmigs pa gnyis la 'jug pa ste /
adhyātmam upādānavijñaptitaḥbahirdhāparicchinnākārabhājanavijñaptitaś ca
# nang gi nye bar len pa'i rnam par rig pa dang phyi rol gyi snod la rnam par rig pa rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa'o /
tatrādhyātmamupādānaṃ parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśavāsanā sādhiṣṭhānaṃ cendriyarūpam
# de la nang gi nye bar len pa ni kun brtags pa'i ngo bo nyid la mngon par zhen pa'i bag chags dang gnas dang bcas pa'i dbang po'i gzugs so /
etaccālambanaṃ sūkṣmatvāllokapaṇḍitair apiduravadhāram ity ato 'paricchinnālambanākāram ity ucyate napunar anālambanam eva
# dmigs pa 'di gnyis ni phra ba'i phyir 'jig rten gyi mkhas pa rnams kyis kyang rtogs par dka' bas de'i phyir dmigs pa dang rnam pa yongs su ma chad pa zhes bya'i /
pravṛttivijñānaṃ kuśalakliṣṭāvyākṛtajātīyam ālayavijñānaṃ tvekajātīyam
# dmigs pa med pa nyid ni ma yin no / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa ni dge ba dang nyon mongs pa can dang lung du ma bstan pa'i rang bzhin no / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni rigs gcig pa yin no /
tatra na tāvat kuśalākuśalajātīyaṃ / kuśalākuśalair asamprayogāt
# de la dge ba dang mi dge ba'i rang bzhin ni ma yin te / / de dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
tad dhi pañcabhir evasarvatragaiś caitasaiḥ samprayujyatemanaskārasparśavedanāsañjñācetanābhiḥ
# de ni sems las byung ba kun du 'gro ba yid la byed pa dang reg pa dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa lnga po kho na dang mtshungs par ldan no /
ālayavijñānaṃsasamprayogaṃ pūrvakarmasaṃskārahetukatvād ekāntenavipāka evety avyākṛtajātīyam eva / santānānuvṛtti ca
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas par sngon gyi las kyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung bas gcig tu rnam par smin pa nyid yin pa'i phyir lung du ma bstan pa'i rigs so /
atra hyālayavijñānaṃnikāyasabhāgāntareṣu pratisandhim upādāya yāvac cyutiṃtāvat kṣaṇaprabandhapravāhena vartate na tv antarāntarāvicchidyate pravṛttivijñānavat
# rgyun chags par 'jug pa'o / / de la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu nying mtshams sbyor ba nas bzung ste / / ji tsam na 'chi 'pho ba de'i bar du skad cig rgyun mi 'chad par 'jug gi / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa bzhin du bar skabs bar skabs su chad pa ni ma yin te /
tathā hi cakṣurvijñānānantaraṃśrotrādivijñānāny utpadyante śrotravijñānānantaraṃcakṣurādivijñānāni / evaṃ ghrāṇādivijñānānantaram itivistareṇa vācyam
# 'di ltar mig gi rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu rna ba la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung ba dang rna ba'i rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung ba dang de bzhin du sna la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i 'og tu zhes bya ba rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
tathā kuśalānantaram akuśalam utpadyateakuśalānantaraṃ kuśalam tadubhayānantaram avyākṛtamhīnadhātukānantaraṃ madhyadhātukammadhyadhātukānantaraṃ praṇītadhātukampraṇītadhātukānantaram apraṇītadhātukamapraṇītadhātukānantaraṃ madhyadhātukam iti vistareṇavācyam
# de bzhin du dge ba'i 'og tu mi dge ba 'byung ba dang mi dge ba'i 'og tu dge ba dang de gnyis ka'i 'og tu lung du mi ston pa dang khams dman pa'i 'og tu khams bar ma dang khams bar ma'i 'og tu khams gya nom pa dang khams gya nom pa'i 'og tu gya nom pa ma yin pa dang khams gya nom pa ma yin pa'i 'og tu khams bar ma zhes bya ba rgya cher brjod par bya ste /
nāpy ekaṃ dravyam ā maraṇād anuvartata iti
# shi ba la thug gi bar du rdzas gcig tu 'jug pa ni ma yin no /
ṣaṭprakārapravṛttivijñānavyatiriktam anyad ālayavijñānamastīti katham vijñāyate / āgamato yuktitaś ca
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug po ma gtogs par gzhan kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod par ci mngon zhe na / / lung dang rigs pas mngon no /
tatrāgama uktaṃbhagavatābhidharmasūtre anādikāliko dhātuḥ sarvadharmasamāśrayaḥ
# de la ni 'di ni lung yin te / / bcom ldan 'das kyis chos mngon pa'i mdo las / / thog ma med pa'i dus kyi dbyings / / chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin te /
tasmin sati gatiḥ sarvā nirvāṇādhigamo 'pica
# de yod pas na 'gro kun dang / / mya ngan 'das pa'ang thob par 'gyur / / zhes gsungs so /
punaś ca sandhinirmocane 'py uktam ādānavijñāna gambhīrasūkṣmo ogho yathā vartati sarvabījaḥ / bālāna eṣo mayi na prakāśito mā haiva ātmā parikalpayeyuḥ
# yang dgongs ba nges par 'grel ba'i mdo las kyang / / len pa'i rnam par shes pa zab cing phra / / sa bon thams cad chu bo'i rgyun bzhin 'bab / / bdag tu rtog par gyur na mi rung zhes / / 'di ni byis pa rnams la ngas ma bstan / / zhes gsungs so /
yuktim apy adhikṛtyāha yatonirodhasamāpattyasañjñisamāpattyāsañjñik / ebhyo vyutthitasya punarviṣayavijñaptyākhyaṃ pravṛttivijñānam / utpadyate
# rigs pa'i dbang du byas te / / 'di ltar 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa po rnams las langs nas yang yul rnam par rig pa zhes bya ba 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung /
tad ālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo'rthāntaram iti vākyaśeṣaḥ
# zhes bya ba smos te / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las don gzhan du gyur pa'o zhes bya ba tshig gi lhag ma'o /
nirodhāsañjñisamāpattisamāpannasyāsañjñike ca prādurbhūteniravaśeṣeṣu pravṛttivijñāneṣu niruddheṣu punarvyutthānakālaālayavijñānam antareṇa pravṛttivijñānotpattir na yujyate / na hisamāpatticittāt tasyotpattir yuktā tasya ciraniruddhatvānniruddhasya cāsattvāt asac ca na kāryaṃ na kāraṇaṃpradhānātmādivat / yo 'pi manyate anapāyopādānavikāraṃbhāvasvarūpam / anāgatavartamānātītatvaṃ tu bhāvānāṃkāritradvārakam / tathā hy akurvatkāritro 'nāgataḥkurvatkāritro vartamānaḥ uparatakāritro 'tīta ity ucyate / evaṃtarhi kāritraṃ bhāvād anyad ityabhyupagantavyamatītānāgatāvasthayoḥkāritre 'saty api bhāvābhyupagamāt / evaṃ ca kāritrasyaivotpādo vyayaś ca na bhāvānām abhūtvābhāvād bhūtvā cābhāvāt na carūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām sarvadāsvarūpādhyāsitatvāt
# 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa la snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa par gyur pa na 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ma lus par 'gag pa las yang ldang ba'i tshe kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung du mi rung ngo / / snyoms par 'jug pa'i sems las de 'byung du mi rung ste / / de 'gags nas ring du lon pa dang 'gags pa de med pa'i phyir ro / / med pa ni rgyur yang mi rung 'bras bur yang mi rung ste / / gtso bo dang bdag la sogs pa bzhin no / / gang yang 'di snyam du dngos po'i rang gi ngo bo la skye ba dang 'jig par 'gyur ba'i dngos po med kyi ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar dang 'das pa ni dngos po rnams kyi byed pa'i sgo nas yin te / / 'di ltar bya ba mi byed pa ni ma 'ongs pa'o / / bya ba byed pa ni da ltar ro / / byed ba rgyun chad pa ni 'das pa'o zhes bya'o snyam du sems pa de lta bu yin na ni byed pa las dngos po gzhan yin par khas blang bar bya ste / / 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa gnyis kyi dus na byed pa med kyang dngos po khas len pa'i phyir ro / / de ltar na med pa las byung ba dang byung nas kyang med par 'gyur ba'i phyir 'byung ba dang 'jig pa ni byed pa yin gyi / / dngos po rnams kyis ni ma yin no / / gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams kyis ma yin pa nyid de /
tataś cotpādavyayābhāvān nirodhavannānityā rūpādayaḥ skandhāḥ syuḥ
