# rtag tu rang gi ngo bo dang ldan pa dang de yang 'byung ba dang 'jig pa med ba'i phyir te / / gzugs la sogs pa'i phung po rnams ni 'gog pa bzhin du mi rtag pa ma yin par 'gyur ro /
tataś ca duḥkhā api na syuḥ
# de'i phyir sdug bsngal bar yang mi 'gyur te /
uktaṃ hi sūtre yad anityaṃ tad duḥkhamiti
# mdo las ni mi rtag pa gang yin pa de sdug bsngal ba'o zhes gsungs so /
evaṃ caskandhān anityato duḥkhataś ca cintayato viparyāsa evasyāt
# de lta na ni phung po rnams la ni mi rtag pa nyid dang sdug bsngal ba nyid du sems pa phyin ci log nyid du 'gyur ro /
na ca viparyāsāt kleśaprahāṇaṃ yuktam anitye duḥkhe canityasukhaviparyāsavat
# phyin ci log gis ni nyon mongs pa spang bar mi rigs te / / mi rtag pa dang sdug bsngal ba la rtag pa dang bde bar phyin ci log pa bzhin no /
kāritrasya cotpādavyayasambhavāt saṃskṛtatvam rūpādiṣu ca skandheṣusaṅgrahābhāvāt ṣaṣṭhaḥskandho 'bhyupagantavyaḥ
# byed pa la ni 'byung ba dang 'jig pa yod pas 'dus byas nyid yin te / / gzugs la sogs pa'i phung po rnams su ni ma 'dus pas phung po drug par khas blang bar bya'o /
na ca sāsravā dharmāupādānaskandhaiḥ sarve vā saṃskṛtāḥ skandhaiḥ saṅgṛhītā itivaktavyam
# yang nye bar len pa'i phung po rnams kyis zag pa dang bcas pa'i chos thams cad dang phung po rnams kyis 'dus byas thams cad bsdus so zhes ma zer cig /
anyaḥ punar āha kāritraṃ nāma phalaparigrahaḥ
# yang gzhan na re byed pa zhes bya ba ni 'bras bu yongs su 'dzin pa'o /
dharmo hi yasya dharmasya hetubhāvena vyavatiṣṭhatesa dharmas taṃdharmaṃ phalatvena gṛhṇātīty ato hetubhāvavyavasthānaṃbhāvānāṃ phalaparigrahaḥ / hetubhāvena ca sa eva dharmo vyavatiṣṭhata itidharmebhyaḥ kāritram ananyat
# chos gang zhig chos gang gi rgyu dngos por gnas pa ste / / chos dang chos de 'bras bur 'dzin pa de'i phyir rgyu'i dngos por gnas pa ni dngos po rnams kyi 'bras bu yongs su 'dzin te / / chos de nyid rgyu'i dngos por gnas pas na chos rnams las byed pa gzhan ma yin no /
ataś canānantaroktadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ / ananyo hi nāma sa eva / etad uktaṃ bhavati nānyat kāritraṃ dharmāt kiṃ tarhi dharma eva kāritram / tathā kāritrān nānyo dharmaḥ / kāritram evadharma iti / evaṃ cātītānāgatayor adhvanoḥ kāritravaddharmābhāvaḥ
# de bas na gong du smos pa'i skyon du mi 'gyur ro zhes zer ro / / gzhan ma yin zhes bya ba ni de nyid de / / de ni 'di skad du chos las byed pa gzhan ma yin te / / chos nyid byed pa'o / / de bzhin du byed pa las kyang chos gzhan ma yin te / / byed pa nyid chos yin no zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / de lta na ni 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa gnyis kyis chos rnams byed pa bzhin du med par 'gyur te /
tataś cātītānāgatāstitvavādaḥ parityaktobhavati
# de'i phyir 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa yod do zhes smras pa btang ba yin no /
kāritrasya vā dharmasvarūpavad dharmād ananyatvāttraiyadhvakatvam abhyupagantavyam
# yang na byed pa yang chos kyi rang gi ngo bo bzhin du chos las gzhan ma yin pa'i phyir dus gsum par khas blang dgos te /
evam apikāritreṇādhvāno vyavasthitā iti vādahāniḥ / kāritraṃ ca kurvanvartamāna iṣyate / anyac cānyena kriyate na svātmanaivatasya kṛtatvāt / akṛtaṃ ca kriyate na kṛtam
# de lta na yang byed pa las dus rnams rnam par gzhag par smra ba nyams par 'gyur ro / / bya ba byed pa ni da ltar du 'dod de / / gzhan ni gzhan gyis byed pa la / / de byas zin pa'i phyir bdag nyid kyis ni ma yin no / / ma byas pa ni byed dgos kyi byas zin pa la ni ma yin no /
ataś cadharmakāritrayoḥ kṛtākṛtatvāt spaṣṭam anyatvam / tasmātpūrvoktadoṣas tadavastha eva
# de'i phyir byed pa dang chos gnyis ni byas pa dang ma byas pa ma yin pas tha dad par mngon no; / / de lta bas na gong du smos pa'i skyon de yod do /
dharmakāritrayoś cānanyatvehetuphalābhāvaprasaṅgaḥ
# chos dang byed pa gnyis kyang tha dad pa ma yin na ni rgyu dang 'bras bu med par 'gyur te /
tathā hi phalasya kāraṇavat pūrvameva pariniṣpannatvāt phalasya kiṃ kurvat kāraṇaṃ bhavatiakurvad vā kathaṃ kāraṇam / phalam api tenākriyamāṇaṃkathaṃ tasya kāryaṃ bhavati
# 'di ltar 'bras bu yang rgyu bzhin du thog ma nyid nas yongs su grub pa'i phyir 'bras bu la ji zhig byed na rgyur 'gyur / / mi byed na yang rgyu zhes ji skad du bya 'bras bu yang des ma byas na de'i 'bras bur ji ltar 'gyur /
kāritrāṇām eva ca parasparatohetuphalabhāvaḥ na dharmāṇām
# byed pa rnams nyid phan tshun rgyu dang 'bras bu'i dngos por 'gyur gyi / / chos rnams kyi ni ma yin te /
tathā hi kāritre satikāritrāntaraṃ bhavatināsati
# 'di ltar byed pa yod na byed pa gzhan 'byung gi med na ni ma yin te /
na tu dharmasvarūpam nāpidharmasvarūpād dharmasvarūpam sarvadāstitvāt / tathā cayasmin sati yad bhavati asati ca na bhavatitat tasya kāraṇamitarac ca kāryam
# chos kyi rang bzhin la ni ma yin no / / chos kyi rang bzhin las kyang chos kyi rang bzhin ma yin te / / rtag tu yod pa'i phyir ro / / de ltar na gang yod na gang 'byung gi med na ni mi 'byung ba de ni de'i rgyu yin no /
lokaprasiddham etat / evaṃ ca nadharmasvarūpaṃ kāraṇaṃ na kāryam iti lokaśāstravirodhaḥ / kāritraṃ dharmasya tattvānyatvenāvācyam ity anye / kimarthaṃ tattvenāvācyam / dharmasvabhāvaṃ na bhavatīti
# cig shos ni 'bras bu yin no zhes bya ba 'di ni 'jig rten gyi grags pa'o / / de ltar na chos kyi rang bzhin ni rgyu yang ma yin 'bras bu yang ma yin pa ni 'jig rten pa dang bstan bcos dang 'gal lo / / gzhan dag na re chos rnams las byed pa de nyid dang gzhan du brjod par bya ba ma yin no zhes zer te / / ci'i phyir de nyid ces mi brjod ce na / / chos kyi rang bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir ro; /
kimartham anyatvena nocyate / anyasvabhāvam api tan naivetyanyatvenāpi nocyate
# ci'i phyir gzhan zhes mi brjod ce na / / chos kyi rang bzhin de'i ngo bo nyid yang ma yin pas gzhan zhes mi bya'o /
evaṃ tarhi yan na tatsvabhāvaṃ nānyasvabhāvam tac chaśaviṣāṇavan niḥsvabhāvatvān nāstyeveti / katham avidyamānam adhvavyavasthānimittaṃbhaviṣyati
# de lta na ni gang de'i ngo bo nyid kyang ma yin la gzhan gyi ngo bo nyid kyang ma yin pa de ni ri bong gi rva bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa'i phyir med pa nyid yin te / / med pa ni dus rnam par gzhag pa'i rgyur ji ltar 'gyur /
evaṃ kāritrāt sarvathāpy adhvavyavasthā nasidhyati / tasmād anutpanno bhāvo 'nāgataḥ niruddho 'tītaḥutpannāniruddho vartamāna ity abhyupeyam
# de ltar na byed pa las dus rnam par gzhag pa ni rnam pa thams cad du mi 'grub bo / / de lta bas na dngos po ma byung ba ni ma 'ongs pa yin / / 'gags pa ni 'das pa yin / / byung lam 'gags pa ni de ltar yin par khas blang bar bya'o /
na punar akurvatkāritro 'nāgataḥ kurvatkāritro vartamānaḥuparatakāritro 'tīta iti
# bya ba mi byed pa ni ma 'ongs pa / / bya ba byed pa ni da ltar / / byed pa rgyun chad pa ni 'das pa'o zhes khas blang bar mi bya'o /
anyaḥ punar āha sendriyaṃ rūpaṃ cittaṃ cānyonyabījakamity ato nirodhāsañjñisamāpattibhyām asañjñikāc cavyuttiṣṭhataḥ sendriyād rūpāc cittam utpadyate
# yang gzhan dag na re dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs dang sems ni gcig gi sa bon gcig yin te / / de'i phyir 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa las ldang ba na dbang po dang bcas ba'i gzugs las sems 'byung ste /
yathārūpyadhātoś cyavamānasya cittād eva ciraniruddham api sendriyaṃ rūpam utpadyata iti / tasmān nātra kiñcid ālayavijñānena prayojanam iti
# dper na gzugs med pa'i khams nas 'chi 'pho ba'i sems las kyang 'gags nas ring du lon ba dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs 'byung ba lta bu'o / / de lta bas na 'di la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ca dgos zhes zer te /
evaṃ tarhy ekaikasya sattvasyadvau cittasantānau syātām / ekaḥ sendriyād rūpāt aparaś cittāt
# de ltar na sems can re re'i sems kyi rgyud kyang gnyis gnyis su 'gyur te / / gcig ni dbang po dang bcas pa'i gzugs las byung / / cig shos ni sems las 'byung bar 'gyur ro /
ārūpyeṣu ca nirodhasamāpannasya rūpābhāvādvyutthānābhāvaḥ
# gzugs med pa'i sems su 'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa ni gzugs med pas ldang ba yang med do /
tataś cāsya parinirvāṇam eva syād ityakalpaneyam
# de'i phyir 'di ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa nyid du 'gyur bas rtog pa 'di ni mi rung ngo /
ekaṃ ca kāraṇaṃ svasattādhyāsitaṃ nirīhamanityaṃ śaktaṃ ceṣyate na viparyāsāt
# rgyu ni bdag yod pa dang ldan zhing gyo ba med la mi rtag cing nus pa yod pa gcig pur 'dod kyi / / bzlog pa ni ma yin no /
tathā hy uktaṃbhagavatā asmin satīdaṃ bhavati asyotpādād idamutpadyate / yad utāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti / tasmān na nityohetuḥ nāpy asan na sadvyāpāro nāpy aśaktaiti / ālayavijñānaṃhi sarvasaṃskṛtadharmabījānugatam ā maraṇāt santānavṛtticety ālayavijñānād evācittakāvasthāto vyuttiṣṭhataḥpravṛttivijñānam utpadyata iti
# de skad du bcom ldan 'das kyis kyang 'di yod pa'i phyir 'di 'byung / / 'di skye ba'i phyir 'di skye ste / / 'di ltar ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis 'du byed rnams zhes gsungs te / / de lta bas na rgyu rtag pa ma yin zhing med pa yang ma yin la / / byed pa yod pa yang ma yin zhing nus pa med pa yang ma yin no / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni 'dus byas kyi chos thams cad kyi sa bon dang ldan pa ste / / shi ba la thug gi bar du rgyun chags par 'byung ba'o / / sems med pa'i gnas las ldang ba na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid las 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung ste /
sūtre ca nirodhasamāpannasyavijñānaṃ kāyād anapakrāntamity uktam / na cālayavijñānādanyasya nirodhasamāpattyavasthāyāṃ vijñānasya kāyādanapakramo yujyate / kiṃ kāraṇam
# mdo las kyang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa lus las mi 'da'o zhes gsungs so / / snyoms par zhugs pa'i dus na rnam par shes pa lus las mi 'da' ba ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan mi rung ngo / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
nirodhasamāpannasyālayavijñānād yadyanyavijñānasamudācāra iṣyate tataś catrayāṇāṃ sannipātaḥsparśaḥ sparśasahajā vedanā sañjñā cetaneti sūtre vacanātsañjñāvedanayor api samudācāro 'bhyupagantavyaḥ
# gal te 'gog pa la snyoms par zhugs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan zhig kun du 'byung bar 'dod na / / de lta na ni gsum 'dus pa'i rig pa dang reg pa dang lhan cig skyes pa'i tshor ba dang 'du shes dang sems pa zhes mdo las gsungs pa'i phyir 'du shes dang tshor ba gnyis kyang kun du 'byung bar khas blang dgos so /
tataś cavedanāsañjñāsadbhāvāt sañjñāveditanirodha eva na syāt
# de'i phyir 'du shes dang tshor ba yod pas 'du shes dang tshor ba 'gog pa nyid du mi 'gyur ro /
yo 'pimanyate sūtrevedanāpratyayā tṛṣṇāuktā na ca sarvā vedanātṛṣṇāyāḥ pratyayaḥ
# gang yang mdo las tshor ba'i rkyen gyis sred pa zhes gsungs pa yang tshor ba thams cad sred pa'i rkyen ma yin te /
evaṃ sparśo 'pi na sarvaḥsañjñāvedanāpratyaya iti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ / naitad evam
# de bzhin du reg pa thams cad kyang 'du shes dang tshor ba'i rkyen ma yin pas nyes pa med do snyam du sems pa de yang de lta ma yin te /
viśeṣitā hivedanā sūtrāntare avidyāsaṃsparśajaṃ veditaṃpratītyotpannā tṛṣṇeti / na tv evaṃ kvacit sparśo viśeṣita ity asamānam etat
# mdo gzhan las ma rig pa dang ldan pa'i reg pa las byung ba'i tshor ba la brten nas sred pa 'byung zhes bye brag tu mdzad kyi reg pa ni gang du yang de ltar bye brag mi mdzad pa 'di mtshungs pa ma yin no /
tasmād avaśyam ālayavijñānād evasarvabījakāt sarvāsv avasthāsu santānena vartamānānnirodhāsañjñisamāpattyāsañjñikebhyo vyutthānacittamutpadyata ity abhyupeyam
# de lta bas na 'gog pa dang 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa dang 'du shes med pa pa rnams las ldang ba na gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pas sa bon thams cad gnas skabs kun du 'byung ba las skye bar khas blang bar bya'o /
punaś cālambanapratyayāpekṣāṃ prakārāntaravṛttitām upādāyapravṛttivijñānād / ālayavijñānam anyad iti pratipattavyam / upādāyety ante 'padiṣṭam ihāpi sambadhyate
# dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid kyi phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yod par khong du chud par bya'o / / phyir ro zhes tha mar bstan pa ni 'dir yang sbyar ro /
ālambanapratyayaḥ pañcānāṃcakṣurādivijñānānāṃ rūpādayaḥ pañca viṣayāḥmanovijñānasya sarvadharmāḥ
# dmigs pa'i rkyen ni mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa lnga dang yul gzugs la sogs pa lnga'i yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i chos thams cad do /
rūpādyākārāc chabdādyākāraḥ prakārāntaram
# gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam pa las sgra la sogs pa'i rnam pa ni rnam pa gzhan no /
evaṃ śabdādyākārād rūpādyākāraḥ / pītādyākārān nīlādyākāraḥ prakārāntaram
# de bzhin du sgra la sogs pa'i rnam pa las gzugs la sogs pa'i rnam pa dang ser po la sogs pa'i rnam pa las sngon po la sogs pa'i rnam pa ni rnam pa gzhan no /
evaṃ sarvatravistareṇa vācyam
# de ltar kun du yang rgya cher brjod par bya'o /
prakārāntareṇa vṛttir ātmalābho'syavijñānasyeti tad vijñānaṃ prakārāntaravṛtti / tadbhāvaḥprakārāntaravṛttitā
# rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa bdag thob pa ni rnam par shes pa 'di'i yin pas rnam par shes pa de ni rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa ste de yod pas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid do /
ālambanapratyayāpekṣā kāraṇaṃ yasyāḥprakārāntaravṛttitāyāḥ sālambanapratyayāpekṣā tādṛśīṃprakārāntaravṛttitām upādāya gṛhītvā pravṛttivijñānād anyadālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānabījabhūtam astīti vijñāyate
# de dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos pa'i rgyus rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa gang gi yin pad de dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltos nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid do / / nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni bzung nas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yod par shes so /
atrahi vijñānaṃ pratyavabhāsabhedāt parasparato bhidyate nasamanantarādhipatipratyayabhedāt / ata etad evam uktam ālambanapratyayāpekṣāṃ prakārāntaravṛttitām upādāya
# 'dir ni rnam par shes pa rnams dmigs pa so sor snang ba tha dad pas phan tshun tha dad kyi de ma thag pa dang bdag po'i rkyen tha dad pas ni ma yin no / / de'i phyir 'di skad du dmigs pa'i rkyen la ltas nas rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bshad do /
sācaprakārāntaravṛttitā yathā nālambananirapekṣā yujyate tathāhetupratyayanirapekṣāpi naiva yujyate
# rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa nyid de yang ji ltar dmigs pa la mi ltos par mi rung ba de bzhin du rgyu'i rkyen la mi ltos par mi rung ba nyid do /
yaś ca yeṣāṃ bījairanugataḥ sa teṣāṃ hetupratyayaḥ
# gang dag gi sa bon rnams dang ldan pa gang yin pa de ni de dag gi spyi'i rkyen te /
na ca pravṛttivijñānānāṃparasparabījatvaṃ yujyate kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtānāṃhīnamadhyapraṇītadhātūnāṃ laukikalokottarāṇāṃsāsravānāsravāṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ paryāyeṇa bhāvāt
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ni gcig gi sa bon du gcig mi rung ngo / / dge ba dang mi dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa rnams dang dman pa dang 'bring dang gya nom pa'i khams pa rnams dang 'jig rten pa rnams dang 'jig rten las 'das pa rnams dang zag pa dang bcas pa dang zag pa med pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams la rim pa yod pa'i phyir ro / / de nyid kyi bag chags bsgo ba yang ma mthong la /
na hitenaiva tasya vāsanā dṛṣṭā nāpy anyenabhinnakālenāsambaddhena vā kiṃ tarhi sahotpādavināśair evapuṣpādibhis tilādīnāṃ vāsanā dṛṣṭā
# gzhan gyi dus gzhan na yang ma yin zhing 'brel pa med par yang ma yin no / / 'on kyang lhan cig 'byung ba dang 'jig pa nyid kyi me tog la sogs pas 'bru mar rnams la bsgo bar mthong ste /
ato vipākavāsanāvijñānena samakālaṃ tata evotpadyamānāninirudhyamānāni capravṛttivijñānāni svānurūpakāryotpādanasamarthaṃvipākavijñānaṃ kurvanti
# de'i phyir rnam par smin pa'i bag chags kyi rnam par shes pa dang dus mtshungs pa de nyid las 'byung ba dang 'gag pa ni 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams rang dang mthun pa'i 'bras bu skyed nus ba rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa la byed do /
tasya sāmarthyaṃ vāsanety ucyate
# de'i nus pa ni bag chags zhes bya'o /
taiś ca prakārāntaravṛttibhiḥ pravṛttivijñānair vāsitādvipākavijñānāt punar apy ālambanāpekṣāṇi kuśalākuśalādiprakārāntaravṛttīni pravṛttivijñānāny utpadyantaity avaśyam abhyupagantavyam / tataś ca vipākavijñānaṃsarvasaṃskṛtadharmabījānugataṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo 'nyad itisiddham
# 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa dang dus rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa de dag gis bsras [?] pa rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa las yang dmigs pa la ltos pa dge ba dang mi dge ba la sogs pa'i rnam pa gzhan du 'jug pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung bar gdon mi za bar khas blang bar bya'o / / de'i phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa 'dus byas kyi chos thams cad kyi sa bon dang ldan pa gzhan yin par grub pa'o /
chinnapunarvṛttitāṃ copādāyālayavijñānaṃ pravṛttivijñānebhyo 'nyad astīti pratipattavyam
# chad nas 'byung ba'i phyir 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yin par khong du chud par bya'o /
acittakamiddhamūrchādyavasthāsu cchinnepravṛttivijñānasantāne punar acittakamiddhamūrchāpagataālayavijñānam antareṇa pravṛttivijñānotpattir na yujyate / nirodhasamāpattyādivyutthānacittavad ihāpi vicāraḥkartavyaḥ
# sems med pa'i gnyid kyis log pa dang brgyal ba la sogs pa 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa rgyun chad pa las yang sems med pa'i nyid kyis log pa dang brgyal ba las sangs pa na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med pa'i 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa 'byung bar mi rung ngo / / 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa las ldang ba'i sems dang 'dra bar 'dir yang dpyad par bya'o /
saṃsārapravṛttinivṛttitāṃcopādāya / pravṛttivijñānād anyad ālayavijñānam yannimittāsaṃsārapravṛttir nivṛttiś ca gamyate
# 'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog pa'i phyir ro zhes bya ba ni gang gi rgyu las byung ba'i 'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog pa yod pas 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa las kun gzhi rnam par shes pa gzhan yin par shes so /
kṣaṇāvasthānikāyasabhāganairantaryaprabandhenopādānaskandhotpādaḥ saṃsāra ity ucyate
# skad cig kyang mi gnas par ris mthun pa rgyun mi 'chad ba'i rgyun gyi nye bar len pa'i phung po 'byung ba ni 'khor ba zhes bya'o /
tasya punaḥpravṛttirnikāyasabhāgāntareṣu pratisandhiḥ
# de'i 'jug pa ni ris mthun pa gzhan dag tu nying mtshams sbyor ba'o /
nivṛttiḥ sopadhiśeṣonirupadhiśeṣaś ca nirvāṇadhātuḥ
# ldog pa ni phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings so /
tatr ālay avij ñānā nabh yupa gamesaṃskārapratyayavijñānābhāvāt saṃsārapravṛttir na yujyate
# de la kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas mi len na 'du byed kyi rgyu rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba med pa'i phyir 'khor bar 'jug bar mi rung ngo / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas mi len na /
ālayavijñānānabhyupagame hi pratisandhivijñānaṃ vāsaṃskārapratyayaṃ parikalpyeta saṃskāraparibhāvitā vā ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥsaṃskārapratyayaṃ vijñānam
# 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes 'byung ba nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa 'am / / 'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug 'du byed kyi rkyen las byung bar brtag grang na /
tatra napratisandhivijñānaṃ pūrvajanmopacitasaṃskārapratyayampūrvajanmopacitasaṃskārāṇāṃciraniruddhatvāt niruddhasya cāsattvāt asataś ca pratyayābhāvāt
# de'i tshe nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa ni tshe snga ma la bsags pa'i 'du byed kyi rkyen las byung ba ma yin te / / tshe snga ma la bsags pa'i 'du byed ni 'gags nas ring du lon pa'i phyir ro / / 'gags pa ni med pa'i phyir ro /
yadi niruddhasyapratyayatvaṃ neṣyate evaṃ ca saty aphalam eva karma syātna hi vartamānāt karmaṇo vipāko nirvartate / naitad evam tajjabhāvanāvasthānāt / karmāhitāyāś cittasantāne vāsanāyāḥparipākaviśeṣaṃ gatāyā vipāko nirvartate
# med pa ni rkyen du mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / gal te 'gags pa rkyen du mi 'dod na de ltar na / / da ltar gyi las las ni rnam par smin pa mngon par mi 'grub pa las kyi 'bras bu med pa nyid du 'gyur ro / / de ni de lta ma yin te / / de las byung ba'i bsgos pa gnas pa'i phyir ro / / gang las 'gyur ba bye brag tu gyur nas rnam par smin pa 'grub pa'i bag chags las kyis bskyed pa sems kyi rgyud la yod do /
tasmān na viphalaṃkarma na ca niruddhāt karmaṇo vipāka iti / pratisandhau canāmarūpam eva na kevalaṃ vijñānam
# de lta bas na las kyi 'bras bu med pa ma yin la / / las 'gags pa las rnam par smin pa 'byung ba yang ma yin no / / nying mtshams sbyor ba'i tshe ni ming dang gzugs kyi yin te /
tatra vijñānam evasaṃskārapratyayam na ca nāmarūpam iti kātra yuktiḥ
# rnam par shes pa 'ba' zhig ni ma yin na / / de la rnam par shes pa nyid 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung gi / / ming dang gzugs ni ma yin no zhes bya ba 'di la rigs pa ci yod /
tasmāt saṃskārapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam iti vaktayam natu vijñānamiti / katamad vānyad vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam
# de lta bas na 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs zhes brjod par bya'i / / rnam par shes pa ma yin no zhes brjod pa'o / / rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs zhes bya ba gzhan gang zhe na /
yatpratisandhikṣaṇād uttarakālam / tasya prātisandhikānnāmarūpāt ka ātmātiśayo yatas tad eva vijñānapratyayaṃ napūrvam pūrvaṃ ca saṃskārapratyayaṃ nottaram ity ataś ca saṃskārapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam evāstu / kiṃpratisandhivijñānenāṅgāntareṇa parikalpitena / tasmān napratisandhivijñānaṃ saṃskārapratyayaṃ yujyate / gsaṃskārās tv avidyāpratyayāḥ / tadadhivāsitaṃ ca vijñānaṃsaṃskārapratyayam / tatpratyayaṃ pratisandhau ca nāmarūpamevety eṣaiva nītir niravadyā
# nyid mtshams sbyor ba'i skad cig las dus phyi ma gang yin pa'o zhe na / / de nying mtshams sbyor ba'i ming dang gzugs las rang bzhin bye brag tu gyur pa ci yod na / / 'di ltar de nyid rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis byung ba yin la / / snga ma ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung ba yin la / / phyi ma ni ma yin te de'i phyir 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs nyid du 'gyur gyi / / nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes ba'i yan lag gzhan kun du brtags pas ci zhig bya / / de lta bas na nying mtshams sbyor ba'i rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung bar mi rung ngo / / 'du byed rnams ni ma rig pa'i rkyen gyis byung ba yin la des bsgos pa'i rnam par shes pa ni 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis byung ba dang de'i rkyen gyis byung ba nying mtshams sbyor ba ni ming dang gzugs nyid do zhes bya ba'i tshul 'di la ni nyes pa med do /
ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥsaṃskāraparibhāvitāḥ saṃskārapratyayam vijñānam ity ayamapi pakṣo durghaṭita eva / kiṃ kāraṇam
# rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po 'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa dag 'du byed kyi rkyen gyis rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i phyogs 'di yang sbyar ma legs pa nyid de / / ci'i phyir zhe na /
na hi vijñānaṃvipākavāsanāṃ niṣyandavāsanāṃ vātmany ādhātuṃsamartham ātmani kāritravirodhāt
# rnam par shes pa ni rnam par smin pa'i bag chags dang rgyu mthun pa'i bag chags bdag la skyed par mi nus te / / bdag la byed pa 'gal ba'i phyir ro /
nāpy anantare tasyatadānutpannatvād anutpannasya cāsattvāt / nāpy utpannepūrvasya tadā niruddhatvāt
# de ma theg pa la yang ma yin te / / de ni de'i tshe ma byung ba'i phyir ro / / ma byung ba ni med pa'i phyir ro / / byung ba la yang ma yin te / / de ni de'i tshe sngar 'gags pa'i phyir ro /
acittakāsu ca middhādyavasthāsupunaḥ saṃskāraparibhāvitacittotpattyasambhavādvijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ na syāt
# sems med pa'i gnyid kyis log pa la sogs pa'i dus na ni 'du byed kyis yongs su bsgos pa'i sems 'byung mi srid pa'i phyir rnam par shes pa'i rkyen gyis ming dang gzugs med par 'gyur ro /
tadabhāvātṣaḍāyatanaṃna syāt
# de med par skye mched drug kyang med par 'gyur ro /
evaṃ yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ na syāt / tataś casaṃsārapravṛttir evavirudhyate
# de bzhin du rga shi'i bar du yang med par 'gyur ro /
saṃsāranivṛttir apyālayavijñāne 'satinopapadyate
# de'i phyir 'khor bar 'jug pa nyid dang 'gal lo / / 'khor ba las ldog pa yang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med na mi 'thad de /
saṃsārasya hi karmakleśāḥkāraṇam
# 'khor ba'i rgyu ni las dang nyon mongs pa rnams so /
tayoḥ kleśāḥ pradhānam
# de gnyis las kyang nyon mongs pa ni gtso bo ste /
tathā hi kleśādhipatyātkarma punarbhavākṣepasamarthaṃ bhavatinānyathā
# 'di ltar nyon mongs pa'i dbang gis na las kyis yang srid pa 'phen nus par 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
ata evana dṛṣṭasatyānāṃ karmāṇi punarbhavam ākṣipantidarśanaprahātavyakleśābhāvāt
# de'i phyir bden pa mthong ba rnams kyi las las yang srid pa mi 'phen te / / mthong bas spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir ro /
ākṣiptapunarbhavam api karmakleśābhāvān na punarbhavībhavatīti
# de bzhin du yang srid pa 'phangs pa'i las kyang nyon mongs pa med na yang srid pa 'byung bar mi 'gyur te /
tathā hitraidhātukavītarāgāṇām ākṣiptapunarbhavam api karmakleśābhāvād bhavībhavituṃ notsahate
# 'di ltar khams gsum gyi 'dod chags dang bral ba rnams kyi yang srid pa 'phangs pa'i las kyang nyon mongs pa med pa'i phyir yang srid pa 'byung bar byed mi nus so /
ataś ca teṣāṃpunarbhavo nābhinirvartate
# de'i phyir de dag gi yang srid pa mngon par mi 'grub bo /
evaṃ ca pradhānatvāt kleśā evasaṃsārapravṛtter mūlam
# de ltar na gtso bo yin pa'i phyir nyon mongs pa nyid 'khor bar 'jug pa'i rtsa ba ste /
atas teṣu prahīṇeṣu saṃsāro nivartatenānyathā
# de'i phyir de dag spangs na 'khor ba las ldog par 'gyur gyi gzhan du ni ma yin no /
na cālayavijñānam antareṇa tatprahāṇaṃ yujyate
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa med par de dag spang du mi rung ste /
sammukhībhūto vā kleśaḥ prahīyeta bījāvastho vā
# nyon mongs pa mngon du gyur pa'am / / sa bon gyi tshe spang grang na /
tatrasammukhībhūtaḥ prahīyata ity aniṣṭir eveyam tadātatprahāṇamārgābhāvāt
# de la mngon du gyur pa spang ngo zhe na ni / / de mi 'dod pa nyid de / / de'i tshe de dag spong ba'i lam med pa'i phyir ro /
bījāvastho 'pi naiva prahīyate na hipratipakṣāt tadānīṃ kiñcid anyad abhyupagamyate yatrakleśabījaṃ vyavasthitaṃtatpratipakṣeṇa prahīyeta / atha pratipakṣacittameva kleśabījānuṣaktam iṣyate na hi kleśabījānuṣaktam eva tatpratipakṣo yujyate
# sa bon gyi tshe yang spang du mi rung ste / / gang la nyon mongs pa'i sa bon gnas pa de gnyen pos spong na / / de'i tshe ni gnyen po las ci yang khas ma blangs pa'i phyir ro / / ji ste gnyen po'i sems nyid nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang 'dres na ni nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang 'dres pa nyid pas gnyen por mi rung ste /
nacāprahīṇakleśabījānāṃ saṃsāravinivṛttiḥsambhavatīti tasmādavaśyam ālayavijñānaṃ tadanyavijñānasahabhūtaiḥ kleśopakleśair bhāvyatesvabījapuṣṭyādhānata ity upeyam
# nyon mongs pa'i sa bon ma spangs pa rnams ni 'khor ba las ldog mi srid do / / de lta bas na gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la de las gzhan pa'i rnam par shes pa dang lhan cig 'byung ba'i nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams kyis rang gi sa bon gso bar bya ba'i phyir bag chags bsgo bar khas blangs so /
punaś ca tata eva santatipariṇāmaviśeṣād yathābalaṃbhāvanāvṛttilābhe sati kleśopakleśāḥ pravartante
# rgyun 'gyur ba'i bye brag gi stobs ji lta ba bzhin du bsgos pa 'jug pa rnyed nas / / yang de nyid las nyon mongs pa dang nye ba'i nyon mongs pa rnams 'byung ste /
teṣāṃcālayavijñānavyavasthitaṃ bījaṃtatsahabhuvākleśapratipakṣamārgeṇāpanīyate
# de dag gi sa bon kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la gnas pa ni de dang lhan cig 'byung ba nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po lam gyis sel to /
tasmiṃś cāpanīte punastenāśrayeṇa kleśānām anutpattir iti sopadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥprāpyate
# de bsal nas gnas de nas nyon mongs pa rnams mi 'byung bas phung po lhag ma dang bcas pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings thob bo /
pūrvakarmākṣiptajanmanirodhe ca tato'nyajanmāpratisandhānān nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥ
# sngon gyi las kyis 'phangs pa'i skye ba ni 'gags la / / de las gzhan pa'i skye ba dang nying mtshams mi sbyor ba ni lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings te /
na hikarmavidyamānam api kleśeṣu prahīṇeṣusahakārikāraṇābhāvātpunarbhavam abhinirvartayituṃsamartham
# las yod du zin kyang nyon mongs pa rnams spangs na lhan cig byed pa'i rgyu med pa'i phyir / / yang srid pa mngon par 'grub par byed mi nus so /
ata evālayavijñāne sati saṃsārapravṛttir nivṛttiś canānyathety avaśyam ālayavijñānam abhyupagantavyam
# de ltar na kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yod na 'khor bar 'jug pa dang ldog par rung gi gzhan du ni ma yin te / / gdon mi za bar kun gzhi rnam par shes pa khas blang bar bya'o /
kiṃ kāraṇaṃtad ālayavijñānam ity ucyate
# ci'i phyir kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya zhe na /
ālayavijñānatvaṃ punas tasyasarvabījālayatām
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa 'di ni sa bon thams cad kyi gzhi nyid do /
upādāyety ante 'padiṣṭaṃsarvatrābhisambadhyate / ālayavijñānabhāva ālayavijñānatvam / tat punar ālayavijñānaśabdapravṛttinimittam
# phyir ro zhes bya ba tha mar gang bstan pa de ni thams cad du sbyar bar bya'o / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa'i dngos po ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid do / / de ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba 'jug pa'i rgyu'o /
tatravijānātītivijñānaṃ
# de la rnam par shes par byed pas rnam par shes pa ste /
tadvyatiriktavijñātrabhāvapradarśanārthaṃbhāvamātre kartṛvyapadeśaḥ
# de las ma gtogs par shes par byed pa po med par bstan pa'i phyir dngos po tsam la byed par bstan to /
sarvabījālayatāsarvasāṅkleśikadharmabījasthānatā / ālayaṃ sthānam itiparyāyaḥ
# sa bon thams cad kyi gzhi nyid ni kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos kyi sa bon thams cad kyi gnas nyid do; / / gzhi ni gnas kyi rnam grangs su gtogs pa'o /
athavālīyanta upanibadhyante 'smin sarvadharmāḥkāryabhāvena tad vālīyata upanibadhyate kāraṇabhāvenasarvadharmeṣv ity ālayaḥ / ātmabhāvālayanimittatāṃ copādāya / ātmabhāvo / nāmarūpam / ālīyate 'sminn ātmabhāvaḥ tadbalenānuvṛttita ity ālayaḥ
# yang na 'dir chos thams cad 'bras bu'i dngos por sbyor zhing nye bar 'brel ba'am / / de chos thams cad la rgyu'i dngos por sbyor zhing nye bar 'brel bas kun gzhi'o / / lus kyi kun gzhi nyid dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir zhes bya ba la lus ni ming dang gzugs so / / der lus sbyor te / / de'i stobs kyis 'byung bas kun gzhi nyid do /
tadbhāva ālayatā / ātmabhāvanimittaṃ tadbījaparipoṣātpratisandhāv ātmabhāvanirvartanāt
# de'i dngos po ni kun gzhi nyid do / / lus kyi rgyu ni de'i sa bon yongs su gsos pas nying mtshams sbyor ba ni lus mngon par 'grub pa'i phyir te /
ātmabhāvālayatāmātmabhāvanimittatāṃ copādāyālayavijñānatvamabhyupagantavyam / anye punar anyathā paṭhanti ātmamānālayanimittatāṃ copādāyeti
# lus kyi gzhi nyid dang lus kyi rgyu nyid yin pas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid khas blang bar bya'o gzhan nas de bzhin du 'byung ste / / bdag tu nga rgyal gyi gzhi dang rgyu nyid kyi phyir ro zhes 'byung ngo /
ālayavijñānam ātmatvenālambamānasya yo mānaḥsa ātmamāna
# kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la bdag tu dmigs pa'i nga rgyal gang yin pa de bdag tu nga rgyal lo /
ālīyatetasmin viṣayibhāvenātmamāna ityālayavijñānamātmamānālayaḥ
# bdag tu nga rgyal ni 'di la yul can gyi dngos por sbyor bas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni bdag tu nga rgyal gyi kun gzhi'o /
ālīyate vā tannimittabhāvenātmamāna ity ālayaucyate / śeṣaṃ pūrvavat / kāyālīnatāṃ copādāyeti / caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ
# yang na de dag tu nga rgyal la rgyu'i dngos por sbyor bas kun gzhi zhes bya'o / / lhag ma ni snga ma bzhin no / / lus la gnas pa nyid kyi yang phyir ro zhes bya ba la yang zhes bya ba ni bsdu ba'i don to /
kāyo 'tra sendriyaṃ śarīram / samantaṃ hi śarīraṃvyāpyālayavijñānaṃ vartate
# lus ni 'dir dbang po dang bcas pa'i khog pa'o / / kun gzhi rnam par shes pa ni khog pa thams cad la khyab pa'o /
ataḥ kāyapratibaddhavṛttitvāt tatkāye ālīnam iti kāyālīnam / tadbhāvaḥkāyālīnatā
# de'i phyir lus dang 'brel bar 'jug pas lus la gnas pa'i phyir lus la gnas pa'o / / de'i dngos po ni lus la gnas pa nyid de /
tāṃkāyālīnatām upādāya gṛhītvālayavijñānatvam asyapratipattavyam
# lus la gnas pa nyid kyi phyir bzung nas 'di kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid du khong du chud par bya'o /
na kevalam ālayavijñānam etad ucyate kiṃ tarhyādānavijñānam apīti / kiṃ kāraṇaṃ tad ādānavijñānam / ity ucyate / ataḥ kāraṇam āha kāyopādānatāmupādāyeti / ādīyate kāyo 'nenety ādānavijñānam ity ucyate
# de ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba 'ba' zhig tu ma zad kyi / / len pa'i rnam par shes pa yang de yin te / / ci'i phyir de len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya zhe na / / de'i phyir lus len pa'i phyir ro zhes rgyu smos so / / 'dis lus len bas len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya ste /
cittena kāyasyopādānaṃ nānyeneti prasiddham
# sems kyis lus len gyi bdag gis ni ma yin no zhes bya bar rab tu grub bo /
tac ca yatpūrvasaṃskārahetukaṃśukraśoṇitasammūrchitāvasthāyāṃ bhavam upādatte
# de yang sngon gyi 'du byed kyi rgyu las 'byung ba ste / / khu ba dang khrag gi nang du brgyal ba'i dus na srid pa len te /
tad evāmaraṇāt kāyopādātṛtveneṣyate
# de nyid shi ba la thug gi bar lus len par byed par 'dod kyi /
na cakṣurādivijñānānitatpṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ vā manovijñānam teṣāṃ tata ūrdhvaṃvartamānacakṣurādipratyayanimittatvāt
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams dang de'i rjes las byung ba yid kyi rnam par shes pas ni ma yin te / / de dag ni de'i 'og tu mig la sogs pa rkyen rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro /
na ca tatrānyanmanovijñānaṃ saṃskārahetukaṃ tasya kuśalākuśalatvāt
# de la yid kyi rnam par shes pa gzhan 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba ni ma yin te / / de dag dge ba dang mi dge ba'i phyir ro /
saṃskārahetukaṃ hy ekāntenāvyākṛtam vipākatvāt
# 'du byed kyi rgyu las byung ba ni rnam par smin pa yin pa'i phyir gcig tu lung ma bstan pa'o /
vipākaśca na vicchinnaḥ sandhīyate cakṣurādivat
# rnam par smin pa la yang mig la sogs pa bzhin du rgyun chad nas yang nying mtshams sbyor ba ma yin no /
na cālayavijñānāanyad ekāntenāvyākṛtajātīyam upalabhyateyadvipākavijñānatvena parikalpyeta
# gang rnam par smin pa'i rnam par shes pa nyid kun du rtag pa gcig tu lung ma bstan pa'i rang bzhin can ni kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las gzhan ma mthong ngo /
api capratiniyatāśrayapravṛttatvāt ṣaṇṇāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃvicchedapravṛttatvāc ca na sarvasyāśrayasyopādānaṃprasajyate
# yang rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag ni gnas so sor nges pa las 'byung ba dang rgyun chad nas 'byung ba'i phyir gnas thams cad len par mi rung ste /
tathā hiyena yenāśrayeṇa yad vijñānaṃ pravartatesa eva tenopāttaḥ syāt avaśiṣṭasyānupāttatvaṃvijñānavirahitatvāt
# 'di ltar gnas gang dang gang las rnam par shes pa gang 'byung ba des de nyid zin par 'gyur gyi / / lhag ma ni rnam par shes pa dang bral ba'i phyir zin pa ma yin no /
tathā cakṣurādivijñānaṃ vicchedena punaḥ punaḥ pravartata ititadāśrayasya punaḥ punarupādānadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ
# de ltar mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rgyun chad nas yang dang yang 'byung ba'i phyir gnas de yang dang yang nye bar len pa'i skyon du 'gyur ro /
tasmād ālayavijñānam evapratisandhau kāyam upādatte ā maraṇāc ca samastakāyāśrayeṇa pravartata iti tad eva rpratisandhibandhātprabhṛty ā maraṇāt kāyam upādātta ity ādānavijñānam ity ucyate / prādhānyena mana ālayavijñānālambanam / iti / kliṣṭaṃ hi mana ālayavijñānam ātmatvena nityam ālambateātmālambanair mohadṛṣṭimānasnehaiḥ samprayuktatvāt / tac canityakālaṃmanyanātmakatvān manaḥ / prādhānyena tad eva mana ucyate
# de lta bas kun gzhi rnam par shes pa nyid nying mtshams sbyor ba'i dus nas lus bzung nas shi ba la thug gi bar du lus mtha' dag la brten te 'byung bas de nyid nying mtshams sbyor ba nas shi ba la thug gi bar du lus 'dzin pas na len pa'i rnam par shes pa zhes bya'o / / dngos su na yid kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la dmigs zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi yid kun gzhi rnam par shes pa la rtag par bdag tu dmigs te / / bdag tu rmongs pa dang lta ba dang nga rgyal dang chags par dmigs pa rnams dang mtshungs bar ldan pa'i phyir ro / / de yang rtag par rlom sems pa'i bdag nyid yin pas yod do / / dngos su na de yid ces bya'o /
yat ṣaṇṇāṃ cakṣurādivijñānakāyānāṃ samanantaraniruddhaṃ vijñānaṃ mana ity uktam tat ṣaṣṭhasyamanovijñānasyāśrayaprasiddhyartham na tumanyanākāratvāt / ato na tasya prādhānyena manastvam
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs drug po dag 'gags ma thag pa'i rnam par shes pa la yid ces brjod pa gang yin pa de ni drug pa yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i gnas sgrub pa'i phyir yin gyi ngar sems pa'i rna ba'i phyir ni ma yin no / / de'i phyir dngos su na de ni yid nyid ma yin no /
taccaturbhiḥ kleśairnityaṃ samprayuktam / vātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmamānātmasnehaiḥ
# de yang bdag tu rmongs pa dang bdag tu lta ba dang bdag tu nga rgyal dang bdag la chags pa ste / / nyon mongs pa bzhi dang rtag par mtshungs par ldan te /
atra tv ātmagrahaṇaṃ na mohamātreṇa samprayujyate kiṃtarhy ātmaniyo mohaḥ / evaṃ yāvad ātmasnehe vaktavyam
# de la bdag tu rmongs pa ni gti mug tsam dang mtshungs par ldan pa ma yin gyi / / bdag tu rmongs pa gang yin pa'o / / de bzhin du bdag la chags pa'i bar dag la yang brjod par bya'o /
ādigrahaṇāt pañcabhiḥsarvatragaiś casparśamanaskārādibhiḥ sadā samprayuktam
# sogs pa ni reg pa dang yid la byed pa la sogs pa kun du 'gro ba lnga po dag dang yang rab tu mtshungs par ldan pa'o /
tasyāpratītatvāccaittānām api caittaiḥ samprayogāc catatsvarūpanirdhāraṇārtham āha vijñānam iti
# de yang ma grags pa dang sems las byung ba rnams dang mtshungs par ldan pas na de'i rang gi ngo bo dmigs kyis dbye ba'i phyir / / rnam par shes pa ste zhes bya ba smos so /
ekajātīyam iti kliṣṭajātīyam na kuśalam avyākṛtaṃ vānityam ātmamohādibhiś caturbhiḥ kleśaiḥ samprayuktatvāt
# rigs gcig pa zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa can gyi rigs yin gyi / / dge ba'am / / lung du ma bstan pa ni ma yin te / / bdag tu rmongs pa la sogs pa nyon mongs pa bzhi dang rtag tu mtshungs par ldan pa'i phyir ro /
santānānuvṛtti cety avicchedena vartata ity arthaḥ
# rgyun chags par 'jug pa ste zhes bya ba ni rgyun mi 'chad par rjes su 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go /
asyotsargasyāpavādam ārabhatearhattvāryamārganirodhasamāpattyavasthāṃ sthāpayitvā / arhattvāvasthāyāṃ na pravartate arhato / nira vaśe ṣatr aidh ātuk akli ṣṭad harm apra hīṇa tvāt
# spyir btang ba 'di'i dmigs kyis bsal ba rtsom ste / / dgra bcom pa dang 'phags pa'i lam dang 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus ma gtogs so / / dgra bcom pa ni khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa can gyi chos spangs pa'i phyir dgra bcom pa'i dus ni mi 'byung ngo /
āryamārgāvasthāyām api na pravartate paramārthajñānasyātmadṛṣṭisamudācāreṇātyantavirodhāt
# 'phags pa'i lam gyi dus na yang mi 'byung ste / / de na dam pa shes pa ni bdag tu lta ba kun du 'byung ba dang shin tu mi mthun pa'i phyir ro /
tataūrdhvam asyālayavijñānāt pravṛttiḥ śaikṣasyāprahīṇatvāt / nirodhasamāpattyavasthāyām api na pravartate
# de'i 'og tu kun gzhi rnam par shes pa las 'byung ste / / slob pa'i dus na ma spangs pa'i phyir ro / / 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa'i dus na yang mi 'byung ste /
asañjñisamāpattito nirodhasamāpatteḥśāntataratvaṃ tadasamucāratvād eva veditavyam
# 'du shes med pa'i snyoms par 'jug pa bas [?] 'gog pa'i snyoms par zhugs pa ches zhe ba'i phyir / / de kun du mi 'byung bar rig par bya'o /
atra ca mano nirvacanataālambanataḥ samprayogataḥ pravṛttikālataś ca nirdiṣṭaṃveditavyam / kenārthena rūpādiskandhā ity ucyante
# 'dir ni nges pa'i tshig dang dmigs pa dang mtshungs par ldan pa dang 'byung pa'i dus kyi yid bstan par rig par bya'o / / ci'i phyir phung po zhes bya zhe na /
rāśyarthena / rāśiḥ skandha iti paryāyaḥ / etad uktaṃ bhavati rūparāśī rūpaskandhaḥ
# spungs pa'i phyir te zhes bya ba la spungs pa ni phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su gtogs pa'o / / de ni 'di skad du gzugs spungs pa ni gzugs kyi phung po ste /
evaṃ yāvad vijñānarāśirvijñānaskandha iti / yasmāt sūtre adhvasantānaprakāragatideśabhedabhinnān / āṃ rūpādīnāṃ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatāmupādāya rūpādayaḥ skandhā uktāḥ / y zyat kiñcid rūpam aatītānāgatapratyutpannam ādhyātmikaṃ vā bāhyaṃ vāaudarikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yad vā dūre yad vāntikesarvam aikadhyam abhisaṅkṣipya rūpaskandhaitisaṅkhyāṃ gacchatītyevaṃ yāvad vijñānam
# de bzhin du rnam par shes pa'i bar du sbungs pa la rnam par shes pa'i phung po zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / 'di ltar mdo las dus dang rgyu dang rnam pa dang 'gro ba dang yul tha dad pa'i gzugs la sogs pa mdor bsdus pa'i phyir / / gzugs la sogs pa phung por bstan te / / gzugs gang yin pa ci yang rung 'das pa'am ma 'ongs pa'am da ltar byung pa'am / / nang gi'am phyi'i'am / / rags pa'am / / phra ba'am / / ngan pa'am / / gya nom pa'am / / thag nye ba gang yin pa'am / / rgyang ring ba gang yin pa thams cad gcig tu bsdus nas gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o / / de bzhin du rnam par shes pa'i bar du'o zhes 'byung ste /
atītānāgatapratyutpannā ity adhvabhedena bhinnāḥ
# 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba zhes bya ba'i bye brag gis dus tha dad pa'o /
ādhyātmikā vā bāhyā veti santānabhedena yasmādādhyātmikāḥ svāsāntānikāḥ bāhyās tato 'nye
# nang ngam phyi zhes bya ba ni rgyu tha dad pas so / / 'di ltar nang gi rnams ni rang gi rgyud du gtogs pa dag go / / phyi'i rnams ni de las gzhan pa dag go /
audārikā vāsūkṣmā veti prakārabhedena
# rags pa'am / / phra ba zhes bya ba ni rnam pa'i bye brag gis so /
tatra rūpasyāpekṣikamaudārikasūkṣmatvam
# de la gzugs kyi rags pa dang phra ba nyid ni ltos ba can no /
sapratigham audārikam apratighaṃsūkṣmaṃ
# yang na thogs pa dang bcas pa ni rags pa'o / / thogs pa med pa ni phra ba'o /
vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānāni tupañcendriyāśrayotpannāny audārikāṇi mānasāni sūkṣmāṇi
# tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams kyang dbang po lnga la brten te / / byung ba dag ni rags pa'o / / yid la brten te byung ba dag ni phra ba'o; /
hīnā vā praṇītā veti gatibhedena bhinnāḥ
# ngan pa'am gya nom pa zhes bya ba ni 'gro ba'i bye brag gis tha dad pa rnams te /
tathā hihīnagatisaṅgṛhītā hīnāḥpraṇītagatisaṅgṛhītāḥ praṇītāḥ
# 'di ltar 'gro ba ngan pas zin pa dag ni ngan pa rnams so / / 'gro ba gya nom pas zin pa dag ni gya nom pa rnams so /
yad vādūre yad vāntika iti deśabhedena bhinnāḥ
# thag nye ba gang yin pa'am / / rgyang ring po gang yin pa zhes bya ba ni yul gyi bye brag gis tha dad pa rnams so /
vedanādīnāṃ tudūrāntikatvam āśrayavaśena
# tshor ba la sogs pa ni gnas kyi dbang gis nye ba dang ring ba'o /
rūpādīnām iti rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām
# gzugs la sogs pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so /
saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatām upādāyetydhva sant ānap rakā raga tide śabh edab hinn ānāṃrūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānāṃ pratyekaṃ saṅkṣepeṇasaṅgrahaḥ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahaḥ / tadbhāvaḥ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatā
# mdor bsdus pa nyid kyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni dus dang rgyu dang rnam pa dang 'gro ba dang yul tha dad pa rnams kyi gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so sor mdor bsdus pa ni mdor bsdus pa'o / / de'i dngos po ni mdor bsdus pa nyid do /
tāṃ saṅkṣepasaṅgrahatām upādāya sūtre rāśyarthaḥskandhārtho vijñāyate
# de dag mdor bsdus pa'i phyir mdo las sbungs pa'i don zhes 'byung ba ni phung po'i don ni zhes bya bar shes te /
tathā hy uktam / tat sarvam atītādikaṃrūpam ekadhyam abhisaṅkṣipya rūpaskandha itisaṅkhyāṃ gacchatīti / evaṃ yāvad vijñānam / uktāḥ pañca skandhāḥ skandhārthaś ca
# 'di ltar 'das pa la sogs pa'i gzugs de dag thams cad ni gcig tu bsdus nas gzugs kyi phung po zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro ba zhes bya ba nas / / de bzhin du rnam par shes pa zhes bya ba'i bar du bstan to / / phung po lnga po rnams dang phung po'i don bshad zin to / / phung po lnga'i rab tu byed pa bye brag tu bshad pa / / bam po bzhi pa ste tha ma'o /
sarvasaṃskārāḥpañcaskandhasaṅgraheṇoktāḥ sarvadharmāḥsaṃskṛtā asaṃskṛtāś cāyatanadhātusaṅgraheṇa / tatraskandhanirdeśānantaram āyatanāni vaktavyāni / kaścāyatanārtha ity ata āha dvādaśāyatanānīti / tāni punaḥ
# 'dus byas thams cad ni phung po lngas bsdus la / / 'dus byas dang; 'dus ma byas kyi chos thams cad ni skye mched dang khams su bsdus par bstan pa de la phung po bshad pa'i 'og tu skye mched rnams brjod dgos pas du zhig gang dang gang skye mched kyi don ni ci zhe na / / de'i phyir / / skye mched bcu gnyis zhes bya ba smos so /
katamāni / cakṣurāyatanaṃ rūpāyatanaṃ yāvadmanaāyatanaṃ dharmāyatanaṃ caiti / cakṣurādīnāṃ pūrvavan nirdeśa iti
# de dag kyang gang zhe na; mig gi skye mched dang gzugs kyi skye mched dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa nas / / yid kyi skye mched dang chos kyi skye mched do zhes bya ba'i bar du'o /
rūpaskandhavibhāge yathā cakṣurādayaḥ svarūpato nirdiṣṭāḥtathehāpi svarūpatonirdeṣṭavyā iti
# mig la sogs pa ni snga ma bzhin du bshad do zhes bya ba ni gzugs kyi phung po rnam par phye ba ni ji ltar mig la sogs pa'i rang gi ngo bo bstan pa de bzhin du 'dir yang rang gi ngo bo bstan par bya'o /
tatra hy uktaṃ catvāri mahābhūtāny upādāya varṇaviṣayo rūpaprasādaścakṣurindriyam iti
# de la mig gi dbang po ni 'byung ba chen po bzhi rgyur byas pa ste / / yul kha dog gzugs dang ba'o zhes bstan to /
evaṃ śabdagandharasaspraṣṭavyaviṣayāyathākramaṃ rūpātmakāḥ prasādāḥśrotrādayaḥ
# de bzhin du sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya yang yul te; go rims bzhin no / / rna ba la sogs pa yang gzugs kyi bdag nyid dang ba'o /
rūpaśabdagandharasāyatanānāṃ ca pūrvavan / nirdeśa iti sambadhyate
# gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro'i skye mched rnams kyang snga ma bzhin du bshad do zhes bya bar sbyar ro /
pūrvaṃ hi nirdiṣṭaś cakṣuṣo viṣayovarṇaḥsaṃsthānaṃ vijñaptiś ca rūpam
# sngar ni mig gi yul ni / / kha dog dang dbyibs dang rnam par rig byed kyi gzugs so /
upāttānupāttobhayamahābhūtahetukaḥ śrotrasya viṣayaḥśabdaityādi
# rna ba'i yul ni sgra ste / / zin pa dang ma zin pa dang gnyi ga'i ste 'byung ba chen po'i rgyu las byung ba'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa bstan to /
mahābhūtāni yaś ca / spraṣṭavyasyaikadeśa uktaḥ tat saha mahābhūtaiḥspraṣṭavyāyatanam
# 'byung ba chen po dag dang gang reg bya'i phyogs gcig bshad pa ste / / de 'byung ba chen po rnams dang bcas pa ni reg bya'i skye mched do /
tat punaḥ ślakṣṇatvam ityādi
# de yang 'jam pa nyid la sogs pa'o /
manaāyatanaṃ yo vijñānaskandhaiti / aṣṭau / vijñānāni vijñānaskandhaḥ ṣaḍ pravṛttivijñānāniālayavijñānaṃ kliṣṭaṃ ca manaḥ
# yid kyi skye mched ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po gang yin pa'o zhes bya ba la rnam par shes pa brgyad ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po ste / / 'jug pa'i rnam par shes pa drug dang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa dang nyon mongs pa can gyi yod do /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ tuvijñānaskandha eva manaāyatanam ucyate / dharmāyatanaṃ punar aṣṭaprakāraṃ
# skye mched rnam par gzhag pa la ni rnam par shes pa'i phung po nyid la yid kyi skye mched ces bya'o / / chos kyi skye mched ni rnam pa brgyad de /
vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāraskandhā avijñaptiścāsaṃskṛtāni cacatvāri
# tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed kyi phung po dang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa dang 'dus ma byas bzhi'o /
tatra / vedanāsañjñāsaṃskāraskandhā avijñaptiś ca skandhavibhaṅgaevoktāḥ / asaṃskṛtaṃ tu noktam ity atas tatprabhedabubhutsayā pṛcchati asaṃskṛtaṃ katamad iti
# de la tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed kyi phung po dang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa ni phung po rnam par phye bas bshad pa yin no / / 'dus ma byas ni ma bshad de / / de'i phyir de dag rab tu dbye bar 'dod nas / / 'dus ma byas gang zhe na zhes dris so /
yan na / hetupratyayapratibaddhasvarūpam tad asaṃskṛtam ucyate / ākāśam apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥpratisaṅkhyānirodhas tathatā cety
# gang rgyu dang rkyen la rag las pa ma yin pa'i bdag nyid kyi rang gi ngo bo ni 'dus ma byas zhes bya ste / / nam mkha' dang so sor brtags ba ma yin pa'i 'gog pa dang so so brtags pa'i 'gog pa dang de bzhin nyid do /
asaṃskṛtaprabhedapradarśanam
# 'dus ma byas kyi rab tu dbye ba ston te /
ākāśaṃ katamad ity / ākāśasvarūpāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ / yo rūpāvakāśaiti tatsvarūpanirdeśaḥ
# nam mkha' gang zhe na zhes bya ba ni nam mkha'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir 'dri ba'o / / gang gzugs kyi go 'byed pa'o zhes bya ba ni de'i rang gi ngo bo bshad pa'o /
evam apratisaṅkhyānirodhādiṣv api pratyekaṃ vācyam / sapratighaṃ rūpaṃ yatra pradeśe napratihanyatesa tasyāvakāśaḥ
# de bzhin du so sor brtags pa ma yin pa la sogs pa so sor brjod par bya'o / / phyogs gang du thogs pa dang bcas pa'i gzugs la thogs par mi byed pa ni go 'byed pa'o /
ato rūpiṇāṃ bhāvānāmavakāśadānād ākāśam ity ucyate
# de'i phyir dngos po gzugs can rnams la skabs 'byed pa nam mkha' zhes bya'o /
ākāśānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt tann irde ś ānant aram evāpratisaṅkhyānirodhasvarūpāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ katama iti
# nam mkha'i 'og tu bstan pa'i phyir de bshad pa'i 'og tu so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'i rang gi ngo bo khong du chud par 'dod nas / / so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa gang zhe na zhes dris so /
saṅkhyānaṃ / tulanaṃ vicayaḥprajñety anarthāntaram / pratir vīpsārthaḥ
# brtags pa dang gzhal ba dang rnam par 'byed pa dang shes rab ces bya ba ni don gcig go / / so sor zhes bya ba ni spyir bsnyag pa'i don te /
tad uktaṃ bhavati duḥkhādīnām āryasatyānāṃpratipratisaṅkhyānaṃ pratisaṅkhyā
# de ni 'di ltar sdug bsngal la sogs pa 'phags pa'i bden pa rnams la so sor rtog pa ni so sor brtags pa ste /
prajñāviśeṣa ity arthaḥ / napratisaṅkhyā apratisaṅkhyā / kā punar asau / pratyayavaikalyam
# shes rab kyi khyad par zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / so sor ma brtags pa ni so sor brtags pa ma yin pa ste / / de yang gang zhe na /
etad uktaṃ bhavati pratyayavaikalyādanāgatānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yo 'tyantam anutpādaḥ so'pratisaṅkhyānirodhaiti
# rkyen ma tshang ba'o / / de ni 'di skad du rkyen ma tshang ba'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams gtan du mi skye ba gang yin pa de so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro /
yo nirodho na cavisaṃyogaityādi praśnavyākaraṇam
# gang 'gog pa la 'bral ba ma yin pa ste zhes bya ba la sogs pa ni 'dri ba'i lan no /
nirodhaśabdo hy atra / pratisaṅkhyānirodhasamāpattyupapattyanityatānirodheṣv apivartata iti pratisaṅkhyānirodhavyavacchedārtham āha na cavisaṃyoga iti
# 'gog pa zhes byas na ni so sor brtags pa ma yin pas 'gog pa bzhin du so sor brtags pa dang; snyoms par 'jug pa dang skye ba dang mi rtag pa'i 'gog pa rnams la yang snyegs pas 'dir so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa rnam par dbye ba'i phyir 'bral ba ma yin pa zhes bya ba smos te /
saṃyogo hy anāgatair dharmair bīje sati teṣāmutpattidharmatām upādāya vyavasthāpyate / tatpratipakṣeṇasvāśrayāt teṣāṃ bīje 'poddhṛte yo 'tyantam anutpādaḥ pratilabdha itiso 'py apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ prāpnotīty ata āha sa punar yaḥ kleśapratipakṣeṇa vinā skandhānām atyantam anutpāda iti / etad uktaṃ
# 'bral ba ma yin zhes bya ba ni sa bon yod na de dag 'byung ba'i chos nyid yin pa'i phyir ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams dang phrad par rnam par gzhag ste / / de'i gnyen pos rang gi gnas nas de dag gi sa bon bton bzhin gtan mi skye ba gang yin pa de 'gog pa'o / / de ni 'di skad du sa bon bton la blo sngon du ma btang yang rkyen ma tshang bas ma 'ongs pa'i chos rnams gtan mi skye ba gang yin pa de so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog pa'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / dgra bcom pa la ni ris gzhan dang 'brel ba'i dge ba dang lung dum bstan pa'i phung po rnams kyis bon yod bzhin du gtan mi skye ba thob pas / / de yang so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog par 'gyur ro zhe na / / de'i phyir / / de ni gang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po med par phung po rnams gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba smos te / / de ni 'di skad du /
bhavati ayaṃ hi saty apikuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaskandhabījasadbhāvena vinā kleśapratipakṣeṇa labhyata iti pratisaṅkhyānirodha evāyamnāpratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ
# 'di la dge ba dang lung du ma bstan pa'i phung po'i sa bon yod du zin kyang / / nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po med par mi thob pas so so brtags pa'i 'gog pa nyid de / / 'di ni so sor ma brtags pa'i 'gog pa ma yin no /
evaṃ sopadhiśeṣo nirupadhiśeṣaś canirvāṇadhātuḥ pratisaṅkhyānirodha ity uktaṃ bhavati
# de ltar na phung po'i lhag ma dang bcas pa dang phung po'i lhag ma med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings ni so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
kleśapratipakṣo 'trānāsravo mārgo 'bhipretaḥ
# nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po ni 'dir zag pa med pa'i lam du bzhed do /
atyantamanutpāda ity atyantagrahaṇam upapattisamāpattinirodhavyavacchedārtham
# gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba la gtan du smos pa ni skye ba dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i 'gog pa las rnam par dbye ba'i phyir ro /
sahy anutpādobhavatina tv atyantam punaś cittacaittotpādasadbhāvāt / anutpāda ity anityatānirodhāt / anityatānirodho hi vartamānasyana ca vartamānasyānutpādo 'sti kiṃ tarhy anāgatasyaiveti / tadyathaikarūpaprakāravyāsaktacakṣurvijñānasya yāni viṣayāntarāṇy utpattimanti rūpaprakārāntarāṇi catadālambanaiḥ pañcabhir vijñānakāyair na śakyam utpattumvartamāneṣu samanantarapratyayābhāvāt atīteṣvālambanapratyayābhāvāt / atas teṣām apratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥprāpyate
# de dag mi skye ba yin la gtan du ma yin pa ste / / sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyang 'byung bar 'gyur ba'i phyir ro / / mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba ni mi rtag pa nyid kyi 'gog pa las rnam par 'byed de / / mi rtag pa nyid kyi 'gog pa ni de ltar yod la mi skye ba ni da ltar med pas ma 'ongs pa yin pa nyid de / / dper na gzugs kyi rnam pa gcig la mig gi rnam par shes pa yengs pa yul gzhan dang gzugs kyi rnam pa gzhan 'das pa gang yin pa de dag ni dmigs pa de'i rnam par shes pa'i tshogs lnga bskyed par mi nus te / / da ltar gyi rnam pa la ni de ma thag pa'i rkyen med cing / / 'das pa rnams la ni dmigs pa'i rkyen med pa'i phyir ro / / de'i phyir de dag la so sor brtags pa ma yin pa'i 'gog par 'gyur ro /
pratisaṅkhyānirodhaḥ katama iti
# so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa gang zhe na zhes bya ba la /
kpratisaṅkhyānaṃ pratisaṅkhyāānantaryamārgasaṅgṛhītaḥprajñāviśeṣa ity arthaḥ / pratisaṅkhyayā prāpyo nirodhomadhyapadalopāt / yo nirodhaiti sarvanirodhaprasaṅga ityāha sa cavisaṃyogaiti / evaṃ hi śeṣebhyaś caturbhyo / nirodhebhyo vyavacchinno bhavati teṣāmavisaṃyogātmakatvāt
# so sor rtog pa ni so sor brtags pa ste / / bar chad med pa'i lam gyis shes rab kyi khyad par zhes bya ba'i tha tshig go / / so sor brtags pas thob par bya ba'i 'gog pa ni so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa ste / / tshig bar ma ma smos so / / gang 'gog pa zhes bya ba ni 'gog pa thams cad du thal bar 'gyur bas / / de ni 'brel pa ste zhes bya ba smos so / / de ltar na 'gog pa lhag ma bzhi po las rnam par phye ba yin te /
visaṃyogam eva nirūpayati sapunar yaḥ kleśapratipakṣeṇaskandhānāmatyantam anutpāda iti
# de dag ni 'bral ba'i bdag nyid ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / de ni nyon mongs pa'i gnyen pos phung po gtan du mi skye ba'o zhes bya ba ni 'bral ba nyid dpyod pa ste /
ayaṃ hy āśrayo / niravaśeṣatraidhātukakleśabījānusyūtaḥ pravartate
# lus 'di ni khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon nam lus pa dang rjes su 'brel bar 'byung ba'o /
tatra yasyayasya yo yo mārgakṣaṇaḥ pratipakṣaḥ tasmin mārga utpannesa āśrayakṣaṇas tatpraheyakleśabījānugatamnantarasyāśrayasya kṣaṇāntaram utpādayituṃ na śaknotitadutpattiviruddhapratyayasānnidhyāt
# de la gang dang gang gi gnyen po lam gyi skad cig gang dang gang yin pa'i lam de 'byung na lus kyi skad cig de ni des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i phyi ma lus kyi skad cig gzhan 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen du gyur pa dang phyi ma lus kyi skad cig gzhan skyed par mi nus te / / de 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen nye bar gyur pa'i phyir ro /
kiṃ tarhitatpraheyakleśabījavyāvṛttyātmakasyaiva kāraṇaṃ bhavati tadutpattyanuguṇapratyayasadbhāvāt
# 'on kyang des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon ldog pa bdag nyid kho na'i rgyur 'gyur te / / de byung ba dang mthun pa'i rkyen yod pa'i phyir ro /
sa eva mārgakṣaṇas tatpraheyakleṣabījānugatasya kṣaṇāntarasyotpattaye viguṇaḥpratyayaḥitarasyānuguṇo veditavyaḥ
# lam gyi skad cig de nyid ni des spang bar bya ba'i nyon mongs pa'i sa bon dang ldan pa'i skad cig gzhan 'byung ba dang mi mthun pa'i rkyen du gyur pa dang cig shos dang mthun par brjod par bya'o /
evaṃ yāvadbhāvanāheyasyamṛdumṛdoḥ kleśaprakārasya pratipakṣa utpanne sa āśrayoniravaśeṣatraidhātukadarśanabhāvanāprahātavyakleśabījavyāvṛ ttyātmakasyaiva kṣaṇāntarasya kāraṇībhavati
# de bzhin du bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i srid pa'i rtse mo'i nyon mongs pa chung du chung ngu'i bar gyi gnyen po byung na lus de khams gsum pa'i nyon mongs pa mthong ba dang bsgom pas spang bar bya ba'i sa bon ma lus par ldog pa'i bdag nyid kho na'i skad cig gzhan gyi rgyur 'gyur ro /
evaṃ yasyayasya kleśasyāśrayāpravṛttito bījam uddhṛtaṃ bhavati tasyatasya tatsamprayuktānāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃkleśapratipakṣeṇātyantam anutpādaḥ prāpto bhavati / sa capratisaṅkhyānirodho visaṃyogaś cety ucyate
# de bzhin du nyon mongs pa gang dang gang gi lus mi 'byung bas sa bon bton par gyur pa'i nyon mongs pa de dag mtshungs par ldan pa'i chos rnams kyang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen pos gtan du mi skye bar 'byung ste / / so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa de ni 'bral ba zhes bya'o /
pratisaṅkhyānirodhād anantaraṃ tathatoddiṣṭety atastannirdeśānantaraṃ tathatāvabodhārthaṃ praśnaḥ tathatā
# so sor brtags pa'i 'gog pa'i 'og tu de bzhin nyid bstan pas de'i phyir de bshad pa'i 'og tu de bzhin nyid khong du chud par 'dod nas / / de bzhin nyid gang zhe na zhes 'dri'o /
katameti / yā dharmāṇāṃ dharmatādharmanairātmyamiti tannirdeśaḥ / ananyathātvenatathatā
# gang chos rnams kyi chos nyid dang chos bdag med pa nyid do zhes bya ba de ni de'i bshad pa ste / / gzhan ma yin pa'i don gyi phyir de bzhin nyid do /
dharmāṇām iti rūpavedanāsañjñāsaṃskāravijñānānām / dharmāṇāṃ bhāvo dharmatā yāthātmyaṃ bhūtaprakarṣaḥ
# chos rnams zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang rnam par shes pa rnams so / / chos rnams kyi dngos bo ni chos nyid de ji lta ba bzhin gyi bdag nyid dang yang dag pa'i mthar thug pa'o /
dharmāṇāṃ kāryānityatādayo 'pi dharmatā vidyanta ity ata āha dharmanairātmyam iti
# chos nyid ni chos rnams kyi 'bras bu mi rtag pa nyid la sogs pa yang chos rnams la yod de / / de'i phyir chos bdag med pa nyid ces bya ba smos so /
dharmā hi yena rūpeṇajñānābhidhānayor viṣayībhavanti tat teṣām ātmā / tasmādātmano nirgatā atatsvabhāvatvād itinirātmānaḥ / tadbhāvodharmanairātmyam / tat punar bhāvānāṃkalpitasvabhāvaśūnyatā / atra tu vicāryamāṇe bahu vaktavyaṃjāyata ity alaṃ prasaṅgena prastutam evārabhyate / kenārthenāyatanāni / āyatanaśabdo hi cakṣurādiṣu
# chos ni rang bzhin gang gis shes pa dang brjod pa gnyis kyi yul du 'gyur ba de de dag gi bdag ste / / de'i rang bzhin ma yin pa'i phyir bdag de dang bral ba ni bdag med pa'o / / de'i dngos po ni bdag med pa nyid do / / de ni dngos po rnams rnam par brtags pa'i rang bzhin gyi stong pa nyid do / / 'di la dpyad na brjod pa mang du 'byung ste / / de thal bar 'gyur bas kyang chog gi skabs nyid brtsam mo / / ci'i phyir skye mched ces bya zhe na zhes bya ba la /
parasparavibhinnarūpeṣv aviśeṣeṇa pravartata ity atas teṣu tenasāmānyam artham upādāya pravartitavyam sa ca na vijñāyataiti praśnaḥ kenārthenāyatananīti / vijñānāyadvārārtheneti / āya ucyata āgamaḥ
# skye mched kyi sgra ni mig la sogs pa rang gi ngo bo phan tshun tha dad pa rnams la yang bye brag med par 'byung bas de'i phyir de dag la des spyi'i don rgyur byas nas 'jug go / / de yang mi shes pas ci'i phyir skye mched ces bya zhes 'dri'o / / rnam par shes ba skye ba'i sgo'i phyir ro zhes bya ba la / / skye ba zhes bya ba ni 'byung ba ste /
vijñānānām utpattir ātmalābhaḥ
# rnam par shes pa rnams 'byung bas bdag nyid thob pa'o /
vijñānāyasya dvāraṃ hetuḥkāraṇaṃ nimittaṃ vijñānāyadvāram
# rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo ni rgyu ste / / byed rgyu dang rgyu mtshan ni rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo'o / / de ni 'di skad du /
etad uktaṃ bhavati vijñānotpattikāraṇārthenāyatanānīti / kathaṃ punar etadvijñāyate
# rnam par shes pa 'byung ba'i rgyu'i phyir skye mched rnams zhes bya'o zhes bstan par 'gyur ro / / 'di ltar ci mngon zhe na nges pa'i tshig gis mngon te /
nirvacanāt cittacaittānām āyaṃ tanvantivistṛṇvantīty āyatanāni
# sems dang sems las byung ba rnams kyi 'byung ba mched par byed cing rgyas par byed pas skye mched rnams te /
ātmalābhaṃ prabandhena sthāpayantīty arthaḥ
# bdag thob par byed pa rgyun du 'jog ces bya ba'i tha tshig go /
tatra cakṣū rūpāṇi ca sasamprayogasyacakṣurvijñānasyāyadvāram
# de la mig dang gzugs rnams ni mig gi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa skye ba'i sgo yin no /
evaṃ yāvan mano dharmāś casasamprayogasya manovijñānasyāyadvāram
# de bzhin du yid dang chos rnams kyi bar dag kyang yid kyi rnam par shes pa mtshungs par ldan pa dang bcas pa'i skye ba'i sgo yin no /
āyatanānantaraṃ dhātavaḥ prabhedataḥ svarūpataś ca vaktavyāity ataḥ prabhedadarśanārtham āha aṣṭādaśa dhātava / iti
# skye mched kyi 'og tu khams rnams rab tu dbye ba dang rang gi ngo bo brjod bar bya ste / / de bas na rab tu dbye ba bstan pa'i phyir / / khams bco brgyad ni zhes bya ba smos so /
teṣām eva svarūpapradarśanārtham āha cakṣurdhātū rūpadhātuś cakṣurvijñānadhātur evaṃ yāvanmanodhātur dharmadhātur / manovijñānadhāturiti
# de dag nyid kyi rang rang gi ngo bo bstan pa'i phyir / / mig gi khams dang gzugs kyi khams dang mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang zhes bya ba nas de bzhin du yid kyi khams dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams dang zhes bya ba'i bar du smos so /
atra hi rūpaskandhavibhāgeyāni cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanasparśanāni pañcendriyāṇy uktāni pañca ca rūpaśabdagandharasasparśāḥteṣāṃviṣayatvena
# 'dir yang gzugs kyi phung po rnam par dbye ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus kyi dbang po gang yin pa lnga po dag dang gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg pa lnga yang de dag gi yul nyid du bstan to /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ tāny eva pañcendriyāṇicakṣurādyāyatanatvenoktāni rūpādayaś ca viṣayārūpādyāyatanatvena
# skye mched rnam par gzhag par yang dbang po lnga po de dag nyid mig la sogs pa'i skye mched nyid dang gzugs la sogs pa'i yul rnams kyang gzugs la sogs pa'i skye mched nyid bstan to /
dhātuvyavasthāyāṃ ta eva cakṣurdhāturyāvat kāyadhātuḥ rūpadhātur yāvat spraṣṭavyadhātur ityuktam ity ata āha tatra cakṣurādidhātavo / rūpādidhātavaś ca yathāyatanānīti
# khams rnam par gzhag pa yang de dag nyid mig gi khams nas lus kyi khams kyi bar dang gzugs kyi khams nas reg bya'i khams kyi bar du bstan te / / de'i phyir mig la sogs pa'i khams dang gzugs la sogs pa'i khams ni skye mched rnams ji lta ba bzhin no zhes bya ba smos so /
dharmadhātus tu yad eva dharmāyatanaṃ vedanādayas trayaḥskandhā avijñaptir asaṃskṛtacatuṣṭayaṃ ca
# chos kyi khams ni chos kyi skye mched tshor ba la sogs pa phung po gsum dang rnam bar rig byed ma yin pa dang 'dus ma byas pa zhi gang yin pa nyid do /
āyatanavyavasthāyāṃ vijñānaskandha eva manaāyatanam
# skye mched rnam par gzhag pa'i rnam par shes pa'i phung po nyid yid kyi skye mched do /
napunar evaṃdhātuvyavasthāyāṃ manaāyatanam evamanodhātuḥ kiṃ tarhi manaāyatanaṃ dhātuvyavasthāyāṃsapta cittadhātavaḥ / ata āha ṣaḍ vijñānadhātava / ityādi
# de bzhin du khams rnam par gzhag par yang yid kyi skye mched nyid kyi khams ma yin te / / yid kyi skye mched kyi khams rnam par gzhag pa na / / sems kye khams bdun no / / de'i phyir /
cakṣurādisanniśritā iticakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇarasanakāyamanaḥsanniśritāḥ
# rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po dag ni zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so / / mig la sogs pa la brten te zhes bya ba ni mig dang rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid la brten te'o /
rūpādyālambanā itirūpaśabdagandharasasparśadharmālambanāḥ / vijñaptaya / iti vijñānāni
# gzugs la sogs pa la dmigs pa zhes bya ba ni gzugs dang sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg bya dang chos rnams ni dmigs pa'o / / rnam par rig pa'o zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pa'o /
tatra cakṣurāśrayaṃ rūpālambanaṃcakṣurvijñānaṃ cakṣurvijñānadhātuḥ
# de la mig la brten cing gzugs la dmigs pa ni mig gi rnam par shes pa ste / / mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
evaṃśrot ragh rāṇarasanasparśanamanaāśrayā ṇ iśabdagandharasasparśadharmālambanāni yathākramaṃśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanovijñānāniśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanovijñānadhātavaḥ
# de bzhin du rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid la brten cing / / sgra dang dri dang ro dang reg dang chos rnams la go rims bzhin du dmigs pa ni rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams te; rna ba dang sna dang lce dang lus dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so /
manodhātuḥpunaḥ ṣaḍ vijñānavyatirikto na vidyate kiṃ tarhi ta evaṣaḍvijñānadhātavo 'nantaraniruddhā manodhātur ityucyate
# yid kyi khams ni rnam par shes pa drug las gud na med de / / rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po de dag nyid 'gag sam thog pa la yid kyi khams zhes bya'o /
r snanv evaṃ saptadaśa dhātavaḥ prāpnuvanti dvādaśa vāmanodhātoḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ cā vijñānadhātūnām itaretarāntarbhāvāt / na prāpnuvanti yasmātṣaṣṭhavijñānāśrayaparidīpanārtham
# de ltar na yid kyi khams dang rnam par shes pa'i khams drug po dag gcig gi nang du gcig 'dus pa'i phyir khams bcu bdun nam bcu gnyis su mi 'gyur ram / / mi 'gyur te 'di ltar rnam par shes pa drug pa'i gnas bstan pa'i phyir /
aṣṭādaśadhātuvyavasthānam
# de ltar khams bco brgyad du rnam par gzhag go /
evam ityanantaroktaprakārapradarśanam
# de ltar zhes bya ba ni gong du smos pa'i rnam pa bstan pa'o /
yo rūpaskandha ity / ekādaśadravyako hi rūpaskandha uktaḥ
# gzugs kyi phung po gang yin pa zhes bya ba la rdzas bcu gcig ni gzugs kyi phung po bstan te /
tatra pañcendriyāṇi cakṣurādīni pañca viṣayā rūpādayaāyatanavyavasthāyāṃdaśāyatanāni dhātuvyavasthāyāṃ daśa dhātavaḥ / dharmāyatanaikadeśo dharmadhātvekadeśaś cāvijñaptyākhyaḥ / yo vijñānaskandhaḥ sa
# de la mig la sogs pa dbang po lnga dang gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga ni skye mched rnam par gzhag par skye mched bcu dang; khams rnam par gzhag par khams bcu dang chos kyi skye mched kyi phyogs gcig dang chos kyi khams kyi phyogs gcig ni rnam par rig byed ma yin pa zhes bya'o /
manaāyatanaṃ cittadhātavaś casapta / cakṣurvijñānadhātur yāvan manovijñānadhāturiti
# rnam par shes pa'i phung po gang yin pa de ni yid kyi skye mched dang sems kyi khams bdun no zhes bya ba ni mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams nas yid kyi khams kyi bar du'o /
ye 'nye / rūpaskandhād vijñānaskandhāc ca trayovedanāsañjñāsaṃskārākhyāḥ skandhārūpaskandhapradeśaś cāvijñaptyākhyaḥ tedharmāyatanaṃ dharmadhātuś ca
# gzugs dang rnam par shes pa'i phung po las gzhan phung po gsum gang yin pa dag tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed ces bya ba'i phung po rnams so / / gzugs kyi phung po'i phyogs gcig ni rnam par rig byed ma yin pa zhes bya ste /
sahāsaṃskṛtenākāśādinā / kenārthena dhātava ity āyatanārthavat vistareṇa / vācyam / nirvyāpārasvalakṣaṇadhāraṇārtheneti / nirvyāpāraṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ dhārayantīti dhātavaḥ
# de dag 'dus ma byas nam mkha' la sogs pa dang bcas pa ni chos kyi skye mched dang chos kyi khams so / / ci'i phyir khams zhes bya zhe na zhes bya ba ni / / skye mched bzhin du rgya cher brjod par bya'o / / byed pa med la rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i phyir khams so /
na hikṣaṇikānāṃ vyāpāraḥ sambhavatīti pūrvam evoktam / ya eva dharmāḥ skandhā iti deśitāḥ ta eva punar āyatanatvenadhātutvena cety ataḥ pṛcchati kimarthaṃ / skandhādideśaneti / sarvā hi deśanā bhagavatāṃbuddhānāṃ saprayojanā sattvārthapravṛttatvātkleśapratipakṣeṇa ca / na cātra prayojanaṃ vijñāyate punaḥpunas teṣām eva dharmāṇām anyenānyena ca prakāreṇadeśanā iti kimarthaṃ skandhādideśaneti prayojanaṃvaktavyam ity ata āha trividhātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti
# skad cig rnams la ni byed pa med par mi srid do zhes sngar bstan pa nyid do / / chos gang dag phung po zhes bstan pa de dag nyid skye mched nyid dang khams nyid du yang bshad pas de'i phyir / / ci'i phyir phung po la sogs pa bshad ce na zhes dris so / / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis bshad pa thams cad ni sems can gyi don du 'gyur ba dang nyon mongs pa'i gnyen po yin pas dgos pa dang bcas pa'o / / 'dir ni chos de dag nyid rnam pa gzhan dang gzhan gyis yang dang yang bshad pa'i dgos pa yang mi shes nas / / ci'i phyir phung po la sogs pa bshad ce na zhes bya ba ni dgos pa brjod do /
tatra navijñāyatekatamas trividha ātmagrāhaḥ katamasya vāpratipakṣeṇa katamā deśanety ata āha yathākramaṃ
# de'i phyir bdag tu 'dzin pa rnam pa gsum gyi gnyen por zhes bya ba smos so / / de la bdag tu 'dzin pa gsum dang gang gi gnyen por bshad pa yang mi shes pas de'i phyir go rims bzhin no zhes bya ba smos te /
trividha ātmagrāha ekatvagrāhobhoktṛtvagrāhaḥ kartṛtvagrāhaś ca / tatra / yathākramam iti skandhadeśanaikatvagrāhapratipakṣeṇaāyatanadeśanā bhokṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇadhātudeśanā kartṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti
# bdag tu 'dzin pa rnam pa gsum ni gcig pur 'dzin pa dang za bar 'dzin pa dang byed par 'dzin pa'o / / de la go rims bzhin zhes bya ba la phung po bshad pa ni gcig pur 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o / / skye mched bshad pa ni za bar 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o /
sarve hy ātmavādinaevaṃ pratipannāḥ ya eva paśyati sa eva śṛṇoti jighraty āsvādayatispṛśati ceti / tatra ya eva vedayate sa eva cetayate sañjānītevijānātīti
# khams bshad pa ni byed par 'dzin pa'i gnyen po'o / / bdag tu smra ba thams cad ni mthong ba gang yin pa de nyid thos pa dang snom pa dang ro myong ba dang reg pa yin pa dang de la de nyid sems par byed ba dang 'du shes su byed pa dang rnam par shes par byed pa'o snyam du de ltar 'dzin to /
na hi sattvātmabhāva evaṃ skandhavyatirikto 'nyaḥkaścid ekavyavasthitarūpo vidyatetatsvarūpakāryānupalabdheḥ
# sems can rnams kyi lus la ni phung po lnga las gud na gcig pur rnam par gnas pa'i ngo bo gang yang med de / / rang gi ngo bo dang 'bras bu mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro /
na cakṣurvyatirekeṇānyo draṣṭā vidyate / cakṣur eva hi darśanākhyasya vijñānasyāsādhāraṇaṃkāraṇam āśrayaś cetidraṣṭṛtvenopacaryate / evaṃ pratyekaṃśrotrādiṣu vaktavyam
# mig las gud na lta ba po gzhan med de / / mig nyid mthong ba'o zhes rnam par shes pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rgyu dang gnas yin pas lta ba po zhes gdags so / / de bzhin du rna ba la sogs pa so so la yang brjod par bya'o /
evaṃ vedanānubhavātmakatvātvedayate
# de bzhin du tshor ba ni myong ba'i bdag nyid yin pas myong bar byed /
sañjñaiva nimittodgrahaṇātmikatvāt sañjānītenānyaity evaṃ sarvatra vācyam
# 'du shes nyid mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i bdag nyid yin pas 'du shes su byed kyi gzhan ni ma yin te / / de ltar thams cad du yang brjod par bya'o /
tasmān nātmabhāvaḥ sattvānāṃ pañcaskandhātmakatvādekavastvātmakaḥ
# de lta bas na sems can rnams kyi lus ni phung po'i bdag nyid yin pas dngos po du ma'i bdag nyid can no /
na caskandhavyatirikto 'tra eko vidyate
# 'di la ni phung po lnga las gud na gcig pu med de /
ekatvagrāhe vyāvartiteskandhadeśanayā yas tatraikatvagrāhapūrvaka ātmagrāhaḥasāv api vyāvartita evety ataekatvagrāhapūrvātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇa skandhadeśanā
# phung po bstan pas gcig pu 'dzin pa ldog pa na de la gcig pur 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag tu 'dzin pa gang yin pa de yang ldog pa nyid de / / de'i phyir gcig pur 'dzin pa sngon du 'gro ba'i bdag tu 'dzin pa'i gnyen por phung po bshad do /
ekatvagrāhas tu kāraṇe kāryopacāraṃ kṛtvātmagrāha ity uktaḥ
# gcig pur 'dzin pa ni rgyu la 'bras bu btags nas bdag tu 'dzin pa zhes bya bar bshad do /
bhoktṛgrāhaḥ punaḥ sarvavādināṃ yaḥ śubhāśubhasyakarmaṇa iṣṭāniṣṭaṃ sukhaduḥkhavedanāprabhāvitaṃ phalamupabhuṅkte rūpaśabdādīṃś ca viṣayān sa ātmeti
# za bar 'dzin pa ni smra ba thams cad ci ltar na las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'bras bu 'dod pa dang mi 'dod pa dang bde ba dang sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas rab tu phye ba dang gzugs dang sgra la sogs pa yul la gang sbyod pa de bdag go zhes so /
syātmagrāhasya pratipakṣeṇāyatanadeśanā
# de ltar na bdag tu 'dzin pa 'di'i gnyen por skye mched bshad do /
śubhāśubhakarmaphalasya rūpādīnāṃ ca viṣayāṇāmupabhuktir upalabdhiḥ
# las dge ba dang mi dge ba'i 'bras bu dang gzugs la sogs pa yul rnams la spyod pa ni dmigs pa ste /
tāṃ yaḥ karotisa karmaphalasyarūpādīnāṃ copabhoktā
# de byed pa gang yin pa de ni las kyi 'bras bu dang gzugs la sogs pa la spyod do /
tāṃ ṣaṭprakārām upalabdhimāyatanāny eva kurvanti nānyaḥ
# dmigs pa rnam pa drug de yang skye mched nyid kyis byed kyi gzhan gyis ni ma yin no /
ata eva cakṣurādayorūpādayaś ca vijñānāyadvārārthenāyatanānīty ucyante
# de'i phyir mig la sogs pa dang gzugs la sogs pa ni rnam par shes pa skye ba'i sgo'i phyir skye mched rnams zhes bya'o /
tasmānnāsti kaścid anyaścakṣurādivyatirekeṇa karmaphalasyaviṣayāṇāṃ copabhoktety evam āyatanadeśanābhoktṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti
# de lta bas na las kyi 'bras bu dang yul rnams la spyod pa ni mig la sogs pa las gud na gzhan gang yang med de / / de ltar na skye mched bshad pa ni za bar 'dzin pa'i gnyen po zhes bya'o /
kartṛtvagrāhaḥ punar yaḥśubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartā valganāsphoṭanādīnāṃ casaātmā
# byed par 'dzin pa ni las dge ba dang mi dge ba rnams 'brel ba dang sprugs bsigs pa la sogs pa byed pa ste /
asyātmagrāhasya pratipakṣeṇa dhātudeśanā
# bdag tu 'dzin pa 'di'i gnyen por khams bshad do /
tathā hinirvyāpārasvalakṣaṇadhāraṇārthena dhātava uktāḥ / evaṃkāraṇaṃ sattāmātreṇa kāryotpattiṃ prati vyāpriyate kāryaṃca sattāmātreṇaiva kāraṇam apekṣate
# de ltar na byed pa med la rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i phyir khams zhes bstan to / / de ltar rgyu yod pa tsam gyis 'bras bu yang 'byung bar byed cing 'bras bu yang rgyu la ltos nas yod pa tsam du zad de /
na cakāryakāraṇasvarūpavyatirekeṇānyā kriyāsti tat pūrvam evapratipāditam / kriyām antareṇa ca kutaḥ kartā
# rgyu dang 'bras bu'i rang gi ngo bo las ma gtogs par byed pa gzhan med par sngar bstan pa nyid do / / byed pa med par byed pa po ga la yod de /
tasmāt kartṛtvagrāhapratipakṣeṇa dhātudeśaneti
# de lta bas na byed par 'dzin pa'i gnyen por khams bshad pa yin no /
idānīṃ dharmapravicayānugrahārthaṃ ya evaskandhāyatanadhātutvena dharmā nirdiṣṭāḥ teṣām evaprakārāś cintyante
# de ni chos gang dag rab tu rnam par dbye bas phan gdags pa'i phyir phung po dang skye mched dang khams nyid du chos gang dag bstan pa de dag la rnam pa gzhan gyis bsam par bya ste /
tatra dhātuṣu rūpacittayor vibhaktatvenavistarāpadeśāt sāsravaprakārādīnāṃ sukhagamyo nirdeśa iti dhātūn evārabhya cintyate na skandhāyatanānity ata evāha aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ kati rūpiṇa ityādi
# de la khams rnams kyi nang du gzugs dang sems gnyis rnam par dbye ba lhag par bstan pas zag pa dang bcas pa'i rnam pa la sogs pa bde blag tu rtogs par 'gyur ba'i phyir khams ga las brtsams te / / bsam par bya ba'i phung po dang skye mched rnams la ni ma yin no / / de'i phyir khams bco brgyad la gzugs can du zhe na zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos so /
rūpaṇaṃ rūpaṃ tad eṣām astīti rūpiṇaḥ
# gzugs su yod pas gzugs te / / 'di dag la yod pas gzugs can no /
āśrayāśritaṃ rūpaṃ vā yathāsambhavam eṣām astīti rūpiṇaḥ
# yang na rten dang brten pa'i gzugs ji ltar mthun mthun du 'di dag la yod pas gzugs can no /
na ca cakṣurādivijñāneṣuprasaṅgaḥ cakṣurādīnām ādhāratvena teṣām anāśrayatvāt
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa la thal bar yang mi 'gyur te / / mig la sogs pa rten gyi dngos po de dag gi gzhi byed pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro /
ye rūpaskandhasvabhāvā iti / te punaḥdaśa dhātavaḥ
# gang dag gzugs kyi phung po'i ngo bo nyid do zhes bya ba de dag ni khams bcu ste /
cakṣurdhātur yāvat kāyadhātuḥ rūpadhātur yāvatspraṣṭavyadhātuḥ
# mig gi khams nas lus kyi bar dang gzugs kyi khams nas reg bya'i khams kyi bar du'o /
avijñaptirūpe saty api na dharmadhātorūpitvaprasaṅgas tasyāśrayāśritarūpābhāvād rūpaṇābhāvādrūpaskandhāsaṅgrahāc ca / katy arūpiṇaḥ / śeṣāḥ / rūpiviparyayeṇa ye
# rnam par rig byed ma yin pa gzugs su yod du zin kyang chos kyi khams gzugs can nyid du thal bar mi 'gyur te / / de la rten dang brten pa'i gzugs med pa dang gzugs su yod pa med pa dang gzugs kyi phung por gtogs su zin kyang gzugs su yod pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro / / gzugs can ma yin pa du zhe na / / lhag ma rnams so zhes bya ba la gzugs can las ldog pa ni gzugs can ma yin pa ste /
te punar / aṣṭau sapta cittadhātavo dharmadhātuś ca / kati sanidarśanā iti / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām iti
# de dag ni brgyad de / / sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams so / / bstan du yod pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas der sbyar ro /
prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate / eko rūpadhāturiti / idamihāmutretiayam ayam? eva vyapadeśo nidarśanam / tena sahavartata iti sanidarśanaḥ sālambanavat
# gzugs kyi khams gcig ste zhes bya ba la 'di ni 'di na'o zhes / / pha bi ni pha bi na'o zhes bstan du rung ba de ni bstan pa'o / / de dang lhan cig pa ni bstan du yod pa ste / / dmigs pa dang bcas pa bzhin no /
idam evanidarśanārthaṃ prabhāvayann āha deśanidarśaneneti / tasmiṃs tasmin deśe nidarśyate 'neneti deśanidarśanam / ekasyaiva rūpadhātoḥ sanidarśanatvena parigrahātśeṣāḥsaptadaśa cakṣurādidhātavaḥ pañca śabdādidhātavaś catvārodharmadhātur ekaḥ sapta cittadhātavaḥ anidarśanā itisiddham / kati sapratighāḥ / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnāṃ prakṛtatvāt / sarvatra sambadhyate
# bstan du yod pa 'di nyid rab tu bstan pa'i phyir / / yul bstan du yod pa'o zhes bya ba smos te / / yul de dang der 'dis bstan du yod pas yul bstan du yod pa'o zhes bya'o / / gzugs kyi khams gcig kho na bstan du yod pa nyid du smos pas lhag ma khams bcu bdun ni bstan du med par grub bo / / thogs pa dang bcas pa du zhen zhes bya ba ni khams bco brgyad kyi skabs yin pas thams cad du yang sbyar ro / / gzugs can ma yin pa rnam par gcad pa'i phyir gzugs can smos so /
dharmadhātāv apyavijñaptirūpasadbhāvād asti rūpivyapadeśa itidaśety āha / arūpivyavacchedārthaṃrūpigrahaṇam
# chos kyi khams la yang rnam par rig byed ma yin pa'i gzugs yod pas / / gzugs can yod par bstan pa'i phyir bcu zhes bya ba smos so /
te punaścakṣurādīndriyadhātavaḥpañca tadviṣayā rūpādidhātavaś capañca / pratighātaḥ pratighaḥ / tena sahavartanta itisapratighāḥ
# de dag kyang mig la sogs pa dbang po'i khams rnams dang de dag gi yul gzugs can gyi khams lnga'o / / go gcod pas thogs pa ste / / de dang lhan cig pa ni thogs pa dang bcas pa'o /
dpratighātas triprakāro viṣayālambanāvaraṇapratighātabhedāt
# go gcod pa ni yul dang dmigs pa dang sgrib pas go gcod pa'i bye brag gis rnam pa gsum mo /
iha tv āvaraṇapratighātenaiva sapratighatvam iṣṭam itipratipādayann āha yatra yaś ca pratihanyata iti
# 'dir ni sgrib pa'i go gcod pa nyid thogs pa dang bcas par 'dod pa bstan pa'i phyir gang la gang thogs pa'o zhes bya ba smos so /
āvaraṇapratighāto hi svadeśe parasyotpattipratibandhaḥ
# sgrib pa'i go gcod pa ni rang gi yul du gzhan 'byung ba'i gegs su gyur pa'o /
evaṃca yenānyasya svadeśa utpattiḥ pratibadhyate yasya ca pratibadhyate tadubhayam api sapratigham iti jñāpitaṃbhavati
# de ltar na gang gis rang gi yul du gzhan 'byung ba'i gegs byed pa dang gang la gegs byed pa de gnyi ga yang thogs pa dang bcas pa zhes bstan pa yin no /
etena ca daśa rūpiṇo dhātavaḥparasparasya svadeśautpattiṃ pratibadhnantīty āvaraṇapratighātena sapratighāḥśeṣāḥ sapta cittadhātavo dharmadhātuś cāpratighāiti / siddham / kati sāsravāḥ / dhātūnām iti prakṛtam / pañcadaśa / trayāṇāṃ ca paścimānāṃ bhāga iti / cakṣurādayaḥ / pañcendriyadhātavo rūpādayaḥpañca viṣayadhātavaḥ pañcacakṣurādivijñānadhātavaś ca ete pañcadaśaekāntena sāsravāeva / ādyāapi trayo vidyante cakṣūrūpacakṣurvijñānadhātavaity ata āha paścimānām iti / paścimās trayomanodhāturdharmadhātur manovijñānadhātuś ca / teṣām api bhāgo 'ṃśaḥsāsravaḥ na tu cakṣurādivat sarva eva sāsravāḥ / teṣāṃ punaryo namārgasatyāsaṃskṛtasvabhāvo bhāgaḥsa eva sāsravaḥ / sāsravaiḥ saha vartanta iti sāsravāḥ / ata evāha teṣukleśotpattita iti / teṣu yasmāt kleśā utpadyante tesāsravāiti
# khams gzugs can bcu po de dag kyang rang rang gi yul du 'byung ba la gcig la gcig gegs byed pas sgrib cing go gcod pa'i phyir thogs pa dang bcas pa rnams so / / lhag ma sems kyi khams bdun dang chos kyi khams ni thogs pa med par grub po zag pa dang bcas pa du zhe na zhes bya ba ni khams kyi skabs yin no / / bco lnga dang tha ma gsum gyi cha ste zhes bya ba ni mig la sogs pa dbang po lnga'i khams dang gzugs la sogs pa yul lnga'i khams dang mig gi rnam par shes pa la sogs pa rnam par shes pa'i khams lnga ste / / khams bco lnga po dag ni gcig tu zag pa dang bcas pa nyid do / / dang po la yang gsum yod de / / mig dang gzugs dang mig gi rnam par shes pa'i khams yin pas de'i phyir tha ma zhes smos so / / tha ma gsum ni yid kyi khams dang chos kyi khams dang yid kyi rnam par shes pa'i khams so / / de dag gi cha ni cha shas te / / zag pa dang bcas pa'o / / mig la sogs pa bzhin du thams cad zag pa dang bcas pa nyid ni ma yin no / / de dag las kyang lam gyi bden pa dang 'dus ma byas kyi rang bzhin gyi cha ma yin pa de nyid zag pa dang bcas pa ste / / zag pa dang lhan cig pas zag pa dang bcas pa'o / / de'i phyir de dag nyon mongs pa skye ba zhes bya ba smos te / / 'di ltar de dag las nyon mongs pa skye bas de'i phyir zag pa dang bcas pa zhes bya'o /
cakṣurādivijñānānām avikalpakatvātkathaṃ rūpādiṣukleśotpattiḥ
# mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams ni / / rnam par mi rtog pa yin pas ji ltar gzugs la sogs pa rnams la nyon mongs pa skyed ce na /
nocyate cakṣurādivijñānair eva saha rūpādiṣukleśā utpadyanta itikiṃ tarhi pratyakṣagocaratāmupādāya rūpādiṣu kleśotpattir ucyate
# nyon mongs pa rnams mig la sogs pa'i rnam par shes pa rnams dang lhan cig tu gzugs la sogs pa la 'byung ba zhes mi bya mod kyi / / 'on kyang mngon sum gyi spyod yul gyi phyir ro zhes bya ba ni gzugs la sogs pas nyon mongs la skyed pa ste /
tathā hi cakṣuś capratītya rūpāṇi ca pratītya cakṣurvijñānam utpadyatecakṣurvijñānānubhūtāni rūpāṇi manovijñānena vikalpyantevikalpāc ca kleśā utpadyante iti / evaṃ śeṣeṣv api vācyam / katy anāsravāḥ / trayāṇāṃ paścimānāṃ / bhāgaḥ / manodharmamanovijñānadhātūnāṃ yomārgasatyāsaṃskṛtasaṅgṛhītaḥ pradeśaḥ so 'nāsrava iti / kati kāmapratisaṃyuktāḥ / aṣṭādaśānāṃ dhātūnām / iti sambadhyate / pañca rūpādayo viṣayāḥ kāmyanta iti kāmāḥ / tatpradhāno dhātuḥ kāmadhātuḥ / tatpratisaṃyuktāḥkāmapratisaṃyuktā ity ucyante
